# <span class="text-4505230f--DisplayH900-bfb998fa--textContentFamily-49a318e1">Built-in Functions</span>

They are listed here in alphabetical order.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dc8d1735993443aa92765c104104b4df"><span data-offset-key="dc8d1735993443aa92765c104104b4df:0">`abs`</span><span data-offset-key="dc8d1735993443aa92765c104104b4df:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="dc8d1735993443aa92765c104104b4df:2">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="dc8d1735993443aa92765c104104b4df:3">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="073fd79b16b74033ba450d2a438e9e53"><span data-offset-key="073fd79b16b74033ba450d2a438e9e53:0">Return the absolute value of a number. The argument may be an integer, a floating point number, or an object implementing </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__abs__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8e3c6fdd2e1e473cbe06f7d84b617d1b"><span data-offset-key="8e3c6fdd2e1e473cbe06f7d84b617d1b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**abs**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="268e75ab478a4b099e1578216ce714a6"><span data-offset-key="268e75ab478a4b099e1578216ce714a6:0">. If the argument is a complex number, its magnitude is returned.</span><span data-offset-key="268e75ab478a4b099e1578216ce714a6:1">`all`</span><span data-offset-key="268e75ab478a4b099e1578216ce714a6:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="268e75ab478a4b099e1578216ce714a6:3">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="268e75ab478a4b099e1578216ce714a6:4">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="957127f907ab4a7788c21b52c70d1904"><span data-offset-key="957127f907ab4a7788c21b52c70d1904:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="957127f907ab4a7788c21b52c70d1904:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="957127f907ab4a7788c21b52c70d1904:2"> if all elements of the </span><span data-offset-key="957127f907ab4a7788c21b52c70d1904:3">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="957127f907ab4a7788c21b52c70d1904:4"> are true (or if the iterable is empty). Equivalent to:</span></span></span>

    def all(iterable):    for element in iterable:        if not element:            return False    return True

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="df862d9eda2b432aa986f5b05975604c"><span data-offset-key="df862d9eda2b432aa986f5b05975604c:0">`any`</span><span data-offset-key="df862d9eda2b432aa986f5b05975604c:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="df862d9eda2b432aa986f5b05975604c:2">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="df862d9eda2b432aa986f5b05975604c:3">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0beaa06b18ec4d14928e925c800b77be"><span data-offset-key="0beaa06b18ec4d14928e925c800b77be:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="0beaa06b18ec4d14928e925c800b77be:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="0beaa06b18ec4d14928e925c800b77be:2"> if any element of the </span><span data-offset-key="0beaa06b18ec4d14928e925c800b77be:3">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="0beaa06b18ec4d14928e925c800b77be:4"> is true. If the iterable is empty, return </span><span data-offset-key="0beaa06b18ec4d14928e925c800b77be:5">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="0beaa06b18ec4d14928e925c800b77be:6">. Equivalent to:</span></span></span>

    def any(iterable):    for element in iterable:        if element:            return True    return False

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="97a0115035014310af602b73dd7e5597"><span data-offset-key="97a0115035014310af602b73dd7e5597:0">`ascii`</span><span data-offset-key="97a0115035014310af602b73dd7e5597:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="97a0115035014310af602b73dd7e5597:2">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="97a0115035014310af602b73dd7e5597:3">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="347e2d5bec3344c5af8e1ab73d7521b8"><span data-offset-key="347e2d5bec3344c5af8e1ab73d7521b8:0">As </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#repr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5bf813cfee4141718d101069b25d70ff"><span data-offset-key="5bf813cfee4141718d101069b25d70ff:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">repr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="865e6a1316f34351b78c1fb8fdcce74a"><span data-offset-key="865e6a1316f34351b78c1fb8fdcce74a:0">, return a string containing a printable representation of an object, but escape the non-ASCII characters in the string returned by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#repr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="53f97c3de8c244b09aba95d4a0ee3c6e"><span data-offset-key="53f97c3de8c244b09aba95d4a0ee3c6e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">repr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a2e2f1855d404559a8afb50707b17f97"><span data-offset-key="a2e2f1855d404559a8afb50707b17f97:0"> using </span><span data-offset-key="a2e2f1855d404559a8afb50707b17f97:1">`\x`</span><span data-offset-key="a2e2f1855d404559a8afb50707b17f97:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="a2e2f1855d404559a8afb50707b17f97:3">`\u`</span><span data-offset-key="a2e2f1855d404559a8afb50707b17f97:4"> or </span><span data-offset-key="a2e2f1855d404559a8afb50707b17f97:5">`\U`</span><span data-offset-key="a2e2f1855d404559a8afb50707b17f97:6"> escapes. This generates a string similar to that returned by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#repr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3773230760ce443d97e26f98e86660e6"><span data-offset-key="3773230760ce443d97e26f98e86660e6:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">repr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2282afd27edf4b22a9208f98a352e568"><span data-offset-key="2282afd27edf4b22a9208f98a352e568:0"> in Python 2.</span><span data-offset-key="2282afd27edf4b22a9208f98a352e568:1">`bin`</span><span data-offset-key="2282afd27edf4b22a9208f98a352e568:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="2282afd27edf4b22a9208f98a352e568:3">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="2282afd27edf4b22a9208f98a352e568:4">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c1ca5c33acf842a5b181c88e4e8a44be"><span data-offset-key="c1ca5c33acf842a5b181c88e4e8a44be:0">Convert an integer number to a binary string prefixed with “0b”. The result is a valid Python expression. If </span><span data-offset-key="c1ca5c33acf842a5b181c88e4e8a44be:1">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="c1ca5c33acf842a5b181c88e4e8a44be:2"> is not a Python </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8b05b635877d42809f900fe399ba62fe"><span data-offset-key="8b05b635877d42809f900fe399ba62fe:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="92a572e4d39c44fbb0be64e02abc7e75"><span data-offset-key="92a572e4d39c44fbb0be64e02abc7e75:0"> object, it has to define an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0443bc9e2f574682aff460f7199556c3"><span data-offset-key="0443bc9e2f574682aff460f7199556c3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**index**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="fe59cc72a4b24445becf1c4733c4394d"><span data-offset-key="fe59cc72a4b24445becf1c4733c4394d:0"> method that returns an integer. Some examples:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> bin(3)'0b11'>>> bin(-10)'-0b1010'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a6b7b4eb0ada4270a1bd37967b8b8c15"><span data-offset-key="a6b7b4eb0ada4270a1bd37967b8b8c15:0">If prefix “0b” is desired or not, you can use either of the following ways.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> format(14, '#b'), format(14, 'b')('0b1110', '1110')>>> f'{14:#b}', f'{14:b}'('0b1110', '1110')

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d4cfe9c2a11943ee9736365805aaf79e"><span data-offset-key="d4cfe9c2a11943ee9736365805aaf79e:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#format" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e2cdcd8033f94aeeba91cef09ec6e39b"><span data-offset-key="e2cdcd8033f94aeeba91cef09ec6e39b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">format()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="62c5207eb58a41e38309f57294765a91"><span data-offset-key="62c5207eb58a41e38309f57294765a91:0"> for more information.</span><span data-offset-key="62c5207eb58a41e38309f57294765a91:1">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="62c5207eb58a41e38309f57294765a91:2"> </span><span data-offset-key="62c5207eb58a41e38309f57294765a91:3">`bool`</span><span data-offset-key="62c5207eb58a41e38309f57294765a91:4">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="62c5207eb58a41e38309f57294765a91:5">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="62c5207eb58a41e38309f57294765a91:6">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8cc332a43b6b47a8b7eaa12fa7af354d"><span data-offset-key="8cc332a43b6b47a8b7eaa12fa7af354d:0">Return a Boolean value, i.e. one of </span><span data-offset-key="8cc332a43b6b47a8b7eaa12fa7af354d:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="8cc332a43b6b47a8b7eaa12fa7af354d:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="8cc332a43b6b47a8b7eaa12fa7af354d:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="8cc332a43b6b47a8b7eaa12fa7af354d:4">. </span><span data-offset-key="8cc332a43b6b47a8b7eaa12fa7af354d:5">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="8cc332a43b6b47a8b7eaa12fa7af354d:6"> is converted using the standard </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#truth" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="260cb05473824466af024ad64c81a4e8"><span data-offset-key="260cb05473824466af024ad64c81a4e8:0">truth testing procedure</span></span></a><span data-key="0872dc101ec54735886126b956d06cbf"><span data-offset-key="0872dc101ec54735886126b956d06cbf:0">. If </span><span data-offset-key="0872dc101ec54735886126b956d06cbf:1">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="0872dc101ec54735886126b956d06cbf:2"> is false or omitted, this returns </span><span data-offset-key="0872dc101ec54735886126b956d06cbf:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="0872dc101ec54735886126b956d06cbf:4">; otherwise it returns </span><span data-offset-key="0872dc101ec54735886126b956d06cbf:5">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="0872dc101ec54735886126b956d06cbf:6">. The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#bool" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="07aaf5f097c049b5a584ecccda622b53"><span data-offset-key="07aaf5f097c049b5a584ecccda622b53:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bool</code></span></span></a><span data-key="db48fe81908e45c1a00f804a629c1cdf"><span data-offset-key="db48fe81908e45c1a00f804a629c1cdf:0"> class is a subclass of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="35fa489c2e3749b295cb1e40be39c2b2"><span data-offset-key="35fa489c2e3749b295cb1e40be39c2b2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="37a6174cfb9d450398ef55708da04bfc"><span data-offset-key="37a6174cfb9d450398ef55708da04bfc:0"> (see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesnumeric" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fef25a7ecad14392b3d4b7ce9e7bf995"><span data-offset-key="fef25a7ecad14392b3d4b7ce9e7bf995:0">Numeric Types — int, float, complex</span></span></a><span data-key="3dffd3b2b2034450a2390bd3e5c71b5d"><span data-offset-key="3dffd3b2b2034450a2390bd3e5c71b5d:0">). It cannot be subclassed further. Its only instances are </span><span data-offset-key="3dffd3b2b2034450a2390bd3e5c71b5d:1">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="3dffd3b2b2034450a2390bd3e5c71b5d:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="3dffd3b2b2034450a2390bd3e5c71b5d:3">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="3dffd3b2b2034450a2390bd3e5c71b5d:4"> (see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bltin-boolean-values" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="21763431092d417b913f1a8837a4df8c"><span data-offset-key="21763431092d417b913f1a8837a4df8c:0">Boolean Values</span></span></a><span data-key="c73981bf3ad646ea82fde91870167ecf"><span data-offset-key="c73981bf3ad646ea82fde91870167ecf:0">).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fd84b1cb5a82483bbb72deab90466147"><span data-offset-key="fd84b1cb5a82483bbb72deab90466147:0">Changed in version 3.7: </span><span data-offset-key="fd84b1cb5a82483bbb72deab90466147:1">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="fd84b1cb5a82483bbb72deab90466147:2"> is now a positional-only parameter.</span><span data-offset-key="fd84b1cb5a82483bbb72deab90466147:3">`breakpoint`</span><span data-offset-key="fd84b1cb5a82483bbb72deab90466147:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="fd84b1cb5a82483bbb72deab90466147:5">_\*args_</span><span data-offset-key="fd84b1cb5a82483bbb72deab90466147:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="fd84b1cb5a82483bbb72deab90466147:7">_\*\*kws_</span><span data-offset-key="fd84b1cb5a82483bbb72deab90466147:8">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="67e2a3527a3741f09c07ddcc45cec616"><span data-offset-key="67e2a3527a3741f09c07ddcc45cec616:0">This function drops you into the debugger at the call site. Specifically, it calls </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.breakpointhook" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3b55b8f9625f4af5b4c912c56f71b3a8"><span data-offset-key="3b55b8f9625f4af5b4c912c56f71b3a8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.breakpointhook()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ca2e7bbac8a041b484bb2c5d4975e086"><span data-offset-key="ca2e7bbac8a041b484bb2c5d4975e086:0">, passing </span><span data-offset-key="ca2e7bbac8a041b484bb2c5d4975e086:1">`args`</span><span data-offset-key="ca2e7bbac8a041b484bb2c5d4975e086:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="ca2e7bbac8a041b484bb2c5d4975e086:3">`kws`</span><span data-offset-key="ca2e7bbac8a041b484bb2c5d4975e086:4"> straight through. By default, </span><span data-offset-key="ca2e7bbac8a041b484bb2c5d4975e086:5">`sys.breakpointhook()`</span><span data-offset-key="ca2e7bbac8a041b484bb2c5d4975e086:6"> calls </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/pdb.html#pdb.set_trace" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c727031a16ec46aa95274b93e1223836"><span data-offset-key="c727031a16ec46aa95274b93e1223836:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">pdb.set_trace()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f80d0f0cb64441848cb0379f5329935b"><span data-offset-key="f80d0f0cb64441848cb0379f5329935b:0"> expecting no arguments. In this case, it is purely a convenience function so you don’t have to explicitly import </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/pdb.html#module-pdb" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f8984cff73764e82aa8b7917cc5bd150"><span data-offset-key="f8984cff73764e82aa8b7917cc5bd150:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">pdb</code></span></span></a><span data-key="fbe5c77102c44bd4ba19aff8410d0bb9"><span data-offset-key="fbe5c77102c44bd4ba19aff8410d0bb9:0"> or type as much code to enter the debugger. However, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.breakpointhook" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e365c5b1173f401cac443012976847f0"><span data-offset-key="e365c5b1173f401cac443012976847f0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.breakpointhook()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1d86a6e0d8964516ad49b8f908f03830"><span data-offset-key="1d86a6e0d8964516ad49b8f908f03830:0"> can be set to some other function and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#breakpoint" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6a68e6336ca64dbcb5e7175c7eba866e"><span data-offset-key="6a68e6336ca64dbcb5e7175c7eba866e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">breakpoint()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6a05f044557d497cacc9909bc5d1167b"><span data-offset-key="6a05f044557d497cacc9909bc5d1167b:0"> will automatically call that, allowing you to drop into the debugger of choice.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="80c8015e561742a0951936f08b258108"><span data-offset-key="80c8015e561742a0951936f08b258108:0">Raises an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#auditing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b626e36089144fd4bd528fc53b37e3f7"><span data-offset-key="b626e36089144fd4bd528fc53b37e3f7:0">auditing event</span></span></a><span data-key="9b4c0f31ff9640f9b025de21c3075344"><span data-offset-key="9b4c0f31ff9640f9b025de21c3075344:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="9b4c0f31ff9640f9b025de21c3075344:1">`builtins.breakpoint`</span><span data-offset-key="9b4c0f31ff9640f9b025de21c3075344:2"> with argument </span><span data-offset-key="9b4c0f31ff9640f9b025de21c3075344:3">`breakpointhook`</span><span data-offset-key="9b4c0f31ff9640f9b025de21c3075344:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5ce361e9e8704850b9b9c8c945067f97"><span data-offset-key="5ce361e9e8704850b9b9c8c945067f97:0">New in version 3.7.</span><span data-offset-key="5ce361e9e8704850b9b9c8c945067f97:1">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="5ce361e9e8704850b9b9c8c945067f97:2"> </span><span data-offset-key="5ce361e9e8704850b9b9c8c945067f97:3">`bytearray`</span><span data-offset-key="5ce361e9e8704850b9b9c8c945067f97:4">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="5ce361e9e8704850b9b9c8c945067f97:5">_source_</span><span data-offset-key="5ce361e9e8704850b9b9c8c945067f97:6">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="5ce361e9e8704850b9b9c8c945067f97:7">_encoding_</span><span data-offset-key="5ce361e9e8704850b9b9c8c945067f97:8">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="5ce361e9e8704850b9b9c8c945067f97:9">_errors_</span><span data-offset-key="5ce361e9e8704850b9b9c8c945067f97:10">\]\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0fffcbe4e2f74cd6806c0c9df3670782"><span data-offset-key="0fffcbe4e2f74cd6806c0c9df3670782:0">Return a new array of bytes. The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="07686715806f458c9cb0adea3ad08da7"><span data-offset-key="07686715806f458c9cb0adea3ad08da7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f172065d122a45ad9e1fff468e4333da"><span data-offset-key="f172065d122a45ad9e1fff468e4333da:0"> class is a mutable sequence of integers in the range 0 &lt;= x &lt; 256. It has most of the usual methods of mutable sequences, described in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq-mutable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fe8a46ce802f4bf1bcc115cec1482691"><span data-offset-key="fe8a46ce802f4bf1bcc115cec1482691:0">Mutable Sequence Types</span></span></a><span data-key="5fc1ca3e4bcd4cd3820ef1e0335e4834"><span data-offset-key="5fc1ca3e4bcd4cd3820ef1e0335e4834:0">, as well as most methods that the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="15dc06d1f8e647cba0ed2653a131e6c0"><span data-offset-key="15dc06d1f8e647cba0ed2653a131e6c0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="107adc5ad8494545ba8df30cfc62e104"><span data-offset-key="107adc5ad8494545ba8df30cfc62e104:0"> type has, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes-methods" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0aa8aede72564d04957c94518cbce5ae"><span data-offset-key="0aa8aede72564d04957c94518cbce5ae:0">Bytes and Bytearray Operations</span></span></a><span data-key="8af7952def764959ae9bf74638b70385"><span data-offset-key="8af7952def764959ae9bf74638b70385:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a9be0c6855154c1aaaa4eda8d7279f8b"><span data-offset-key="a9be0c6855154c1aaaa4eda8d7279f8b:0">The optional </span><span data-offset-key="a9be0c6855154c1aaaa4eda8d7279f8b:1">_source_</span><span data-offset-key="a9be0c6855154c1aaaa4eda8d7279f8b:2"> parameter can be used to initialize the array in a few different ways:</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="18f17cf38f2d47038d0afd5e4543bba6"><span data-offset-key="18f17cf38f2d47038d0afd5e4543bba6:0">If it is a </span><span data-offset-key="18f17cf38f2d47038d0afd5e4543bba6:1">_string_</span><span data-offset-key="18f17cf38f2d47038d0afd5e4543bba6:2">, you must also give the </span><span data-offset-key="18f17cf38f2d47038d0afd5e4543bba6:3">_encoding_</span><span data-offset-key="18f17cf38f2d47038d0afd5e4543bba6:4"> (and optionally, </span><span data-offset-key="18f17cf38f2d47038d0afd5e4543bba6:5">_errors_</span><span data-offset-key="18f17cf38f2d47038d0afd5e4543bba6:6">) parameters; </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="972d084be4fa4165ac1844f26edd45c5"><span data-offset-key="972d084be4fa4165ac1844f26edd45c5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ce061e21ecbd4a4998b07db0c79613b6"><span data-offset-key="ce061e21ecbd4a4998b07db0c79613b6:0"> then converts the string to bytes using </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.encode" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f32919a451ca405f8d8efef128911b58"><span data-offset-key="f32919a451ca405f8d8efef128911b58:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str.encode()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="bf8dd51826cc4a948ef7e1a861e1049a"><span data-offset-key="bf8dd51826cc4a948ef7e1a861e1049a:0">.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="923614db12db4e52870f906c68d4d89b"><span data-offset-key="923614db12db4e52870f906c68d4d89b:0">If it is an </span><span data-offset-key="923614db12db4e52870f906c68d4d89b:1">_integer_</span><span data-offset-key="923614db12db4e52870f906c68d4d89b:2">, the array will have that size and will be initialized with null bytes.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4db877e33ef643ee8c281eff2757172e"><span data-offset-key="4db877e33ef643ee8c281eff2757172e:0">If it is an object conforming to the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/c-api/buffer.html#bufferobjects" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a116fc42545c48c3b1fd34f2543bd5e5"><span data-offset-key="a116fc42545c48c3b1fd34f2543bd5e5:0">buffer interface</span></span></a><span data-key="fb9ba02b9d304c12a7d27b74736cd701"><span data-offset-key="fb9ba02b9d304c12a7d27b74736cd701:0">, a read-only buffer of the object will be used to initialize the bytes array.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="481f7e1ea8d74b3984da9bada4d3ac26"><span data-offset-key="481f7e1ea8d74b3984da9bada4d3ac26:0">If it is an </span><span data-offset-key="481f7e1ea8d74b3984da9bada4d3ac26:1">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="481f7e1ea8d74b3984da9bada4d3ac26:2">, it must be an iterable of integers in the range </span><span data-offset-key="481f7e1ea8d74b3984da9bada4d3ac26:3">`0 <= x < 256`</span><span data-offset-key="481f7e1ea8d74b3984da9bada4d3ac26:4">, which are used as the initial contents of the array.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4d4298878e754666b2dec2d80c8bf4a2"><span data-offset-key="4d4298878e754666b2dec2d80c8bf4a2:0">Without an argument, an array of size 0 is created.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dbe97b5f963b42c195baf311f48b5e8e"><span data-offset-key="dbe97b5f963b42c195baf311f48b5e8e:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#binaryseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="33bc1b3b891b40e696d1f628efd080bd"><span data-offset-key="33bc1b3b891b40e696d1f628efd080bd:0">Binary Sequence Types — bytes, bytearray, memoryview</span></span></a><span data-key="f38fc489a7914dd2ad4ca446ee017e29"><span data-offset-key="f38fc489a7914dd2ad4ca446ee017e29:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typebytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0e1749f05dcd4d5eb256cfb3a45e78b3"><span data-offset-key="0e1749f05dcd4d5eb256cfb3a45e78b3:0">Bytearray Objects</span></span></a><span data-key="64ba0bf1a43a4676a577579a275ca5c4"><span data-offset-key="64ba0bf1a43a4676a577579a275ca5c4:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="64ba0bf1a43a4676a577579a275ca5c4:1">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="64ba0bf1a43a4676a577579a275ca5c4:2"> </span><span data-offset-key="64ba0bf1a43a4676a577579a275ca5c4:3">`bytes`</span><span data-offset-key="64ba0bf1a43a4676a577579a275ca5c4:4">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="64ba0bf1a43a4676a577579a275ca5c4:5">_source_</span><span data-offset-key="64ba0bf1a43a4676a577579a275ca5c4:6">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="64ba0bf1a43a4676a577579a275ca5c4:7">_encoding_</span><span data-offset-key="64ba0bf1a43a4676a577579a275ca5c4:8">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="64ba0bf1a43a4676a577579a275ca5c4:9">_errors_</span><span data-offset-key="64ba0bf1a43a4676a577579a275ca5c4:10">\]\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="07984dad82494f8491e4968a61e9dfb1"><span data-offset-key="07984dad82494f8491e4968a61e9dfb1:0">Return a new “bytes” object, which is an immutable sequence of integers in the range </span><span data-offset-key="07984dad82494f8491e4968a61e9dfb1:1">`0 <= x < 256`</span><span data-offset-key="07984dad82494f8491e4968a61e9dfb1:2">. </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ccd1e64cb3184ccba87df664a025b8a2"><span data-offset-key="ccd1e64cb3184ccba87df664a025b8a2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4d951a435cad4d68a0d8e233f5ccdad7"><span data-offset-key="4d951a435cad4d68a0d8e233f5ccdad7:0"> is an immutable version of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f749836b6ec6433aab3e26820878634e"><span data-offset-key="f749836b6ec6433aab3e26820878634e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0b3fdbfebe994062b523bc1d5b054da1"><span data-offset-key="0b3fdbfebe994062b523bc1d5b054da1:0"> – it has the same non-mutating methods and the same indexing and slicing behavior.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c8c1c9ca23a444fc92b0f0850686dfa7"><span data-offset-key="c8c1c9ca23a444fc92b0f0850686dfa7:0">Accordingly, constructor arguments are interpreted as for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c7d112756f8749c2b9b3f7b9d0a0cb0f"><span data-offset-key="c7d112756f8749c2b9b3f7b9d0a0cb0f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b53586124adc4b86ba8462a46808816c"><span data-offset-key="b53586124adc4b86ba8462a46808816c:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="24bdd118be74485aa053668741ba2a82"><span data-offset-key="24bdd118be74485aa053668741ba2a82:0">Bytes objects can also be created with literals, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/lexical_analysis.html#strings" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a73f0595a62640d787516306cce7113a"><span data-offset-key="a73f0595a62640d787516306cce7113a:0">String and Bytes literals</span></span></a><span data-key="18042427d3254effb405728614d0c6d9"><span data-offset-key="18042427d3254effb405728614d0c6d9:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6f85751c18b94446864c608cb6b5edc3"><span data-offset-key="6f85751c18b94446864c608cb6b5edc3:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#binaryseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f50767414a4a4db88a6e45c2c9f24bde"><span data-offset-key="f50767414a4a4db88a6e45c2c9f24bde:0">Binary Sequence Types — bytes, bytearray, memoryview</span></span></a><span data-key="03da914618d4453a9c37c7a0597a9a59"><span data-offset-key="03da914618d4453a9c37c7a0597a9a59:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typebytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a1a1d22a9f574123aa349b306cc2ba0e"><span data-offset-key="a1a1d22a9f574123aa349b306cc2ba0e:0">Bytes Objects</span></span></a><span data-key="372dde97c907445f8808321ef5c2fffa"><span data-offset-key="372dde97c907445f8808321ef5c2fffa:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes-methods" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="596b57f2e9bf4ac099ed2c246325f7c7"><span data-offset-key="596b57f2e9bf4ac099ed2c246325f7c7:0">Bytes and Bytearray Operations</span></span></a><span data-key="9d891424ae734f9f95f8f71a1517387c"><span data-offset-key="9d891424ae734f9f95f8f71a1517387c:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="9d891424ae734f9f95f8f71a1517387c:1">`callable`</span><span data-offset-key="9d891424ae734f9f95f8f71a1517387c:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="9d891424ae734f9f95f8f71a1517387c:3">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="9d891424ae734f9f95f8f71a1517387c:4">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cf4b95a5032e4bceb4299bdfab611499"><span data-offset-key="cf4b95a5032e4bceb4299bdfab611499:0">Return </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/constants.html#True" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="47651563522a41698f3a6c71d95e728d"><span data-offset-key="47651563522a41698f3a6c71d95e728d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">True</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1f76cb2c7a864fe9a65933824fc23a3d"><span data-offset-key="1f76cb2c7a864fe9a65933824fc23a3d:0"> if the </span><span data-offset-key="1f76cb2c7a864fe9a65933824fc23a3d:1">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="1f76cb2c7a864fe9a65933824fc23a3d:2"> argument appears callable, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/constants.html#False" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2364fd27d1e64cc7968a84a6381f421a"><span data-offset-key="2364fd27d1e64cc7968a84a6381f421a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">False</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a6109ec7cda74ff490e5e78b54d0b47d"><span data-offset-key="a6109ec7cda74ff490e5e78b54d0b47d:0"> if not. If this returns </span><span data-offset-key="a6109ec7cda74ff490e5e78b54d0b47d:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="a6109ec7cda74ff490e5e78b54d0b47d:2">, it is still possible that a call fails, but if it is </span><span data-offset-key="a6109ec7cda74ff490e5e78b54d0b47d:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="a6109ec7cda74ff490e5e78b54d0b47d:4">, calling </span><span data-offset-key="a6109ec7cda74ff490e5e78b54d0b47d:5">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="a6109ec7cda74ff490e5e78b54d0b47d:6"> will never succeed. Note that classes are callable (calling a class returns a new instance); instances are callable if their class has a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__call__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="be1291cca5a647d296f4602833e8bf10"><span data-offset-key="be1291cca5a647d296f4602833e8bf10:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**call**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="38bd54d1b16245c08ac02c4f9a270b47"><span data-offset-key="38bd54d1b16245c08ac02c4f9a270b47:0"> method.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2d7ff6d4468c40d581b98bc72ee44194"><span data-offset-key="2d7ff6d4468c40d581b98bc72ee44194:0">New in version 3.2: This function was first removed in Python 3.0 and then brought back in Python 3.2.</span><span data-offset-key="2d7ff6d4468c40d581b98bc72ee44194:1">`chr`</span><span data-offset-key="2d7ff6d4468c40d581b98bc72ee44194:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="2d7ff6d4468c40d581b98bc72ee44194:3">_i_</span><span data-offset-key="2d7ff6d4468c40d581b98bc72ee44194:4">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="34905cfd99434100adee360354c4a8b7"><span data-offset-key="34905cfd99434100adee360354c4a8b7:0">Return the string representing a character whose Unicode code point is the integer </span><span data-offset-key="34905cfd99434100adee360354c4a8b7:1">_i_</span><span data-offset-key="34905cfd99434100adee360354c4a8b7:2">. For example, </span><span data-offset-key="34905cfd99434100adee360354c4a8b7:3">`chr(97)`</span><span data-offset-key="34905cfd99434100adee360354c4a8b7:4"> returns the string </span><span data-offset-key="34905cfd99434100adee360354c4a8b7:5">`'a'`</span><span data-offset-key="34905cfd99434100adee360354c4a8b7:6">, while </span><span data-offset-key="34905cfd99434100adee360354c4a8b7:7">`chr(8364)`</span><span data-offset-key="34905cfd99434100adee360354c4a8b7:8"> returns the string </span><span data-offset-key="34905cfd99434100adee360354c4a8b7:9">`'€'`</span><span data-offset-key="34905cfd99434100adee360354c4a8b7:10">. This is the inverse of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#ord" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0b6d959430cc4e378db5d5a59fed7a78"><span data-offset-key="0b6d959430cc4e378db5d5a59fed7a78:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ord()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="533f160e268f44f1a692f13b5ec6d1ca"><span data-offset-key="533f160e268f44f1a692f13b5ec6d1ca:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="023d3e28743b4b6f86ed56eed83974fc"><span data-offset-key="023d3e28743b4b6f86ed56eed83974fc:0">The valid range for the argument is from 0 through 1,114,111 (0x10FFFF in base 16). </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ValueError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ab1084660c0b40e0b11ddca6806743da"><span data-offset-key="ab1084660c0b40e0b11ddca6806743da:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ValueError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d500d93f618a40da831f558e877700e9"><span data-offset-key="d500d93f618a40da831f558e877700e9:0"> will be raised if </span><span data-offset-key="d500d93f618a40da831f558e877700e9:1">_i_</span><span data-offset-key="d500d93f618a40da831f558e877700e9:2"> is outside that range.</span><span data-offset-key="d500d93f618a40da831f558e877700e9:3">`@classmethod`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="91b4227cde164e7fb86677169bf918ab"><span data-offset-key="91b4227cde164e7fb86677169bf918ab:0">Transform a method into a class method.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c438fa4fb0184eda94a7c92edac5b44b"><span data-offset-key="c438fa4fb0184eda94a7c92edac5b44b:0">A class method receives the class as implicit first argument, just like an instance method receives the instance. To declare a class method, use this idiom:</span></span></span>

    class C:    @classmethod    def f(cls, arg1, arg2, ...): ...

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f5b5591146094d829d37ff8ee5025681"><span data-offset-key="f5b5591146094d829d37ff8ee5025681:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="f5b5591146094d829d37ff8ee5025681:1">`@classmethod`</span><span data-offset-key="f5b5591146094d829d37ff8ee5025681:2"> form is a function </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-decorator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a2f75966b5d2481f9d7fde5dd16a65ed"><span data-offset-key="a2f75966b5d2481f9d7fde5dd16a65ed:0">decorator</span></span></a><span data-key="ea17673b881a4b3399d9aa8c6f48d969"><span data-offset-key="ea17673b881a4b3399d9aa8c6f48d969:0"> – see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#function" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="495e8617e56b4b89b9b609693c06184d"><span data-offset-key="495e8617e56b4b89b9b609693c06184d:0">Function definitions</span></span></a><span data-key="3392833c42ca49e3837a7b76cb909b83"><span data-offset-key="3392833c42ca49e3837a7b76cb909b83:0"> for details.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a78c7383b1664601b34ee637cce5b11e"><span data-offset-key="a78c7383b1664601b34ee637cce5b11e:0">A class method can be called either on the class (such as </span><span data-offset-key="a78c7383b1664601b34ee637cce5b11e:1">`C.f()`</span><span data-offset-key="a78c7383b1664601b34ee637cce5b11e:2">) or on an instance (such as </span><span data-offset-key="a78c7383b1664601b34ee637cce5b11e:3">`C().f()`</span><span data-offset-key="a78c7383b1664601b34ee637cce5b11e:4">). The instance is ignored except for its class. If a class method is called for a derived class, the derived class object is passed as the implied first argument.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5490cbc8897b495db57d8f64db297af3"><span data-offset-key="5490cbc8897b495db57d8f64db297af3:0">Class methods are different than C++ or Java static methods. If you want those, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#staticmethod" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b72ce20a5ab64244bd87f394d9e25146"><span data-offset-key="b72ce20a5ab64244bd87f394d9e25146:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">staticmethod()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f6aa368a31eb4392a4150eed8df3bd20"><span data-offset-key="f6aa368a31eb4392a4150eed8df3bd20:0"> in this section. For more information on class methods, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#types" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2da8baa06a434e3e9d14cdf202b44b5d"><span data-offset-key="2da8baa06a434e3e9d14cdf202b44b5d:0">The standard type hierarchy</span></span></a><span data-key="a71a44711c2345f2808a6fa3b9dd089a"><span data-offset-key="a71a44711c2345f2808a6fa3b9dd089a:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="81bbc5b632f04d4797e0569a7f01f11b"><span data-offset-key="81bbc5b632f04d4797e0569a7f01f11b:0">Changed in version 3.9: Class methods can now wrap other </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-descriptor" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3cbbc9f7e67b4692be6125ef9c48ac8e"><span data-offset-key="3cbbc9f7e67b4692be6125ef9c48ac8e:0">descriptors</span></span></a><span data-key="9a12f3b18f874558bda16f83a1732e31"><span data-offset-key="9a12f3b18f874558bda16f83a1732e31:0"> such as </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#property" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="060c3f7aff6c47fca636440289c5bc32"><span data-offset-key="060c3f7aff6c47fca636440289c5bc32:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">property()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085"><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:1">`compile`</span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:3">_source_</span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:5">_filename_</span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:7">_mode_</span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:8">, </span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:9">_flags=0_</span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:10">, </span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:11">_dont_inherit=False_</span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:12">, </span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:13">_optimize=-1_</span><span data-offset-key="0683d4fb27ba44169273a309e62d4085:14">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="681c5237542c425fb00b9a6b0b640698"><span data-offset-key="681c5237542c425fb00b9a6b0b640698:0">Compile the </span><span data-offset-key="681c5237542c425fb00b9a6b0b640698:1">_source_</span><span data-offset-key="681c5237542c425fb00b9a6b0b640698:2"> into a code or AST object. Code objects can be executed by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#exec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="37afaae73fc2479199eb4149d3f4a58a"><span data-offset-key="37afaae73fc2479199eb4149d3f4a58a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">exec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7154e0b788714ee2afef87b07722b944"><span data-offset-key="7154e0b788714ee2afef87b07722b944:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#eval" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b1221925353042b697deb0cda63b6f7f"><span data-offset-key="b1221925353042b697deb0cda63b6f7f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">eval()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a3571c27b68046978f1414f9e9f3a5bb"><span data-offset-key="a3571c27b68046978f1414f9e9f3a5bb:0">. </span><span data-offset-key="a3571c27b68046978f1414f9e9f3a5bb:1">_source_</span><span data-offset-key="a3571c27b68046978f1414f9e9f3a5bb:2"> can either be a normal string, a byte string, or an AST object. Refer to the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/ast.html#module-ast" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="45ffe71b9f3a4c78830efdd9bcb5e757"><span data-offset-key="45ffe71b9f3a4c78830efdd9bcb5e757:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ast</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5e6377a548a545b4a734f596fe651fe6"><span data-offset-key="5e6377a548a545b4a734f596fe651fe6:0"> module documentation for information on how to work with AST objects.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7da9f54fa3e94265ac4f003ccb050e8c"><span data-offset-key="7da9f54fa3e94265ac4f003ccb050e8c:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="7da9f54fa3e94265ac4f003ccb050e8c:1">_filename_</span><span data-offset-key="7da9f54fa3e94265ac4f003ccb050e8c:2"> argument should give the file from which the code was read; pass some recognizable value if it wasn’t read from a file (</span><span data-offset-key="7da9f54fa3e94265ac4f003ccb050e8c:3">`'<string>'`</span><span data-offset-key="7da9f54fa3e94265ac4f003ccb050e8c:4"> is commonly used).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266"><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:1">_mode_</span><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:2"> argument specifies what kind of code must be compiled; it can be </span><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:3">`'exec'`</span><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:4"> if </span><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:5">_source_</span><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:6"> consists of a sequence of statements, </span><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:7">`'eval'`</span><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:8"> if it consists of a single expression, or </span><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:9">`'single'`</span><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:10"> if it consists of a single interactive statement (in the latter case, expression statements that evaluate to something other than </span><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:11">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="8686dc7ba98b45f991883c1433540266:12"> will be printed).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="13f923af794b420c8a978ca036c2b26f"><span data-offset-key="13f923af794b420c8a978ca036c2b26f:0">The optional arguments </span><span data-offset-key="13f923af794b420c8a978ca036c2b26f:1">_flags_</span><span data-offset-key="13f923af794b420c8a978ca036c2b26f:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="13f923af794b420c8a978ca036c2b26f:3">_dont_inherit_</span><span data-offset-key="13f923af794b420c8a978ca036c2b26f:4"> control which </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/ast.html#ast-compiler-flags" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d782103d970547658afa2c1ca568afa6"><span data-offset-key="d782103d970547658afa2c1ca568afa6:0">compiler options</span></span></a><span data-key="974b44682bd54800989aaa55043215bc"><span data-offset-key="974b44682bd54800989aaa55043215bc:0"> should be activated and which </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#future" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f7127f8f4ad440b0b1e042ccd112dc64"><span data-offset-key="f7127f8f4ad440b0b1e042ccd112dc64:0">future features</span></span></a><span data-key="499d848ac9b740fba0ff9570d3cf7c22"><span data-offset-key="499d848ac9b740fba0ff9570d3cf7c22:0"> should be allowed. If neither is present (or both are zero) the code is compiled with the same flags that affect the code that is calling </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#compile" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9dee8d00a4d84959b3b37407b81a83ff"><span data-offset-key="9dee8d00a4d84959b3b37407b81a83ff:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">compile()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0271c9bbbca54568bad6bbc74a7a0a7f"><span data-offset-key="0271c9bbbca54568bad6bbc74a7a0a7f:0">. If the </span><span data-offset-key="0271c9bbbca54568bad6bbc74a7a0a7f:1">_flags_</span><span data-offset-key="0271c9bbbca54568bad6bbc74a7a0a7f:2"> argument is given and </span><span data-offset-key="0271c9bbbca54568bad6bbc74a7a0a7f:3">_dont_inherit_</span><span data-offset-key="0271c9bbbca54568bad6bbc74a7a0a7f:4"> is not (or is zero) then the compiler options and the future statements specified by the </span><span data-offset-key="0271c9bbbca54568bad6bbc74a7a0a7f:5">_flags_</span><span data-offset-key="0271c9bbbca54568bad6bbc74a7a0a7f:6"> argument are used in addition to those that would be used anyway. If </span><span data-offset-key="0271c9bbbca54568bad6bbc74a7a0a7f:7">_dont_inherit_</span><span data-offset-key="0271c9bbbca54568bad6bbc74a7a0a7f:8"> is a non-zero integer then the </span><span data-offset-key="0271c9bbbca54568bad6bbc74a7a0a7f:9">_flags_</span><span data-offset-key="0271c9bbbca54568bad6bbc74a7a0a7f:10"> argument is it – the flags (future features and compiler options) in the surrounding code are ignored.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="79b1c44867754c36b2d8a16cb8eaa23b"><span data-offset-key="79b1c44867754c36b2d8a16cb8eaa23b:0">Compiler options and future statements are specified by bits which can be bitwise ORed together to specify multiple options. The bitfield required to specify a given future feature can be found as the </span><span data-offset-key="79b1c44867754c36b2d8a16cb8eaa23b:1">`compiler_flag`</span><span data-offset-key="79b1c44867754c36b2d8a16cb8eaa23b:2"> attribute on the </span><span data-offset-key="79b1c44867754c36b2d8a16cb8eaa23b:3">`_Feature`</span><span data-offset-key="79b1c44867754c36b2d8a16cb8eaa23b:4"> instance in the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/__future__.html#module-__future__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c948674f346e4ad98370413433e5c566"><span data-offset-key="c948674f346e4ad98370413433e5c566:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**future**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c0a119c4971c400080856a29d27f0386"><span data-offset-key="c0a119c4971c400080856a29d27f0386:0"> module. </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/ast.html#ast-compiler-flags" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2bd0158d397542aeb3728c59b8cd17cb"><span data-offset-key="2bd0158d397542aeb3728c59b8cd17cb:0">Compiler flags</span></span></a><span data-key="acc7163f8e3f4e2898269cd4f18d7d8d"><span data-offset-key="acc7163f8e3f4e2898269cd4f18d7d8d:0"> can be found in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/ast.html#module-ast" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e25fce06e4504b9b9052d3eb273888b7"><span data-offset-key="e25fce06e4504b9b9052d3eb273888b7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ast</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2291afd0d3a7407caeaac6f53acd4154"><span data-offset-key="2291afd0d3a7407caeaac6f53acd4154:0"> module, with </span><span data-offset-key="2291afd0d3a7407caeaac6f53acd4154:1">`PyCF_`</span><span data-offset-key="2291afd0d3a7407caeaac6f53acd4154:2"> prefix.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="564da59684a54381b56976ef15e324a0"><span data-offset-key="564da59684a54381b56976ef15e324a0:0">The argument </span><span data-offset-key="564da59684a54381b56976ef15e324a0:1">_optimize_</span><span data-offset-key="564da59684a54381b56976ef15e324a0:2"> specifies the optimization level of the compiler; the default value of </span><span data-offset-key="564da59684a54381b56976ef15e324a0:3">`-1`</span><span data-offset-key="564da59684a54381b56976ef15e324a0:4"> selects the optimization level of the interpreter as given by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/using/cmdline.html#cmdoption-o" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2965a1bb5bd849dcbf4f9d71e92d919b"><span data-offset-key="2965a1bb5bd849dcbf4f9d71e92d919b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">-O</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a354e21f3fc844dc88d0f2177bdc19f3"><span data-offset-key="a354e21f3fc844dc88d0f2177bdc19f3:0"> options. Explicit levels are </span><span data-offset-key="a354e21f3fc844dc88d0f2177bdc19f3:1">`0`</span><span data-offset-key="a354e21f3fc844dc88d0f2177bdc19f3:2"> (no optimization; </span><span data-offset-key="a354e21f3fc844dc88d0f2177bdc19f3:3">`__debug__`</span><span data-offset-key="a354e21f3fc844dc88d0f2177bdc19f3:4"> is true), </span><span data-offset-key="a354e21f3fc844dc88d0f2177bdc19f3:5">`1`</span><span data-offset-key="a354e21f3fc844dc88d0f2177bdc19f3:6"> (asserts are removed, </span><span data-offset-key="a354e21f3fc844dc88d0f2177bdc19f3:7">`__debug__`</span><span data-offset-key="a354e21f3fc844dc88d0f2177bdc19f3:8"> is false) or </span><span data-offset-key="a354e21f3fc844dc88d0f2177bdc19f3:9">`2`</span><span data-offset-key="a354e21f3fc844dc88d0f2177bdc19f3:10"> (docstrings are removed too).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="71baacfa2fdf4ead98780691cb9cf171"><span data-offset-key="71baacfa2fdf4ead98780691cb9cf171:0">This function raises </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#SyntaxError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c148029d19f3495491ef12e2c354d14b"><span data-offset-key="c148029d19f3495491ef12e2c354d14b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">SyntaxError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="87640f99bd844e3888bfcbeb85ac9264"><span data-offset-key="87640f99bd844e3888bfcbeb85ac9264:0"> if the compiled source is invalid, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ValueError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ac0f34d55a8142088524cc6b0f48825a"><span data-offset-key="ac0f34d55a8142088524cc6b0f48825a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ValueError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b7cc9c81822b4ac1a6acc0da7b22b2d5"><span data-offset-key="b7cc9c81822b4ac1a6acc0da7b22b2d5:0"> if the source contains null bytes.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fbaaeeafe9e64fe5b073343aa810f725"><span data-offset-key="fbaaeeafe9e64fe5b073343aa810f725:0">If you want to parse Python code into its AST representation, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/ast.html#ast.parse" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e5a13661b8d844b698541a8303ae3b73"><span data-offset-key="e5a13661b8d844b698541a8303ae3b73:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ast.parse()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f0e815b0c2cd4733a0cbcc91c33ed796"><span data-offset-key="f0e815b0c2cd4733a0cbcc91c33ed796:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="93b96841d0fc4d949525cb78060cbd55"><span data-offset-key="93b96841d0fc4d949525cb78060cbd55:0">Raises an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#auditing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9a501f51e0ed42e981797cc9f226c73f"><span data-offset-key="9a501f51e0ed42e981797cc9f226c73f:0">auditing event</span></span></a><span data-key="524a788df7d3438ead4121197f9d8f7b"><span data-offset-key="524a788df7d3438ead4121197f9d8f7b:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="524a788df7d3438ead4121197f9d8f7b:1">`compile`</span><span data-offset-key="524a788df7d3438ead4121197f9d8f7b:2"> with arguments </span><span data-offset-key="524a788df7d3438ead4121197f9d8f7b:3">`source`</span><span data-offset-key="524a788df7d3438ead4121197f9d8f7b:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="524a788df7d3438ead4121197f9d8f7b:5">`filename`</span><span data-offset-key="524a788df7d3438ead4121197f9d8f7b:6">. This event may also be raised by implicit compilation.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ab9d50b8776a47e59d7bd8db7d5bbab2"><span data-offset-key="ab9d50b8776a47e59d7bd8db7d5bbab2:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6181d81106714bf090f79dcbae9fe371"><span data-offset-key="6181d81106714bf090f79dcbae9fe371:0">When compiling a string with multi-line code in </span><span data-offset-key="6181d81106714bf090f79dcbae9fe371:1">`'single'`</span><span data-offset-key="6181d81106714bf090f79dcbae9fe371:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="6181d81106714bf090f79dcbae9fe371:3">`'eval'`</span><span data-offset-key="6181d81106714bf090f79dcbae9fe371:4"> mode, input must be terminated by at least one newline character. This is to facilitate detection of incomplete and complete statements in the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/code.html#module-code" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d6a3578942c94ab3a8523f107a5ded83"><span data-offset-key="d6a3578942c94ab3a8523f107a5ded83:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">code</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7c73837b83354307b402e3c8f1fa0f49"><span data-offset-key="7c73837b83354307b402e3c8f1fa0f49:0"> module.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="11a38df76189431c959dfbe1f38a5da7"><span data-offset-key="11a38df76189431c959dfbe1f38a5da7:0">Warning</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="65914fd0690243b9b35c2b90c550ad87"><span data-offset-key="65914fd0690243b9b35c2b90c550ad87:0">It is possible to crash the Python interpreter with a sufficiently large/complex string when compiling to an AST object due to stack depth limitations in Python’s AST compiler.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="02eae4ed9eaa4a98bd69f5fb771807ed"><span data-offset-key="02eae4ed9eaa4a98bd69f5fb771807ed:0">Changed in version 3.2: Allowed use of Windows and Mac newlines. Also input in </span><span data-offset-key="02eae4ed9eaa4a98bd69f5fb771807ed:1">`'exec'`</span><span data-offset-key="02eae4ed9eaa4a98bd69f5fb771807ed:2"> mode does not have to end in a newline anymore. Added the </span><span data-offset-key="02eae4ed9eaa4a98bd69f5fb771807ed:3">_optimize_</span><span data-offset-key="02eae4ed9eaa4a98bd69f5fb771807ed:4"> parameter.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4e6f09d9317d410d9faa73543d60984f"><span data-offset-key="4e6f09d9317d410d9faa73543d60984f:0">Changed in version 3.5: Previously, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0defd72b2b5647578a236275a644d219"><span data-offset-key="0defd72b2b5647578a236275a644d219:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">TypeError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="929a5c4e2e4843fc9f6733d4062b6b41"><span data-offset-key="929a5c4e2e4843fc9f6733d4062b6b41:0"> was raised when null bytes were encountered in </span><span data-offset-key="929a5c4e2e4843fc9f6733d4062b6b41:1">_source_</span><span data-offset-key="929a5c4e2e4843fc9f6733d4062b6b41:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c"><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:0">New in version 3.8: </span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:1">`ast.PyCF_ALLOW_TOP_LEVEL_AWAIT`</span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:2"> can now be passed in flags to enable support for top-level </span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:3">`await`</span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:5">`async for`</span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:6">, and </span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:7">`async with`</span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:8">.</span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:9">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:10"> </span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:11">`complex`</span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:12">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:13">_real_</span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:14">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:15">_imag_</span><span data-offset-key="5885a941da3b4a63960c41dae070f70c:16">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="37b032291d9d4212af08c80d8d209efc"><span data-offset-key="37b032291d9d4212af08c80d8d209efc:0">Return a complex number with the value </span><span data-offset-key="37b032291d9d4212af08c80d8d209efc:1">_real_</span><span data-offset-key="37b032291d9d4212af08c80d8d209efc:2"> + </span><span data-offset-key="37b032291d9d4212af08c80d8d209efc:3">_imag_</span><span data-offset-key="37b032291d9d4212af08c80d8d209efc:4">\*1j or convert a string or number to a complex number. If the first parameter is a string, it will be interpreted as a complex number and the function must be called without a second parameter. The second parameter can never be a string. Each argument may be any numeric type (including complex). If </span><span data-offset-key="37b032291d9d4212af08c80d8d209efc:5">_imag_</span><span data-offset-key="37b032291d9d4212af08c80d8d209efc:6"> is omitted, it defaults to zero and the constructor serves as a numeric conversion like </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ca8b909401654408bf81dafc608a0709"><span data-offset-key="ca8b909401654408bf81dafc608a0709:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="cc54d4d9739b4621ad7f9a2d6e177d80"><span data-offset-key="cc54d4d9739b4621ad7f9a2d6e177d80:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#float" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ef1aca104a7b4bb19ca3a58622188a83"><span data-offset-key="ef1aca104a7b4bb19ca3a58622188a83:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">float</code></span></span></a><span data-key="eca85c4e047649ceb913b5d2ca92fb7e"><span data-offset-key="eca85c4e047649ceb913b5d2ca92fb7e:0">. If both arguments are omitted, returns </span><span data-offset-key="eca85c4e047649ceb913b5d2ca92fb7e:1">`0j`</span><span data-offset-key="eca85c4e047649ceb913b5d2ca92fb7e:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="501a67d066734c6dafd1255d9dcf5287"><span data-offset-key="501a67d066734c6dafd1255d9dcf5287:0">For a general Python object </span><span data-offset-key="501a67d066734c6dafd1255d9dcf5287:1">`x`</span><span data-offset-key="501a67d066734c6dafd1255d9dcf5287:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="501a67d066734c6dafd1255d9dcf5287:3">`complex(x)`</span><span data-offset-key="501a67d066734c6dafd1255d9dcf5287:4"> delegates to </span><span data-offset-key="501a67d066734c6dafd1255d9dcf5287:5">`x.__complex__()`</span><span data-offset-key="501a67d066734c6dafd1255d9dcf5287:6">. If </span><span data-offset-key="501a67d066734c6dafd1255d9dcf5287:7">`__complex__()`</span><span data-offset-key="501a67d066734c6dafd1255d9dcf5287:8"> is not defined then it falls back to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__float__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3259fd4329bc42949fdfb99a61f0072b"><span data-offset-key="3259fd4329bc42949fdfb99a61f0072b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**float**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a465692ac7ae4096933be5ccc310e5be"><span data-offset-key="a465692ac7ae4096933be5ccc310e5be:0">. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4b393fa298554ff38f0af70ec020547b"><span data-offset-key="4b393fa298554ff38f0af70ec020547b:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9b414ea54fff41d3b21676e306e520af"><span data-offset-key="9b414ea54fff41d3b21676e306e520af:0">When converting from a string, the string must not contain whitespace around the central </span><span data-offset-key="9b414ea54fff41d3b21676e306e520af:1">`+`</span><span data-offset-key="9b414ea54fff41d3b21676e306e520af:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="9b414ea54fff41d3b21676e306e520af:3">`-`</span><span data-offset-key="9b414ea54fff41d3b21676e306e520af:4"> operator. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dc3a89cbd3eb418f9e68c1eba23ab649"><span data-offset-key="dc3a89cbd3eb418f9e68c1eba23ab649:0">The complex type is described in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesnumeric" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ed51e2a8250b4817b0725e26c17fde38"><span data-offset-key="ed51e2a8250b4817b0725e26c17fde38:0">Numeric Types — int, float, complex</span></span></a><span data-key="545af0fb71ff4db19928095e4c8c4648"><span data-offset-key="545af0fb71ff4db19928095e4c8c4648:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="57283fcbbd8549dc9e9a363793336252"><span data-offset-key="57283fcbbd8549dc9e9a363793336252:0">This is a relative of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#setattr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f4d3c80f57e04abf89cf16d75e997490"><span data-offset-key="f4d3c80f57e04abf89cf16d75e997490:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">setattr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4e042c2c1a4f4fc2af633a06eaaf3b0e"><span data-offset-key="4e042c2c1a4f4fc2af633a06eaaf3b0e:0">. The arguments are an object and a string. The string must be the name of one of the object’s attributes. The function deletes the named attribute, provided the object allows it. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4fa9a3d619b34415b5fc22840cedf392"><span data-offset-key="4fa9a3d619b34415b5fc22840cedf392:0">Create a new dictionary. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4da96ff2ad094b83b10b94ea6a96bda2"><span data-offset-key="4da96ff2ad094b83b10b94ea6a96bda2:0">For other
