<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b8f8dcf7905e4da8bbf8b155b2ad5408"><span data-offset-key="b8f8dcf7905e4da8bbf8b155b2ad5408:0">Without arguments, return the list of names in the current local scope. With an argument, attempt to return a list of valid attributes for that object.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e7302d5779d748b4afbba4614bffd503"><span data-offset-key="e7302d5779d748b4afbba4614bffd503:0">If the object has a method named </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__dir__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7081bf01a1a648f68ea02d880f3f736c"><span data-offset-key="7081bf01a1a648f68ea02d880f3f736c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**dir**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b86234acbed3435c939461fe6f351cfe"><span data-offset-key="b86234acbed3435c939461fe6f351cfe:0">, this method will be called and must return the list of attributes. This allows objects that implement a custom </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getattr__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="85a44e0ff9704a8b94e5db3a3b6fa915"><span data-offset-key="85a44e0ff9704a8b94e5db3a3b6fa915:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**getattr**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2281339578734aadbeaee123ace6c082"><span data-offset-key="2281339578734aadbeaee123ace6c082:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getattribute__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fddbf90c18394e9b90e738ad8e67b34f"><span data-offset-key="fddbf90c18394e9b90e738ad8e67b34f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**getattribute**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9936e621c45241a9a2f3b9964c249bf5"><span data-offset-key="9936e621c45241a9a2f3b9964c249bf5:0"> function to customize the way </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#dir" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="420029f941e643eda97f95217da6fe38"><span data-offset-key="420029f941e643eda97f95217da6fe38:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dir()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4a17f07e971445d7a798494a8c6c3a54"><span data-offset-key="4a17f07e971445d7a798494a8c6c3a54:0"> reports their attributes.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a4a0f7d2926f49e7b1e4c88fea2125ee"><span data-offset-key="a4a0f7d2926f49e7b1e4c88fea2125ee:0">If the object does not provide </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__dir__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a51021408ce44f9f83375f868e57525b"><span data-offset-key="a51021408ce44f9f83375f868e57525b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**dir**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="337733c8520e4eb9b06074b57e2ea2e7"><span data-offset-key="337733c8520e4eb9b06074b57e2ea2e7:0">, the function tries its best to gather information from the object’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#object.__dict__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e0336a6f1f694684b03512be7dd289a3"><span data-offset-key="e0336a6f1f694684b03512be7dd289a3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**dict**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="bffe50179c5a47908f6fa3f1b7225c71"><span data-offset-key="bffe50179c5a47908f6fa3f1b7225c71:0"> attribute, if defined, and from its type object. The resulting list is not necessarily complete, and may be inaccurate when the object has a custom </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getattr__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7d399527903346f0ba5631e7540fc088"><span data-offset-key="7d399527903346f0ba5631e7540fc088:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**getattr**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8a2cac38df43402db37b4a30edbd0a9b"><span data-offset-key="8a2cac38df43402db37b4a30edbd0a9b:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="53abad1fc3684e0cbc9c6c90a1769a11"><span data-offset-key="53abad1fc3684e0cbc9c6c90a1769a11:0">The default </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#dir" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b03f7c901d1b40b299c3cfbbe973beb7"><span data-offset-key="b03f7c901d1b40b299c3cfbbe973beb7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dir()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="eb0fd73eb472491b9f0d34e2feab7aec"><span data-offset-key="eb0fd73eb472491b9f0d34e2feab7aec:0"> mechanism behaves differently with different types of objects, as it attempts to produce the most relevant, rather than complete, information:</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="42657c84c83a4fc8ac9237a8d6decb8d"><span data-offset-key="42657c84c83a4fc8ac9237a8d6decb8d:0">If the object is a module object, the list contains the names of the module’s attributes.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="064d1ade07b14808a361bfd2380cc79a"><span data-offset-key="064d1ade07b14808a361bfd2380cc79a:0">If the object is a type or class object, the list contains the names of its attributes, and recursively of the attributes of its bases.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d98d57bbb3e5445e98d890f03992302c"><span data-offset-key="d98d57bbb3e5445e98d890f03992302c:0">Otherwise, the list contains the object’s attributes’ names, the names of its class’s attributes, and recursively of the attributes of its class’s base classes.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a2011c1d4c494f9dafd3cb688e085ca4"><span data-offset-key="a2011c1d4c494f9dafd3cb688e085ca4:0">The resulting list is sorted alphabetically. For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> import struct>>> dir()   # show the names in the module namespace  ['__builtins__', '__name__', 'struct']>>> dir(struct)   # show the names in the struct module ['Struct', '__all__', '__builtins__', '__cached__', '__doc__', '__file__', '__initializing__', '__loader__', '__name__', '__package__', '_clearcache', 'calcsize', 'error', 'pack', 'pack_into', 'unpack', 'unpack_from']>>> class Shape:...     def __dir__(self):...         return ['area', 'perimeter', 'location']>>> s = Shape()>>> dir(s)['area', 'location', 'perimeter']

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f239d8a9309e4431beabf3af9edf850d"><span data-offset-key="f239d8a9309e4431beabf3af9edf850d:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2ff866e2962246c2a32bcc9c1ba40da2"><span data-offset-key="2ff866e2962246c2a32bcc9c1ba40da2:0">Because </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#dir" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8008da7d5d17422385e0a9124c5942e2"><span data-offset-key="8008da7d5d17422385e0a9124c5942e2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dir()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e31ee16476764c22800320294a9dffde"><span data-offset-key="e31ee16476764c22800320294a9dffde:0"> is supplied primarily as a convenience for use at an interactive prompt, it tries to supply an interesting set of names more than it tries to supply a rigorously or consistently defined set of names, and its detailed behavior may change across releases. For example, metaclass attributes are not in the result list when the argument is a class.</span><span data-offset-key="e31ee16476764c22800320294a9dffde:1">`divmod`</span><span data-offset-key="e31ee16476764c22800320294a9dffde:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="e31ee16476764c22800320294a9dffde:3">_a_</span><span data-offset-key="e31ee16476764c22800320294a9dffde:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="e31ee16476764c22800320294a9dffde:5">_b_</span><span data-offset-key="e31ee16476764c22800320294a9dffde:6">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120"><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:0">Take two (non complex) numbers as arguments and return a pair of numbers consisting of their quotient and remainder when using integer division. With mixed operand types, the rules for binary arithmetic operators apply. For integers, the result is the same as </span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:1">`(a // b, a % b)`</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:2">. For floating point numbers the result is </span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:3">`(q, a % b)`</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:4">, where </span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:5">_q_</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:6"> is usually </span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:7">`math.floor(a / b)`</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:8"> but may be 1 less than that. In any case </span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:9">`q * b + a % b`</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:10"> is very close to </span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:11">_a_</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:12">, if </span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:13">`a % b`</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:14"> is non-zero it has the same sign as </span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:15">_b_</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:16">, and </span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:17">`0 <= abs(a % b) < abs(b)`</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:18">.</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:19">`enumerate`</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:20">(</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:21">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:22">, </span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:23">_start=0_</span><span data-offset-key="5f921f25e174463e83f7c1a110d09120:24">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0228663746d34fd48467f45e70fce597"><span data-offset-key="0228663746d34fd48467f45e70fce597:0">Return an enumerate object. </span><span data-offset-key="0228663746d34fd48467f45e70fce597:1">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="0228663746d34fd48467f45e70fce597:2"> must be a sequence, an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-iterator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="85e6b2f2aed243638f7779c8bffed9d9"><span data-offset-key="85e6b2f2aed243638f7779c8bffed9d9:0">iterator</span></span></a><span data-key="ec0bd24c93a044298a3ca1ec965b2b36"><span data-offset-key="ec0bd24c93a044298a3ca1ec965b2b36:0">, or some other object which supports iteration. The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#iterator.__next__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2b650bccfcac418cab2540203751024b"><span data-offset-key="2b650bccfcac418cab2540203751024b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**next**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="143f9ebc5c294dff95df360c138226a5"><span data-offset-key="143f9ebc5c294dff95df360c138226a5:0"> method of the iterator returned by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#enumerate" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b1557a19b3274b979edc9fc808207fe1"><span data-offset-key="b1557a19b3274b979edc9fc808207fe1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">enumerate()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4744d228dcc84603b1b0af79d5f31431"><span data-offset-key="4744d228dcc84603b1b0af79d5f31431:0"> returns a tuple containing a count (from </span><span data-offset-key="4744d228dcc84603b1b0af79d5f31431:1">_start_</span><span data-offset-key="4744d228dcc84603b1b0af79d5f31431:2"> which defaults to 0) and the values obtained from iterating over </span><span data-offset-key="4744d228dcc84603b1b0af79d5f31431:3">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="4744d228dcc84603b1b0af79d5f31431:4">.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> seasons = ['Spring', 'Summer', 'Fall', 'Winter']>>> list(enumerate(seasons))[(0, 'Spring'), (1, 'Summer'), (2, 'Fall'), (3, 'Winter')]>>> list(enumerate(seasons, start=1))[(1, 'Spring'), (2, 'Summer'), (3, 'Fall'), (4, 'Winter')]

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7816e8792fdb4afa9d846813a3c2c189"><span data-offset-key="7816e8792fdb4afa9d846813a3c2c189:0">Equivalent to:</span></span></span>

    def enumerate(sequence, start=0):    n = start    for elem in sequence:        yield n, elem        n += 1

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="91d8d12300514b819bfe3a90cb84f84c"><span data-offset-key="91d8d12300514b819bfe3a90cb84f84c:0">`eval`</span><span data-offset-key="91d8d12300514b819bfe3a90cb84f84c:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="91d8d12300514b819bfe3a90cb84f84c:2">_expression_</span><span data-offset-key="91d8d12300514b819bfe3a90cb84f84c:3">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="91d8d12300514b819bfe3a90cb84f84c:4">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="91d8d12300514b819bfe3a90cb84f84c:5">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="91d8d12300514b819bfe3a90cb84f84c:6">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="91d8d12300514b819bfe3a90cb84f84c:7">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="82f24ad960ba4236820202c909f0d5ec"><span data-offset-key="82f24ad960ba4236820202c909f0d5ec:0">The arguments are a string and optional globals and locals. If provided, </span><span data-offset-key="82f24ad960ba4236820202c909f0d5ec:1">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="82f24ad960ba4236820202c909f0d5ec:2"> must be a dictionary. If provided, </span><span data-offset-key="82f24ad960ba4236820202c909f0d5ec:3">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="82f24ad960ba4236820202c909f0d5ec:4"> can be any mapping object.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4a4c973ba4484f899d73a3765926b1e4"><span data-offset-key="4a4c973ba4484f899d73a3765926b1e4:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="4a4c973ba4484f899d73a3765926b1e4:1">_expression_</span><span data-offset-key="4a4c973ba4484f899d73a3765926b1e4:2"> argument is parsed and evaluated as a Python expression (technically speaking, a condition list) using the </span><span data-offset-key="4a4c973ba4484f899d73a3765926b1e4:3">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="4a4c973ba4484f899d73a3765926b1e4:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="4a4c973ba4484f899d73a3765926b1e4:5">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="4a4c973ba4484f899d73a3765926b1e4:6"> dictionaries as global and local namespace. If the </span><span data-offset-key="4a4c973ba4484f899d73a3765926b1e4:7">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="4a4c973ba4484f899d73a3765926b1e4:8"> dictionary is present and does not contain a value for the key </span><span data-offset-key="4a4c973ba4484f899d73a3765926b1e4:9">`__builtins__`</span><span data-offset-key="4a4c973ba4484f899d73a3765926b1e4:10">, a reference to the dictionary of the built-in module </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/builtins.html#module-builtins" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="73d8e58081954e2db8174a40c80fefad"><span data-offset-key="73d8e58081954e2db8174a40c80fefad:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">builtins</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7c338fe6bcbf48eb9089733d57e28116"><span data-offset-key="7c338fe6bcbf48eb9089733d57e28116:0"> is inserted under that key before </span><span data-offset-key="7c338fe6bcbf48eb9089733d57e28116:1">_expression_</span><span data-offset-key="7c338fe6bcbf48eb9089733d57e28116:2"> is parsed. This means that </span><span data-offset-key="7c338fe6bcbf48eb9089733d57e28116:3">_expression_</span><span data-offset-key="7c338fe6bcbf48eb9089733d57e28116:4"> normally has full access to the standard </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/builtins.html#module-builtins" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7ab2e803a7524cfa8c0068c94b4da703"><span data-offset-key="7ab2e803a7524cfa8c0068c94b4da703:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">builtins</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8496801677ef448f83a5699a68e84cf2"><span data-offset-key="8496801677ef448f83a5699a68e84cf2:0"> module and restricted environments are propagated. If the </span><span data-offset-key="8496801677ef448f83a5699a68e84cf2:1">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="8496801677ef448f83a5699a68e84cf2:2"> dictionary is omitted it defaults to the </span><span data-offset-key="8496801677ef448f83a5699a68e84cf2:3">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="8496801677ef448f83a5699a68e84cf2:4"> dictionary. If both dictionaries are omitted, the expression is executed with the </span><span data-offset-key="8496801677ef448f83a5699a68e84cf2:5">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="8496801677ef448f83a5699a68e84cf2:6"> and </span><span data-offset-key="8496801677ef448f83a5699a68e84cf2:7">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="8496801677ef448f83a5699a68e84cf2:8"> in the environment where </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#eval" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6e53c58eb79544dc887bae3fafd4458c"><span data-offset-key="6e53c58eb79544dc887bae3fafd4458c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">eval()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b98269f7bf9c4b2e9955104fb97576d9"><span data-offset-key="b98269f7bf9c4b2e9955104fb97576d9:0"> is called. Note, </span><span data-offset-key="b98269f7bf9c4b2e9955104fb97576d9:1">_eval()_</span><span data-offset-key="b98269f7bf9c4b2e9955104fb97576d9:2"> does not have access to the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-nested-scope" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="00792b3a00ae4848bd53855f3d670a9a"><span data-offset-key="00792b3a00ae4848bd53855f3d670a9a:0">nested scopes</span></span></a><span data-key="47a4b0bed83e401fac728b4e0e3becfe"><span data-offset-key="47a4b0bed83e401fac728b4e0e3becfe:0"> (non-locals) in the enclosing environment.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="23018334f0df4a57b6371ee6520b4d3f"><span data-offset-key="23018334f0df4a57b6371ee6520b4d3f:0">The return value is the result of the evaluated expression. Syntax errors are reported as exceptions. Example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> x = 1>>> eval('x+1')2

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="93205f0983d14d8fb91845d97f1fe500"><span data-offset-key="93205f0983d14d8fb91845d97f1fe500:0">This function can also be used to execute arbitrary code objects (such as those created by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#compile" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="73d654e6fb1c4ea1aa6e92de3f65bfd2"><span data-offset-key="73d654e6fb1c4ea1aa6e92de3f65bfd2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">compile()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="79aa11a007cd4e55ada51f7bd51b678a"><span data-offset-key="79aa11a007cd4e55ada51f7bd51b678a:0">). In this case pass a code object instead of a string. If the code object has been compiled with </span><span data-offset-key="79aa11a007cd4e55ada51f7bd51b678a:1">`'exec'`</span><span data-offset-key="79aa11a007cd4e55ada51f7bd51b678a:2"> as the </span><span data-offset-key="79aa11a007cd4e55ada51f7bd51b678a:3">_mode_</span><span data-offset-key="79aa11a007cd4e55ada51f7bd51b678a:4"> argument, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#eval" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="54cf81e070314476be8978ce8780cb3b"><span data-offset-key="54cf81e070314476be8978ce8780cb3b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">eval()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b3a5bf9be9d242578ec55be11b0ee135"><span data-offset-key="b3a5bf9be9d242578ec55be11b0ee135:0">’s return value will be </span><span data-offset-key="b3a5bf9be9d242578ec55be11b0ee135:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="b3a5bf9be9d242578ec55be11b0ee135:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="97612426a03f43ffa1b8ee6d64411ede"><span data-offset-key="97612426a03f43ffa1b8ee6d64411ede:0">Hints: dynamic execution of statements is supported by the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#exec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dab2a12925cb47e9a9db7370ada5adda"><span data-offset-key="dab2a12925cb47e9a9db7370ada5adda:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">exec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6a6c05f4cef44786a60dcf15c4dcce3b"><span data-offset-key="6a6c05f4cef44786a60dcf15c4dcce3b:0"> function. The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#globals" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7e1d88f7823c440d8657b884b8bd3231"><span data-offset-key="7e1d88f7823c440d8657b884b8bd3231:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">globals()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="da7470fb46a64127b312ccac9746ee22"><span data-offset-key="da7470fb46a64127b312ccac9746ee22:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#locals" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2e13a918e9a64207a2c5b4954fd51d1c"><span data-offset-key="2e13a918e9a64207a2c5b4954fd51d1c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">locals()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8077d3a7c65c48d7ba061891a61516d5"><span data-offset-key="8077d3a7c65c48d7ba061891a61516d5:0"> functions returns the current global and local dictionary, respectively, which may be useful to pass around for use by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#eval" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="eebe4cc090394f02bcba6d01481568ec"><span data-offset-key="eebe4cc090394f02bcba6d01481568ec:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">eval()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2c9448cb8ece441586425f25d3620041"><span data-offset-key="2c9448cb8ece441586425f25d3620041:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#exec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d226c0ade9d244209f2246f584bdabb2"><span data-offset-key="d226c0ade9d244209f2246f584bdabb2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">exec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="91c9e8c8db684001a9b457742206ac46"><span data-offset-key="91c9e8c8db684001a9b457742206ac46:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d45a05f9f8204c5d86ad6c1d07acade5"><span data-offset-key="d45a05f9f8204c5d86ad6c1d07acade5:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/ast.html#ast.literal_eval" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="88b9883278f8430fbcf238212d1ac9e9"><span data-offset-key="88b9883278f8430fbcf238212d1ac9e9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ast.literal_eval()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e0dcf4f66fe74eab8c3a5e5470953a65"><span data-offset-key="e0dcf4f66fe74eab8c3a5e5470953a65:0"> for a function that can safely evaluate strings with expressions containing only literals.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="57ade929ea8a45ee9d4ed875a9ac0a01"><span data-offset-key="57ade929ea8a45ee9d4ed875a9ac0a01:0">Raises an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#auditing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a515d92298394b5f857f9bb4c9ed675d"><span data-offset-key="a515d92298394b5f857f9bb4c9ed675d:0">auditing event</span></span></a><span data-key="2c82362416144ceba2d4736608cc856a"><span data-offset-key="2c82362416144ceba2d4736608cc856a:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="2c82362416144ceba2d4736608cc856a:1">`exec`</span><span data-offset-key="2c82362416144ceba2d4736608cc856a:2"> with the code object as the argument. Code compilation events may also be raised.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e73d72f9f5524ee0989364873ae0c0ef"><span data-offset-key="e73d72f9f5524ee0989364873ae0c0ef:0">`exec`</span><span data-offset-key="e73d72f9f5524ee0989364873ae0c0ef:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="e73d72f9f5524ee0989364873ae0c0ef:2">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="e73d72f9f5524ee0989364873ae0c0ef:3">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="e73d72f9f5524ee0989364873ae0c0ef:4">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="e73d72f9f5524ee0989364873ae0c0ef:5">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="e73d72f9f5524ee0989364873ae0c0ef:6">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="e73d72f9f5524ee0989364873ae0c0ef:7">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="895e69fdc46a4d86849129c6f144421a"><span data-offset-key="895e69fdc46a4d86849129c6f144421a:0">This function supports dynamic execution of Python code. </span><span data-offset-key="895e69fdc46a4d86849129c6f144421a:1">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="895e69fdc46a4d86849129c6f144421a:2"> must be either a string or a code object. If it is a string, the string is parsed as a suite of Python statements which is then executed (unless a syntax error occurs). </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#id2" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4cefe15b359747f58c4d7c619f773b73"><span data-offset-key="4cefe15b359747f58c4d7c619f773b73:0">1</span></span></a><span data-key="fb8d33de545e478c98f6596b810465e0"><span data-offset-key="fb8d33de545e478c98f6596b810465e0:0"> If it is a code object, it is simply executed. In all cases, the code that’s executed is expected to be valid as file input (see the section “File input” in the Reference Manual). Be aware that the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#nonlocal" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="999b3c84169b409c979a8c97bdc0ebd4"><span data-offset-key="999b3c84169b409c979a8c97bdc0ebd4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">nonlocal</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6ceefc0fa11f4a06804600cba51a8ab6"><span data-offset-key="6ceefc0fa11f4a06804600cba51a8ab6:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#yield" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6659a0ea619f4f9bbeb735973bc3d557"><span data-offset-key="6659a0ea619f4f9bbeb735973bc3d557:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">yield</code></span></span></a><span data-key="318f2a883a0d4c349e48c25417df5af3"><span data-offset-key="318f2a883a0d4c349e48c25417df5af3:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#return" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e5bc6aa0a08e481e9d4a2352387b69cc"><span data-offset-key="e5bc6aa0a08e481e9d4a2352387b69cc:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">return</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a2d2ef7f3f2447c893bcc34ce61ee695"><span data-offset-key="a2d2ef7f3f2447c893bcc34ce61ee695:0"> statements may not be used outside of function definitions even within the context of code passed to the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#exec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8862fc2d36414ad199a550af6f19647e"><span data-offset-key="8862fc2d36414ad199a550af6f19647e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">exec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="40f5476b6b684ca1af9e72b11c219482"><span data-offset-key="40f5476b6b684ca1af9e72b11c219482:0"> function. The return value is </span><span data-offset-key="40f5476b6b684ca1af9e72b11c219482:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="40f5476b6b684ca1af9e72b11c219482:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea"><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:0">In all cases, if the optional parts are omitted, the code is executed in the current scope. If only </span><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:1">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:2"> is provided, it must be a dictionary (and not a subclass of dictionary), which will be used for both the global and the local variables. If </span><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:3">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:5">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:6"> are given, they are used for the global and local variables, respectively. If provided, </span><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:7">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:8"> can be any mapping object. Remember that at module level, globals and locals are the same dictionary. If exec gets two separate objects as </span><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:9">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:10"> and </span><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:11">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="0e7f4856384b41cca7c462403cb313ea:12">, the code will be executed as if it were embedded in a class definition.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="974411bd1c3e44f8b10577b2034c3eb3"><span data-offset-key="974411bd1c3e44f8b10577b2034c3eb3:0">If the </span><span data-offset-key="974411bd1c3e44f8b10577b2034c3eb3:1">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="974411bd1c3e44f8b10577b2034c3eb3:2"> dictionary does not contain a value for the key </span><span data-offset-key="974411bd1c3e44f8b10577b2034c3eb3:3">`__builtins__`</span><span data-offset-key="974411bd1c3e44f8b10577b2034c3eb3:4">, a reference to the dictionary of the built-in module </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/builtins.html#module-builtins" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d5ed8b334e744ac5b8d03db6a4047b36"><span data-offset-key="d5ed8b334e744ac5b8d03db6a4047b36:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">builtins</code></span></span></a><span data-key="386ec989aa0d4a538f41b571dbdb7803"><span data-offset-key="386ec989aa0d4a538f41b571dbdb7803:0"> is inserted under that key. That way you can control what builtins are available to the executed code by inserting your own </span><span data-offset-key="386ec989aa0d4a538f41b571dbdb7803:1">`__builtins__`</span><span data-offset-key="386ec989aa0d4a538f41b571dbdb7803:2"> dictionary into </span><span data-offset-key="386ec989aa0d4a538f41b571dbdb7803:3">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="386ec989aa0d4a538f41b571dbdb7803:4"> before passing it to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#exec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="747af49c5b094fe0bfd09b36d377fb7f"><span data-offset-key="747af49c5b094fe0bfd09b36d377fb7f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">exec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="909824d138fc41f794b11b4710f9d5c6"><span data-offset-key="909824d138fc41f794b11b4710f9d5c6:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d570dc5b45634aacbbacda61d9960bcf"><span data-offset-key="d570dc5b45634aacbbacda61d9960bcf:0">Raises an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#auditing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3dcdc06836b24982b8f0a4aa551a92c3"><span data-offset-key="3dcdc06836b24982b8f0a4aa551a92c3:0">auditing event</span></span></a><span data-key="91fb07c1544d463ba8786d680e71a38b"><span data-offset-key="91fb07c1544d463ba8786d680e71a38b:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="91fb07c1544d463ba8786d680e71a38b:1">`exec`</span><span data-offset-key="91fb07c1544d463ba8786d680e71a38b:2"> with the code object as the argument. Code compilation events may also be raised.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e5a41d54a5ea4e18957164bb2f289903"><span data-offset-key="e5a41d54a5ea4e18957164bb2f289903:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6a2359c7be214b0cb7fe766cb9c05c5e"><span data-offset-key="6a2359c7be214b0cb7fe766cb9c05c5e:0">The built-in functions </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#globals" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bb18814da823483cb852fc81e06bad5e"><span data-offset-key="bb18814da823483cb852fc81e06bad5e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">globals()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="616afa9f87034c0393d28222df89f605"><span data-offset-key="616afa9f87034c0393d28222df89f605:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#locals" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="70de182301ec41599016fd591b78b452"><span data-offset-key="70de182301ec41599016fd591b78b452:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">locals()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="127cb416476e46dab900eb84ee347860"><span data-offset-key="127cb416476e46dab900eb84ee347860:0"> return the current global and local dictionary, respectively, which may be useful to pass around for use as the second and third argument to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#exec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1bf4e8dc0f55485ca254cd7e7d14cd08"><span data-offset-key="1bf4e8dc0f55485ca254cd7e7d14cd08:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">exec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="06daf4e4c64f4bfdac773c3ae1beede1"><span data-offset-key="06daf4e4c64f4bfdac773c3ae1beede1:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ab9b2dd7f87c4e8aa3090054e61be36d"><span data-offset-key="ab9b2dd7f87c4e8aa3090054e61be36d:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7004362541864de09191275b81b85cac"><span data-offset-key="7004362541864de09191275b81b85cac:0">The default </span><span data-offset-key="7004362541864de09191275b81b85cac:1">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="7004362541864de09191275b81b85cac:2"> act as described for function </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#locals" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="175d912abf3f4b85aaf2fe07b4a21ac2"><span data-offset-key="175d912abf3f4b85aaf2fe07b4a21ac2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">locals()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="35416e9b0d80423bbb9cdc524b194d03"><span data-offset-key="35416e9b0d80423bbb9cdc524b194d03:0"> below: modifications to the default </span><span data-offset-key="35416e9b0d80423bbb9cdc524b194d03:1">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="35416e9b0d80423bbb9cdc524b194d03:2"> dictionary should not be attempted. Pass an explicit </span><span data-offset-key="35416e9b0d80423bbb9cdc524b194d03:3">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="35416e9b0d80423bbb9cdc524b194d03:4"> dictionary if you need to see effects of the code on </span><span data-offset-key="35416e9b0d80423bbb9cdc524b194d03:5">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="35416e9b0d80423bbb9cdc524b194d03:6"> after function </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#exec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9e2f821f5198472ba389f056e3821844"><span data-offset-key="9e2f821f5198472ba389f056e3821844:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">exec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="42e60d2f8a19423d9fdf3e4bd3bfaf1d"><span data-offset-key="42e60d2f8a19423d9fdf3e4bd3bfaf1d:0"> returns.</span><span data-offset-key="42e60d2f8a19423d9fdf3e4bd3bfaf1d:1">`filter`</span><span data-offset-key="42e60d2f8a19423d9fdf3e4bd3bfaf1d:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="42e60d2f8a19423d9fdf3e4bd3bfaf1d:3">_function_</span><span data-offset-key="42e60d2f8a19423d9fdf3e4bd3bfaf1d:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="42e60d2f8a19423d9fdf3e4bd3bfaf1d:5">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="42e60d2f8a19423d9fdf3e4bd3bfaf1d:6">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa"><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:0">Construct an iterator from those elements of </span><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:1">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:2"> for which </span><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:3">_function_</span><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:4"> returns true. </span><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:5">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:6"> may be either a sequence, a container which supports iteration, or an iterator. If </span><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:7">_function_</span><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:8"> is </span><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:9">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:10">, the identity function is assumed, that is, all elements of </span><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:11">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="dcc53d138cfe41fbb9e459859d6980fa:12"> that are false are removed.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6b428538f6e54713818fb3a04894971e"><span data-offset-key="6b428538f6e54713818fb3a04894971e:0">Note that </span><span data-offset-key="6b428538f6e54713818fb3a04894971e:1">`filter(function, iterable)`</span><span data-offset-key="6b428538f6e54713818fb3a04894971e:2"> is equivalent to the generator expression </span><span data-offset-key="6b428538f6e54713818fb3a04894971e:3">`(item for item in iterable if function(item))`</span><span data-offset-key="6b428538f6e54713818fb3a04894971e:4"> if function is not </span><span data-offset-key="6b428538f6e54713818fb3a04894971e:5">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="6b428538f6e54713818fb3a04894971e:6"> and </span><span data-offset-key="6b428538f6e54713818fb3a04894971e:7">`(item for item in iterable if item)`</span><span data-offset-key="6b428538f6e54713818fb3a04894971e:8"> if function is </span><span data-offset-key="6b428538f6e54713818fb3a04894971e:9">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="6b428538f6e54713818fb3a04894971e:10">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4f9505d6c4764d0fa72428eb53d4f802"><span data-offset-key="4f9505d6c4764d0fa72428eb53d4f802:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/itertools.html#itertools.filterfalse" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7675f5acfab64e1a87bc1e6442826c58"><span data-offset-key="7675f5acfab64e1a87bc1e6442826c58:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">itertools.filterfalse()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="dbcb26fbac0045d3b3c4cdaff9407882"><span data-offset-key="dbcb26fbac0045d3b3c4cdaff9407882:0"> for the complementary function that returns elements of </span><span data-offset-key="dbcb26fbac0045d3b3c4cdaff9407882:1">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="dbcb26fbac0045d3b3c4cdaff9407882:2"> for which </span><span data-offset-key="dbcb26fbac0045d3b3c4cdaff9407882:3">_function_</span><span data-offset-key="dbcb26fbac0045d3b3c4cdaff9407882:4"> returns false.</span><span data-offset-key="dbcb26fbac0045d3b3c4cdaff9407882:5">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="dbcb26fbac0045d3b3c4cdaff9407882:6"> </span><span data-offset-key="dbcb26fbac0045d3b3c4cdaff9407882:7">`float`</span><span data-offset-key="dbcb26fbac0045d3b3c4cdaff9407882:8">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="dbcb26fbac0045d3b3c4cdaff9407882:9">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="dbcb26fbac0045d3b3c4cdaff9407882:10">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b218f2705aaf4af4b2b3b60efaac7dad"><span data-offset-key="b218f2705aaf4af4b2b3b60efaac7dad:0">Return a floating point number constructed from a number or string </span><span data-offset-key="b218f2705aaf4af4b2b3b60efaac7dad:1">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="b218f2705aaf4af4b2b3b60efaac7dad:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fe4b4b4e46454ba38d269dd1dcd022b8"><span data-offset-key="fe4b4b4e46454ba38d269dd1dcd022b8:0">If the argument is a string, it should contain a decimal number, optionally preceded by a sign, and optionally embedded in whitespace. The optional sign may be </span><span data-offset-key="fe4b4b4e46454ba38d269dd1dcd022b8:1">`'+'`</span><span data-offset-key="fe4b4b4e46454ba38d269dd1dcd022b8:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="fe4b4b4e46454ba38d269dd1dcd022b8:3">`'-'`</span><span data-offset-key="fe4b4b4e46454ba38d269dd1dcd022b8:4">; a </span><span data-offset-key="fe4b4b4e46454ba38d269dd1dcd022b8:5">`'+'`</span><span data-offset-key="fe4b4b4e46454ba38d269dd1dcd022b8:6"> sign has no effect on the value produced. The argument may also be a string representing a NaN (not-a-number), or a positive or negative infinity. More precisely, the input must conform to the following grammar after leading and trailing whitespace characters are removed:</span></span></span>

    sign           ::=  "+" | "-"infinity       ::=  "Infinity" | "inf"nan            ::=  "nan"numeric_value  ::=  floatnumber | infinity | nannumeric_string ::=  [sign] numeric_value

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6459ab2b74a0490ca00cc3ea7a23025f"><span data-offset-key="6459ab2b74a0490ca00cc3ea7a23025f:0">Here </span><span data-offset-key="6459ab2b74a0490ca00cc3ea7a23025f:1">`floatnumber`</span><span data-offset-key="6459ab2b74a0490ca00cc3ea7a23025f:2"> is the form of a Python floating-point literal, described in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/lexical_analysis.html#floating" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6f5b3f6e092f4d419d7612b3735346d5"><span data-offset-key="6f5b3f6e092f4d419d7612b3735346d5:0">Floating point literals</span></span></a><span data-key="5c8f6c138e7b46e6aefeef51421e9ed7"><span data-offset-key="5c8f6c138e7b46e6aefeef51421e9ed7:0">. Case is not significant, so, for example, “inf”, “Inf”, “INFINITY” and “iNfINity” are all acceptable spellings for positive infinity.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b83e6933323c4e1482a3a8efdeee73ff"><span data-offset-key="b83e6933323c4e1482a3a8efdeee73ff:0">Otherwise, if the argument is an integer or a floating point number, a floating point number with the same value (within Python’s floating point precision) is returned. If the argument is outside the range of a Python float, an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#OverflowError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="945956e38cab4c919833ce4c1e37013a"><span data-offset-key="945956e38cab4c919833ce4c1e37013a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">OverflowError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="638f0fb6d0a24d369918348849b5fa37"><span data-offset-key="638f0fb6d0a24d369918348849b5fa37:0"> will be raised.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="adba3d4fad594f3796de76d3f27479f5"><span data-offset-key="adba3d4fad594f3796de76d3f27479f5:0">For a general Python object </span><span data-offset-key="adba3d4fad594f3796de76d3f27479f5:1">`x`</span><span data-offset-key="adba3d4fad594f3796de76d3f27479f5:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="adba3d4fad594f3796de76d3f27479f5:3">`float(x)`</span><span data-offset-key="adba3d4fad594f3796de76d3f27479f5:4"> delegates to </span><span data-offset-key="adba3d4fad594f3796de76d3f27479f5:5">`x.__float__()`</span><span data-offset-key="adba3d4fad594f3796de76d3f27479f5:6">. If </span><span data-offset-key="adba3d4fad594f3796de76d3f27479f5:7">`__float__()`</span><span data-offset-key="adba3d4fad594f3796de76d3f27479f5:8"> is not defined then it falls back to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f4c710f14e9b444988b81f235b66b93d"><span data-offset-key="f4c710f14e9b444988b81f235b66b93d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**index**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9599e198198e492fb4ad51aaa1157ebe"><span data-offset-key="9599e198198e492fb4ad51aaa1157ebe:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="42fe0e03604d4e03ae78d551b641eccc"><span data-offset-key="42fe0e03604d4e03ae78d551b641eccc:0">If no argument is given, </span><span data-offset-key="42fe0e03604d4e03ae78d551b641eccc:1">`0.0`</span><span data-offset-key="42fe0e03604d4e03ae78d551b641eccc:2"> is returned.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4011801b3e524fc09577c7b7f870e32f"><span data-offset-key="4011801b3e524fc09577c7b7f870e32f:0">Examples:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> float('+1.23')1.23>>> float('   -12345\n')-12345.0>>> float('1e-003')0.001>>> float('+1E6')1000000.0>>> float('-Infinity')-inf

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f93d4e3f636644d0b43d306815bde291"><span data-offset-key="f93d4e3f636644d0b43d306815bde291:0">The float type is described in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesnumeric" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d3d50509b7c8433bb7a34eae08ed1c77"><span data-offset-key="d3d50509b7c8433bb7a34eae08ed1c77:0">Numeric Types — int, float, complex</span></span></a><span data-key="1e5fc1a1fcb349d5a4446ec7dcfd084b"><span data-offset-key="1e5fc1a1fcb349d5a4446ec7dcfd084b:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f99c28ab4adb4cd686e77635159a9766"><span data-offset-key="f99c28ab4adb4cd686e77635159a9766:0">Changed in version 3.6: Grouping digits with underscores as in code literals is allowed.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="886ac823c214406b82889bfbb326c090"><span data-offset-key="886ac823c214406b82889bfbb326c090:0">Changed in version 3.7: </span><span data-offset-key="886ac823c214406b82889bfbb326c090:1">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="886ac823c214406b82889bfbb326c090:2"> is now a positional-only parameter.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="868d7772f9754f358e7c57884b991e7d"><span data-offset-key="868d7772f9754f358e7c57884b991e7d:0">Changed in version 3.8: Falls back to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7baaa69915aa44b6a74c8c4abe2a1672"><span data-offset-key="7baaa69915aa44b6a74c8c4abe2a1672:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**index**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4c940fc882e547fb80dda542fe9fee40"><span data-offset-key="4c940fc882e547fb80dda542fe9fee40:0"> if </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__float__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ff9a415630d0446da030f61b2fe447cd"><span data-offset-key="ff9a415630d0446da030f61b2fe447cd:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**float**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="825feac6301f4ff5bb4b2b289c4b0257"><span data-offset-key="825feac6301f4ff5bb4b2b289c4b0257:0"> is not defined.</span><span data-offset-key="825feac6301f4ff5bb4b2b289c4b0257:1">`format`</span><span data-offset-key="825feac6301f4ff5bb4b2b289c4b0257:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="825feac6301f4ff5bb4b2b289c4b0257:3">_value_</span><span data-offset-key="825feac6301f4ff5bb4b2b289c4b0257:4">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="825feac6301f4ff5bb4b2b289c4b0257:5">_format_spec_</span><span data-offset-key="825feac6301f4ff5bb4b2b289c4b0257:6">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="337fe32c326c4411979f7a1e806e6732"><span data-offset-key="337fe32c326c4411979f7a1e806e6732:0">Convert a </span><span data-offset-key="337fe32c326c4411979f7a1e806e6732:1">_value_</span><span data-offset-key="337fe32c326c4411979f7a1e806e6732:2"> to a “formatted” representation, as controlled by </span><span data-offset-key="337fe32c326c4411979f7a1e806e6732:3">_format_spec_</span><span data-offset-key="337fe32c326c4411979f7a1e806e6732:4">. The interpretation of </span><span data-offset-key="337fe32c326c4411979f7a1e806e6732:5">_format_spec_</span><span data-offset-key="337fe32c326c4411979f7a1e806e6732:6"> will depend on the type of the </span><span data-offset-key="337fe32c326c4411979f7a1e806e6732:7">_value_</span><span data-offset-key="337fe32c326c4411979f7a1e806e6732:8"> argument, however there is a standard formatting syntax that is used by most built-in types: </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/string.html#formatspec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dbcb297dcf084668895bfb112afea6dd"><span data-offset-key="dbcb297dcf084668895bfb112afea6dd:0">Format Specification Mini-Language</span></span></a><span data-key="d88832c2de614e428a0d793551a2ba8c"><span data-offset-key="d88832c2de614e428a0d793551a2ba8c:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="363a5797ce3f4781b24ebe9484d6fc74"><span data-offset-key="363a5797ce3f4781b24ebe9484d6fc74:0">The default </span><span data-offset-key="363a5797ce3f4781b24ebe9484d6fc74:1">_format_spec_</span><span data-offset-key="363a5797ce3f4781b24ebe9484d6fc74:2"> is an empty string which usually gives the same effect as calling </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a8493c8d1f96489a8ebe58db4c943474"><span data-offset-key="a8493c8d1f96489a8ebe58db4c943474:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str(value)</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1a253744261146a4856a0f4ea168216a"><span data-offset-key="1a253744261146a4856a0f4ea168216a:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fda0441aaae747eeaca3c818fc44e560"><span data-offset-key="fda0441aaae747eeaca3c818fc44e560:0">A call to </span><span data-offset-key="fda0441aaae747eeaca3c818fc44e560:1">`format(value, format_spec)`</span><span data-offset-key="fda0441aaae747eeaca3c818fc44e560:2"> is translated to </span><span data-offset-key="fda0441aaae747eeaca3c818fc44e560:3">`type(value).__format__(value, format_spec)`</span><span data-offset-key="fda0441aaae747eeaca3c818fc44e560:4"> which bypasses the instance dictionary when searching for the value’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__format__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5da537f8f56440e7a735b4077ef47f1e"><span data-offset-key="5da537f8f56440e7a735b4077ef47f1e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**format**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="890bfd25a6fa432db1ae5229a669cb01"><span data-offset-key="890bfd25a6fa432db1ae5229a669cb01:0"> method. A </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="066b9bb3d55f43d7bef591adafef321c"><span data-offset-key="066b9bb3d55f43d7bef591adafef321c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">TypeError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c6cf686c699942c4a911456ae05aa64e"><span data-offset-key="c6cf686c699942c4a911456ae05aa64e:0"> exception is raised if the method search reaches </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="69a83859d3914564892e3ff5f4e60eeb"><span data-offset-key="69a83859d3914564892e3ff5f4e60eeb:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">object</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d8d4cade0a9848cd808f523b3cc0e851"><span data-offset-key="d8d4cade0a9848cd808f523b3cc0e851:0"> and the </span><span data-offset-key="d8d4cade0a9848cd808f523b3cc0e851:1">_format_spec_</span><span data-offset-key="d8d4cade0a9848cd808f523b3cc0e851:2"> is non-empty, or if either the </span><span data-offset-key="d8d4cade0a9848cd808f523b3cc0e851:3">_format_spec_</span><span data-offset-key="d8d4cade0a9848cd808f523b3cc0e851:4"> or the return value are not strings.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e346df4d134d46bf8f590e700690b965"><span data-offset-key="e346df4d134d46bf8f590e700690b965:0">Changed in version 3.4: </span><span data-offset-key="e346df4d134d46bf8f590e700690b965:1">`object().__format__(format_spec)`</span><span data-offset-key="e346df4d134d46bf8f590e700690b965:2"> raises </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="82b7f886760e400885486417e4fb7acd"><span data-offset-key="82b7f886760e400885486417e4fb7acd:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">TypeError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="edab7dcad6f1450dad897bfe84422d6a"><span data-offset-key="edab7dcad6f1450dad897bfe84422d6a:0"> if </span><span data-offset-key="edab7dcad6f1450dad897bfe84422d6a:1">_format_spec_</span><span data-offset-key="edab7dcad6f1450dad897bfe84422d6a:2"> is not an empty string.</span><span data-offset-key="edab7dcad6f1450dad897bfe84422d6a:3">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="edab7dcad6f1450dad897bfe84422d6a:4"> </span><span data-offset-key="edab7dcad6f1450dad897bfe84422d6a:5">`frozenset`</span><span data-offset-key="edab7dcad6f1450dad897bfe84422d6a:6">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="edab7dcad6f1450dad897bfe84422d6a:7">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="edab7dcad6f1450dad897bfe84422d6a:8">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5d1ccb096d69475381f96c1623ee551c"><span data-offset-key="5d1ccb096d69475381f96c1623ee551c:0">Return a new </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="81cf84a970b64e46b2a832f50c384f8e"><span data-offset-key="81cf84a970b64e46b2a832f50c384f8e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">frozenset</code></span></span></a><span data-key="19137740bc654a13b5ae3241f78f3b1e"><span data-offset-key="19137740bc654a13b5ae3241f78f3b1e:0"> object, optionally with elements taken from </span><span data-offset-key="19137740bc654a13b5ae3241f78f3b1e:1">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="19137740bc654a13b5ae3241f78f3b1e:2">. </span><span data-offset-key="19137740bc654a13b5ae3241f78f3b1e:3">`frozenset`</span><span data-offset-key="19137740bc654a13b5ae3241f78f3b1e:4"> is a built-in class. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="20072585eccc48d8ae2bcc5ddcbdac56"><span data-offset-key="20072585eccc48d8ae2bcc5ddcbdac56:0">Return the value of the named attribute of </span><span data-offset-key="20072585eccc48d8ae2bcc5ddcbdac56:1">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="20072585eccc48d8ae2bcc5ddcbdac56:2">. </span><span data-offset-key="20072585eccc48d8ae2bcc5ddcbdac56:3">_name_</span><span data-offset-key="20072585eccc48d8ae2bcc5ddcbdac56:4"> must be a string. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="447c6561ddc0479c9afa10bbc854dcc1"><span data-offset-key="447c6561ddc0479c9afa10bbc854dcc1:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5dd9c92b441e456c8cf144bff1d06657"><span data-offset-key="5dd9c92b441e456c8cf144bff1d06657:0">Since </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/expressions.html#private-name-mangling" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0cce802ce4224826b9280c5500fbc4d0"><span data-offset-key="0cce802ce4224826b9280c5500fbc4d0:0">private name mangling</span></span></a><span data-key="18fac967a256471db22c2e2648224e39"><span data-offset-key="18fac967a256471db22c2e2648224e39:0"> happens at compilation time, one must manually mangle a private attribute’s (attributes with two leading underscores) name in order to retrieve it with </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#getattr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c637cc251be74ee88f850c82fad99e70"><span data-offset-key="c637cc251be74ee88f850c82fad99e70:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">getattr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5366d47cc95a4f0197ab3a3dfd4c11b9"><span data-offset-key="5366d47cc95a4f0197ab3a3dfd4c11b9:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="5366d47cc95a4f0197ab3a3dfd4c11b9:1">`globals`</span><span data-offset-key="5366d47cc95a4f0197ab3a3dfd4c11b9:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c870a09c0f374adea332ddd5aab958c3"><span data-offset-key="c870a09c0f374adea332ddd5aab958c3:0">Return a dictionary representing the current global symbol table. This is always the dictionary of the current module (inside a function or method, this is the module where it is defined, not the module from which it is called).</span><span data-offset-key="c870a09c0f374adea332ddd5aab958c3:1">`hasattr`</span><span data-offset-key="c870a09c0f374adea332ddd5aab958c3:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="c870a09c0f374adea332ddd5aab958c3:3">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="c870a09c0f374adea332ddd5aab958c3:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="c870a09c0f374adea332ddd5aab958c3:5">_name_</span><span data-offset-key="c870a09c0f374adea332ddd5aab958c3:6">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="79cf9090d54c44118c1a0593b72bf046"><span data-offset-key="79cf9090d54c44118c1a0593b72bf046:0">The arguments are an object and a string.
