<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="30ed4aee5d964f36bc7f7cd49d940455"><span data-offset-key="30ed4aee5d964f36bc7f7cd49d940455:0">Return the hash value of the object (if it has one). Hash values are integers. They are used to quickly compare dictionary keys during a dictionary lookup. Numeric values that compare equal have the same hash value (even if they are of different types, as is the case for 1 and 1.0).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d98510e7fc3c4d12900fcbc087f26511"><span data-offset-key="d98510e7fc3c4d12900fcbc087f26511:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="26ae4333475d4b04bc32a2df3864074a"><span data-offset-key="26ae4333475d4b04bc32a2df3864074a:0">For objects with custom </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__hash__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4ebb3ca96de04440b63b13eea04250ad"><span data-offset-key="4ebb3ca96de04440b63b13eea04250ad:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**hash**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a1acbda3dd3841be99db9ceebbddf318"><span data-offset-key="a1acbda3dd3841be99db9ceebbddf318:0"> methods, note that </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#hash" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d33f102e560e4a96a0f589a6f49489e6"><span data-offset-key="d33f102e560e4a96a0f589a6f49489e6:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">hash()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="80800a4133544946934c809242b73d61"><span data-offset-key="80800a4133544946934c809242b73d61:0"> truncates the return value based on the bit width of the host machine. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__hash__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="21fcd3be2f9e4d57978cbda351edceac"><span data-offset-key="21fcd3be2f9e4d57978cbda351edceac:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**hash**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="49722a4eccaa41cf92ddcf71dfbd705e"><span data-offset-key="49722a4eccaa41cf92ddcf71dfbd705e:0"> for details.</span><span data-offset-key="49722a4eccaa41cf92ddcf71dfbd705e:1">`help`</span><span data-offset-key="49722a4eccaa41cf92ddcf71dfbd705e:2">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="49722a4eccaa41cf92ddcf71dfbd705e:3">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="49722a4eccaa41cf92ddcf71dfbd705e:4">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5b59e1f3d4b349df95ea5f6d118f2bcd"><span data-offset-key="5b59e1f3d4b349df95ea5f6d118f2bcd:0">Invoke the built-in help system. (This function is intended for interactive use.) If no argument is given, the interactive help system starts on the interpreter console. If the argument is a string, then the string is looked up as the name of a module, function, class, method, keyword, or documentation topic, and a help page is printed on the console. If the argument is any other kind of object, a help page on the object is generated.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="13e7b0698fbb441799b2b5b92547b284"><span data-offset-key="13e7b0698fbb441799b2b5b92547b284:0">Note that if a slash(/) appears in the parameter list of a function, when invoking </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#help" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="160d3bdcf7c447728190276526e613fc"><span data-offset-key="160d3bdcf7c447728190276526e613fc:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">help()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d9b7bb5a9aea40b9b9e3c618dac603fd"><span data-offset-key="d9b7bb5a9aea40b9b9e3c618dac603fd:0">, it means that the parameters prior to the slash are positional-only. For more info, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/faq/programming.html#faq-positional-only-arguments" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="94f6069661114f1d8606613606a97f05"><span data-offset-key="94f6069661114f1d8606613606a97f05:0">the FAQ entry on positional-only parameters</span></span></a><span data-key="1b2c9c81ac92439b9286a6a04c2d466c"><span data-offset-key="1b2c9c81ac92439b9286a6a04c2d466c:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b3c3d09121d74eaaa097fdb749763ddb"><span data-offset-key="b3c3d09121d74eaaa097fdb749763ddb:0">This function is added to the built-in namespace by the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/site.html#module-site" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a653c0de6fd24007badba22b2d62a6c6"><span data-offset-key="a653c0de6fd24007badba22b2d62a6c6:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">site</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b2b9be32196c4cb895dc81a11dcdfec1"><span data-offset-key="b2b9be32196c4cb895dc81a11dcdfec1:0"> module.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ced352b8024749f1bfd457539f2435c5"><span data-offset-key="ced352b8024749f1bfd457539f2435c5:0">Changed in version 3.4: Changes to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/pydoc.html#module-pydoc" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8d45421abd3f43868708f2e9500a2434"><span data-offset-key="8d45421abd3f43868708f2e9500a2434:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">pydoc</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5499b29e77204880bf8a8178d3dc93a6"><span data-offset-key="5499b29e77204880bf8a8178d3dc93a6:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/inspect.html#module-inspect" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bfd2a5e22fab49078ca6b8efa5ccd3e4"><span data-offset-key="bfd2a5e22fab49078ca6b8efa5ccd3e4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">inspect</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3e48336730a34ffabe6129c1e0c01a73"><span data-offset-key="3e48336730a34ffabe6129c1e0c01a73:0"> mean that the reported signatures for callables are now more comprehensive and consistent.</span><span data-offset-key="3e48336730a34ffabe6129c1e0c01a73:1">`hex`</span><span data-offset-key="3e48336730a34ffabe6129c1e0c01a73:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="3e48336730a34ffabe6129c1e0c01a73:3">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="3e48336730a34ffabe6129c1e0c01a73:4">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="da375412624e4eac865669cb285d2095"><span data-offset-key="da375412624e4eac865669cb285d2095:0">Convert an integer number to a lowercase hexadecimal string prefixed with “0x”. If </span><span data-offset-key="da375412624e4eac865669cb285d2095:1">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="da375412624e4eac865669cb285d2095:2"> is not a Python </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e93c2769802f489aa7d0c676bbc27830"><span data-offset-key="e93c2769802f489aa7d0c676bbc27830:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1ad86ecc461c4986bcce9780b8dc64e7"><span data-offset-key="1ad86ecc461c4986bcce9780b8dc64e7:0"> object, it has to define an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="917ee2c8c6464642ad36b2ad5c56abe8"><span data-offset-key="917ee2c8c6464642ad36b2ad5c56abe8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**index**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="aecfe10ce2a34873adc1ca73d31ce298"><span data-offset-key="aecfe10ce2a34873adc1ca73d31ce298:0"> method that returns an integer. Some examples:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> hex(255)'0xff'>>> hex(-42)'-0x2a'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="edfd231f674148e3bb0d92cb7a3b3efa"><span data-offset-key="edfd231f674148e3bb0d92cb7a3b3efa:0">If you want to convert an integer number to an uppercase or lower hexadecimal string with prefix or not, you can use either of the following ways:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> '%#x' % 255, '%x' % 255, '%X' % 255('0xff', 'ff', 'FF')>>> format(255, '#x'), format(255, 'x'), format(255, 'X')('0xff', 'ff', 'FF')>>> f'{255:#x}', f'{255:x}', f'{255:X}'('0xff', 'ff', 'FF')

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a1c501f4963849c7add347d0ae2f8129"><span data-offset-key="a1c501f4963849c7add347d0ae2f8129:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#format" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="baa995e6eb4848639f85b89fca462802"><span data-offset-key="baa995e6eb4848639f85b89fca462802:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">format()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f50d20529ff44b25b287c403ca0f5318"><span data-offset-key="f50d20529ff44b25b287c403ca0f5318:0"> for more information.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="71ce203919664627a7318be79e199ef0"><span data-offset-key="71ce203919664627a7318be79e199ef0:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8f30f979e01648699253032e1020d724"><span data-offset-key="8f30f979e01648699253032e1020d724:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ca3b58d936e8448c8abab4f90f8f95d9"><span data-offset-key="ca3b58d936e8448c8abab4f90f8f95d9:0"> for converting a hexadecimal string to an integer using a base of 16.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="24ccc346acc141cebd38dd6fb259f0bc"><span data-offset-key="24ccc346acc141cebd38dd6fb259f0bc:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="979117ad25704c78bb6fb807ac30231f"><span data-offset-key="979117ad25704c78bb6fb807ac30231f:0">To obtain a hexadecimal string representation for a float, use the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#float.hex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="44df28e9611247078420ffe588f8ee04"><span data-offset-key="44df28e9611247078420ffe588f8ee04:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">float.hex()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="431a2ef2870344a4a9ff878e29e6e085"><span data-offset-key="431a2ef2870344a4a9ff878e29e6e085:0"> method.</span><span data-offset-key="431a2ef2870344a4a9ff878e29e6e085:1">`id`</span><span data-offset-key="431a2ef2870344a4a9ff878e29e6e085:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="431a2ef2870344a4a9ff878e29e6e085:3">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="431a2ef2870344a4a9ff878e29e6e085:4">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bfc4ad961b79447f81378c48acd0312c"><span data-offset-key="bfc4ad961b79447f81378c48acd0312c:0">Return the “identity” of an object. This is an integer which is guaranteed to be unique and constant for this object during its lifetime. Two objects with non-overlapping lifetimes may have the same </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#id" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4dc45db4aa6640eb9daa5f03175ff1cc"><span data-offset-key="4dc45db4aa6640eb9daa5f03175ff1cc:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">id()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1d66ca266fe8407facefb0c7a40530c0"><span data-offset-key="1d66ca266fe8407facefb0c7a40530c0:0"> value.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7ab1a255c0414635ac0d8255189d53ad"><span data-offset-key="7ab1a255c0414635ac0d8255189d53ad:0">**CPython implementation detail:**</span><span data-offset-key="7ab1a255c0414635ac0d8255189d53ad:1"> This is the address of the object in memory.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="80aa9dcd4d3b4840b070d772c75906cf"><span data-offset-key="80aa9dcd4d3b4840b070d772c75906cf:0">Raises an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#auditing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ef01bbf8a39448dbb29a6b7ddc39618b"><span data-offset-key="ef01bbf8a39448dbb29a6b7ddc39618b:0">auditing event</span></span></a><span data-key="fcfaa341cefb45adbde1a1c23f292481"><span data-offset-key="fcfaa341cefb45adbde1a1c23f292481:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="fcfaa341cefb45adbde1a1c23f292481:1">`builtins.id`</span><span data-offset-key="fcfaa341cefb45adbde1a1c23f292481:2"> with argument </span><span data-offset-key="fcfaa341cefb45adbde1a1c23f292481:3">`id`</span><span data-offset-key="fcfaa341cefb45adbde1a1c23f292481:4">.</span><span data-offset-key="fcfaa341cefb45adbde1a1c23f292481:5">`input`</span><span data-offset-key="fcfaa341cefb45adbde1a1c23f292481:6">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="fcfaa341cefb45adbde1a1c23f292481:7">_prompt_</span><span data-offset-key="fcfaa341cefb45adbde1a1c23f292481:8">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c1742b31cd804f9eb101198325c7c942"><span data-offset-key="c1742b31cd804f9eb101198325c7c942:0">If the </span><span data-offset-key="c1742b31cd804f9eb101198325c7c942:1">_prompt_</span><span data-offset-key="c1742b31cd804f9eb101198325c7c942:2"> argument is present, it is written to standard output without a trailing newline. The function then reads a line from input, converts it to a string (stripping a trailing newline), and returns that. When EOF is read, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#EOFError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="563546978193439d9d35235d943e14c4"><span data-offset-key="563546978193439d9d35235d943e14c4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">EOFError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6b6b92606cc2488a8ade00d499ce95d7"><span data-offset-key="6b6b92606cc2488a8ade00d499ce95d7:0"> is raised. Example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> s = input('--> ')  --> Monty Python's Flying Circus>>> s  "Monty Python's Flying Circus"

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a44e38654b934ed3beb59d0f60c3493a"><span data-offset-key="a44e38654b934ed3beb59d0f60c3493a:0">If the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/readline.html#module-readline" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="429e17325e134737af193dce41f38d50"><span data-offset-key="429e17325e134737af193dce41f38d50:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">readline</code></span></span></a><span data-key="20ef0932ee374b2aa652283134bce6f2"><span data-offset-key="20ef0932ee374b2aa652283134bce6f2:0"> module was loaded, then </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#input" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a0d628419b264ad781553f1200fb6696"><span data-offset-key="a0d628419b264ad781553f1200fb6696:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">input()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3873cc5ede414933b7d94f413d0eef62"><span data-offset-key="3873cc5ede414933b7d94f413d0eef62:0"> will use it to provide elaborate line editing and history features.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="33affdc1df37454994bb1d27744f43f9"><span data-offset-key="33affdc1df37454994bb1d27744f43f9:0">Raises an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#auditing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="385e4b69850348508a6466f51aa23ed2"><span data-offset-key="385e4b69850348508a6466f51aa23ed2:0">auditing event</span></span></a><span data-key="d22b07b072d149469b65ae9c114025dc"><span data-offset-key="d22b07b072d149469b65ae9c114025dc:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="d22b07b072d149469b65ae9c114025dc:1">`builtins.input`</span><span data-offset-key="d22b07b072d149469b65ae9c114025dc:2"> with argument </span><span data-offset-key="d22b07b072d149469b65ae9c114025dc:3">`prompt`</span><span data-offset-key="d22b07b072d149469b65ae9c114025dc:4"> before reading input</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f8a7bf5f21ec4ba18f684aa8f0b722a4"><span data-offset-key="f8a7bf5f21ec4ba18f684aa8f0b722a4:0">Raises an auditing event </span><span data-offset-key="f8a7bf5f21ec4ba18f684aa8f0b722a4:1">`builtins.input/result`</span><span data-offset-key="f8a7bf5f21ec4ba18f684aa8f0b722a4:2"> with the result after successfully reading input.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08"><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:0">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:1"> </span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:2">`int`</span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:3">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:4">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:5">\])</span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:6">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:7"> </span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:8">`int`</span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:9">(</span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:10">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:11">, </span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:12">_base=10_</span><span data-offset-key="fab9e85e48a349a78cd019ac68a0ec08:13">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5d6344702f9346bb8cd90866390f5eb8"><span data-offset-key="5d6344702f9346bb8cd90866390f5eb8:0">Return an integer object constructed from a number or string </span><span data-offset-key="5d6344702f9346bb8cd90866390f5eb8:1">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="5d6344702f9346bb8cd90866390f5eb8:2">, or return </span><span data-offset-key="5d6344702f9346bb8cd90866390f5eb8:3">`0`</span><span data-offset-key="5d6344702f9346bb8cd90866390f5eb8:4"> if no arguments are given. If </span><span data-offset-key="5d6344702f9346bb8cd90866390f5eb8:5">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="5d6344702f9346bb8cd90866390f5eb8:6"> defines </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__int__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b592a5368b394a7db8a9fecb3192f429"><span data-offset-key="b592a5368b394a7db8a9fecb3192f429:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**int**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9e9b05db6dd2424b94f0500362528488"><span data-offset-key="9e9b05db6dd2424b94f0500362528488:0">, </span><span data-offset-key="9e9b05db6dd2424b94f0500362528488:1">`int(x)`</span><span data-offset-key="9e9b05db6dd2424b94f0500362528488:2"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="9e9b05db6dd2424b94f0500362528488:3">`x.__int__()`</span><span data-offset-key="9e9b05db6dd2424b94f0500362528488:4">. If </span><span data-offset-key="9e9b05db6dd2424b94f0500362528488:5">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="9e9b05db6dd2424b94f0500362528488:6"> defines </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0d751d2e268f42e28b9bc008ca9bde58"><span data-offset-key="0d751d2e268f42e28b9bc008ca9bde58:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**index**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6b2d834de3324595a9a75f8b0c99d868"><span data-offset-key="6b2d834de3324595a9a75f8b0c99d868:0">, it returns </span><span data-offset-key="6b2d834de3324595a9a75f8b0c99d868:1">`x.__index__()`</span><span data-offset-key="6b2d834de3324595a9a75f8b0c99d868:2">. If </span><span data-offset-key="6b2d834de3324595a9a75f8b0c99d868:3">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="6b2d834de3324595a9a75f8b0c99d868:4"> defines </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__trunc__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8ac1e9ba4d604726a31c0b8c6d4dadbc"><span data-offset-key="8ac1e9ba4d604726a31c0b8c6d4dadbc:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**trunc**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2a12c7612c5c4f7f90e2241ce32e3d61"><span data-offset-key="2a12c7612c5c4f7f90e2241ce32e3d61:0">, it returns </span><span data-offset-key="2a12c7612c5c4f7f90e2241ce32e3d61:1">`x.__trunc__()`</span><span data-offset-key="2a12c7612c5c4f7f90e2241ce32e3d61:2">. For floating point numbers, this truncates towards zero.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4e3bc70fbb9d4a268c15cd29cfd016f8"><span data-offset-key="4e3bc70fbb9d4a268c15cd29cfd016f8:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="4e3bc70fbb9d4a268c15cd29cfd016f8:1">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="4e3bc70fbb9d4a268c15cd29cfd016f8:2"> is not a number or if </span><span data-offset-key="4e3bc70fbb9d4a268c15cd29cfd016f8:3">_base_</span><span data-offset-key="4e3bc70fbb9d4a268c15cd29cfd016f8:4"> is given, then </span><span data-offset-key="4e3bc70fbb9d4a268c15cd29cfd016f8:5">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="4e3bc70fbb9d4a268c15cd29cfd016f8:6"> must be a string, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="263f1c7f51af4906a7f597e1aa204b41"><span data-offset-key="263f1c7f51af4906a7f597e1aa204b41:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f2f4b2d366a64c2c86f1d079d780f842"><span data-offset-key="f2f4b2d366a64c2c86f1d079d780f842:0">, or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c6a148558f844dcdbd88c4d7f7c5b736"><span data-offset-key="c6a148558f844dcdbd88c4d7f7c5b736:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytearray</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8a13bcfddbc54c42a45da65bc27da5ee"><span data-offset-key="8a13bcfddbc54c42a45da65bc27da5ee:0"> instance representing an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/lexical_analysis.html#integers" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ad563121e31f4f1c8e36840047d66c88"><span data-offset-key="ad563121e31f4f1c8e36840047d66c88:0">integer literal</span></span></a><span data-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09"><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:0"> in radix </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:1">_base_</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:2">. Optionally, the literal can be preceded by </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:3">`+`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:4"> or </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:5">`-`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:6"> (with no space in between) and surrounded by whitespace. A base-n literal consists of the digits 0 to n-1, with </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:7">`a`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:8"> to </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:9">`z`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:10"> (or </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:11">`A`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:12"> to </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:13">`Z`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:14">) having values 10 to 35. The default </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:15">_base_</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:16"> is 10. The allowed values are 0 and 2–36. Base-2, -8, and -16 literals can be optionally prefixed with </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:17">`0b`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:18">/</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:19">`0B`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:20">, </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:21">`0o`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:22">/</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:23">`0O`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:24">, or </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:25">`0x`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:26">/</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:27">`0X`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:28">, as with integer literals in code. Base 0 means to interpret exactly as a code literal, so that the actual base is 2, 8, 10, or 16, and so that </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:29">`int('010', 0)`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:30"> is not legal, while </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:31">`int('010')`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:32"> is, as well as </span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:33">`int('010', 8)`</span><span data-offset-key="28805b8ede2e42ccacda863866aead09:34">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4d10e97176b1489386c759f5bbb6af12"><span data-offset-key="4d10e97176b1489386c759f5bbb6af12:0">The integer type is described in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesnumeric" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4ec7b5d283254694b0543e52341564d0"><span data-offset-key="4ec7b5d283254694b0543e52341564d0:0">Numeric Types — int, float, complex</span></span></a><span data-key="c7cb70d5fcf844a495eb8e1f88417462"><span data-offset-key="c7cb70d5fcf844a495eb8e1f88417462:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a50af1b6818e4cc59820e214f2bdbf9a"><span data-offset-key="a50af1b6818e4cc59820e214f2bdbf9a:0">Changed in version 3.4: If </span><span data-offset-key="a50af1b6818e4cc59820e214f2bdbf9a:1">_base_</span><span data-offset-key="a50af1b6818e4cc59820e214f2bdbf9a:2"> is not an instance of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="614f0dc88ee64e2a8d6cb03ac07c68fc"><span data-offset-key="614f0dc88ee64e2a8d6cb03ac07c68fc:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="50100b7b27a541f1ab2433dfaa560661"><span data-offset-key="50100b7b27a541f1ab2433dfaa560661:0"> and the </span><span data-offset-key="50100b7b27a541f1ab2433dfaa560661:1">_base_</span><span data-offset-key="50100b7b27a541f1ab2433dfaa560661:2"> object has a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fc3ff663b6ff463db4c7f1da73bcafae"><span data-offset-key="fc3ff663b6ff463db4c7f1da73bcafae:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">base.**index**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e0940ce8a5194aa4b281788ea13a368f"><span data-offset-key="e0940ce8a5194aa4b281788ea13a368f:0"> method, that method is called to obtain an integer for the base. Previous versions used </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__int__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="01232a96e858478d82ab13d70a3598a0"><span data-offset-key="01232a96e858478d82ab13d70a3598a0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">base.**int**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5d80a5ac90a74080b3bd20dc7c69289a"><span data-offset-key="5d80a5ac90a74080b3bd20dc7c69289a:0"> instead of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="25b722c7a56645569f5b8dd3d8872151"><span data-offset-key="25b722c7a56645569f5b8dd3d8872151:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">base.**index**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ff384cc28b1e431dad1498e9f6823aad"><span data-offset-key="ff384cc28b1e431dad1498e9f6823aad:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="82e2c1e21ecc4dde9761006f13d84542"><span data-offset-key="82e2c1e21ecc4dde9761006f13d84542:0">Changed in version 3.6: Grouping digits with underscores as in code literals is allowed.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="72f25aef4b7b4001af3eab0f9fff98aa"><span data-offset-key="72f25aef4b7b4001af3eab0f9fff98aa:0">Changed in version 3.7: </span><span data-offset-key="72f25aef4b7b4001af3eab0f9fff98aa:1">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="72f25aef4b7b4001af3eab0f9fff98aa:2"> is now a positional-only parameter.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="93d1d0968450419e84156eb6b9a2b968"><span data-offset-key="93d1d0968450419e84156eb6b9a2b968:0">Changed in version 3.8: Falls back to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d3c2c72bddca445f8dd0d211ced3d10e"><span data-offset-key="d3c2c72bddca445f8dd0d211ced3d10e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**index**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ea2d021159074e71ac2de2aabb950994"><span data-offset-key="ea2d021159074e71ac2de2aabb950994:0"> if </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__int__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="29fd5b51cb8c434eaf9e55cbaf6becf5"><span data-offset-key="29fd5b51cb8c434eaf9e55cbaf6becf5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**int**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4efba638aecb4098acdd4725cdd429a4"><span data-offset-key="4efba638aecb4098acdd4725cdd429a4:0"> is not defined.</span><span data-offset-key="4efba638aecb4098acdd4725cdd429a4:1">`isinstance`</span><span data-offset-key="4efba638aecb4098acdd4725cdd429a4:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="4efba638aecb4098acdd4725cdd429a4:3">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="4efba638aecb4098acdd4725cdd429a4:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="4efba638aecb4098acdd4725cdd429a4:5">_classinfo_</span><span data-offset-key="4efba638aecb4098acdd4725cdd429a4:6">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="02c41f710a65439eb8c869776b497eea"><span data-offset-key="02c41f710a65439eb8c869776b497eea:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="02c41f710a65439eb8c869776b497eea:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="02c41f710a65439eb8c869776b497eea:2"> if the </span><span data-offset-key="02c41f710a65439eb8c869776b497eea:3">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="02c41f710a65439eb8c869776b497eea:4"> argument is an instance of the </span><span data-offset-key="02c41f710a65439eb8c869776b497eea:5">_classinfo_</span><span data-offset-key="02c41f710a65439eb8c869776b497eea:6"> argument, or of a (direct, indirect or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-abstract-base-class" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="19f88a1fa1194cb19c3aafbf828c7aa8"><span data-offset-key="19f88a1fa1194cb19c3aafbf828c7aa8:0">virtual</span></span></a><span data-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255"><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:0">) subclass thereof. If </span><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:1">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:2"> is not an object of the given type, the function always returns </span><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:4">. If </span><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:5">_classinfo_</span><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:6"> is a tuple of type objects (or recursively, other such tuples), return </span><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:7">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:8"> if </span><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:9">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:10"> is an instance of any of the types. If </span><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:11">_classinfo_</span><span data-offset-key="55905311635740dca43008c34b83f255:12"> is not a type or tuple of types and such tuples, a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6c8f8efa97eb47069c023986c6c1e74d"><span data-offset-key="6c8f8efa97eb47069c023986c6c1e74d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">TypeError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8d40a87eb16441d886c297b2cf406559"><span data-offset-key="8d40a87eb16441d886c297b2cf406559:0"> exception is raised.</span><span data-offset-key="8d40a87eb16441d886c297b2cf406559:1">`issubclass`</span><span data-offset-key="8d40a87eb16441d886c297b2cf406559:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="8d40a87eb16441d886c297b2cf406559:3">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="8d40a87eb16441d886c297b2cf406559:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="8d40a87eb16441d886c297b2cf406559:5">_classinfo_</span><span data-offset-key="8d40a87eb16441d886c297b2cf406559:6">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3f2e1c0b087e4515869712ed1dbef4ff"><span data-offset-key="3f2e1c0b087e4515869712ed1dbef4ff:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="3f2e1c0b087e4515869712ed1dbef4ff:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="3f2e1c0b087e4515869712ed1dbef4ff:2"> if </span><span data-offset-key="3f2e1c0b087e4515869712ed1dbef4ff:3">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="3f2e1c0b087e4515869712ed1dbef4ff:4"> is a subclass (direct, indirect or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-abstract-base-class" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="37a6cb6eafb64e9cbf93731d17bcc8d6"><span data-offset-key="37a6cb6eafb64e9cbf93731d17bcc8d6:0">virtual</span></span></a><span data-key="99d94367943e49cc8b33778efff3cc7f"><span data-offset-key="99d94367943e49cc8b33778efff3cc7f:0">) of </span><span data-offset-key="99d94367943e49cc8b33778efff3cc7f:1">_classinfo_</span><span data-offset-key="99d94367943e49cc8b33778efff3cc7f:2">. A class is considered a subclass of itself. </span><span data-offset-key="99d94367943e49cc8b33778efff3cc7f:3">_classinfo_</span><span data-offset-key="99d94367943e49cc8b33778efff3cc7f:4"> may be a tuple of class objects, in which case every entry in </span><span data-offset-key="99d94367943e49cc8b33778efff3cc7f:5">_classinfo_</span><span data-offset-key="99d94367943e49cc8b33778efff3cc7f:6"> will be checked. In any other case, a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2bed965ff1ae48b9b823543ab52ea5c1"><span data-offset-key="2bed965ff1ae48b9b823543ab52ea5c1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">TypeError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b0d6df135f1f4e0e930ce61ed79289da"><span data-offset-key="b0d6df135f1f4e0e930ce61ed79289da:0"> exception is raised.</span><span data-offset-key="b0d6df135f1f4e0e930ce61ed79289da:1">`iter`</span><span data-offset-key="b0d6df135f1f4e0e930ce61ed79289da:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="b0d6df135f1f4e0e930ce61ed79289da:3">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="b0d6df135f1f4e0e930ce61ed79289da:4">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="b0d6df135f1f4e0e930ce61ed79289da:5">_sentinel_</span><span data-offset-key="b0d6df135f1f4e0e930ce61ed79289da:6">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fe70fffa315449fd92b82558644b4087"><span data-offset-key="fe70fffa315449fd92b82558644b4087:0">Return an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-iterator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9748c1db3dd64479aa4ee53323020dbf"><span data-offset-key="9748c1db3dd64479aa4ee53323020dbf:0">iterator</span></span></a><span data-key="cacfc53ef19a45c6a9339f6062d16057"><span data-offset-key="cacfc53ef19a45c6a9339f6062d16057:0"> object. The first argument is interpreted very differently depending on the presence of the second argument. Without a second argument, </span><span data-offset-key="cacfc53ef19a45c6a9339f6062d16057:1">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="cacfc53ef19a45c6a9339f6062d16057:2"> must be a collection object which supports the iteration protocol (the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__iter__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="15adb16f981b4a3e860d49bab511fcfd"><span data-offset-key="15adb16f981b4a3e860d49bab511fcfd:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**iter**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="cc1b8ee1bacf4742a69f05367b3a4fb1"><span data-offset-key="cc1b8ee1bacf4742a69f05367b3a4fb1:0"> method), or it must support the sequence protocol (the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="df0833b11be448f89dc98fe0aa328e91"><span data-offset-key="df0833b11be448f89dc98fe0aa328e91:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**getitem**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3cf3576de598420b822dcc2235a03947"><span data-offset-key="3cf3576de598420b822dcc2235a03947:0"> method with integer arguments starting at </span><span data-offset-key="3cf3576de598420b822dcc2235a03947:1">`0`</span><span data-offset-key="3cf3576de598420b822dcc2235a03947:2">). If it does not support either of those protocols, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="aba94f8fa61f4a8a845e705541573419"><span data-offset-key="aba94f8fa61f4a8a845e705541573419:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">TypeError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="603c78989c084efcbb4a516afc951a62"><span data-offset-key="603c78989c084efcbb4a516afc951a62:0"> is raised. If the second argument, </span><span data-offset-key="603c78989c084efcbb4a516afc951a62:1">_sentinel_</span><span data-offset-key="603c78989c084efcbb4a516afc951a62:2">, is given, then </span><span data-offset-key="603c78989c084efcbb4a516afc951a62:3">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="603c78989c084efcbb4a516afc951a62:4"> must be a callable object. The iterator created in this case will call </span><span data-offset-key="603c78989c084efcbb4a516afc951a62:5">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="603c78989c084efcbb4a516afc951a62:6"> with no arguments for each call to its </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#iterator.__next__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="feb33dc4c9474dfba8a0535b713f0164"><span data-offset-key="feb33dc4c9474dfba8a0535b713f0164:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**next**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="029b59564c674bd8911227bf60a5f5ce"><span data-offset-key="029b59564c674bd8911227bf60a5f5ce:0"> method; if the value returned is equal to </span><span data-offset-key="029b59564c674bd8911227bf60a5f5ce:1">_sentinel_</span><span data-offset-key="029b59564c674bd8911227bf60a5f5ce:2">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#StopIteration" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="179c8edd3e4c435a87e966d39c216fb9"><span data-offset-key="179c8edd3e4c435a87e966d39c216fb9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">StopIteration</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4732a3c110fc478e948010a30b5f7fea"><span data-offset-key="4732a3c110fc478e948010a30b5f7fea:0"> will be raised, otherwise the value will be returned.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="af56665bef0142448ca4b9092f901d5c"><span data-offset-key="af56665bef0142448ca4b9092f901d5c:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typeiter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2244455bb7a34f62bd41d8b53c10fda9"><span data-offset-key="2244455bb7a34f62bd41d8b53c10fda9:0">Iterator Types</span></span></a><span data-key="598d334cbfd2419e88e28e3c6c5ba29e"><span data-offset-key="598d334cbfd2419e88e28e3c6c5ba29e:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f0158b6abad942418bc8ed198c5ef0f4"><span data-offset-key="f0158b6abad942418bc8ed198c5ef0f4:0">One useful application of the second form of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#iter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0c8b86203753426da0e73163f371bbc3"><span data-offset-key="0c8b86203753426da0e73163f371bbc3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">iter()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2246ccf8db8d4afaa62705daa867a597"><span data-offset-key="2246ccf8db8d4afaa62705daa867a597:0"> is to build a block-reader. For example, reading fixed-width blocks from a binary database file until the end of file is reached:</span></span></span>

    from functools import partialwith open('mydata.db', 'rb') as f:    for block in iter(partial(f.read, 64), b''):        process_block(block)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="08410658b57244db8f4bcbb36bfe0359"><span data-offset-key="08410658b57244db8f4bcbb36bfe0359:0">`len`</span><span data-offset-key="08410658b57244db8f4bcbb36bfe0359:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="08410658b57244db8f4bcbb36bfe0359:2">_s_</span><span data-offset-key="08410658b57244db8f4bcbb36bfe0359:3">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="932864bfebdd485bbb8e30e09aaaae4c"><span data-offset-key="932864bfebdd485bbb8e30e09aaaae4c:0">Return the length (the number of items) of an object. The argument may be a sequence (such as a string, bytes, tuple, list, or range) or a collection (such as a dictionary, set, or frozen set).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ec28447841714a9193fed4a486cdbea8"><span data-offset-key="ec28447841714a9193fed4a486cdbea8:0">**CPython implementation detail:**</span><span data-offset-key="ec28447841714a9193fed4a486cdbea8:1"> </span><span data-offset-key="ec28447841714a9193fed4a486cdbea8:2">`len`</span><span data-offset-key="ec28447841714a9193fed4a486cdbea8:3"> raises </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#OverflowError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4c7b408b340d4941b78cfe668001347d"><span data-offset-key="4c7b408b340d4941b78cfe668001347d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">OverflowError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="59e0c01e4c9348caa4e46eaa02877cb1"><span data-offset-key="59e0c01e4c9348caa4e46eaa02877cb1:0"> on lengths larger than </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.maxsize" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b08e9ffd031442ce97d7060b4299a066"><span data-offset-key="b08e9ffd031442ce97d7060b4299a066:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.maxsize</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e6dc87d5643d4d68bcce9881bb6e1b7b"><span data-offset-key="e6dc87d5643d4d68bcce9881bb6e1b7b:0">, such as </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#range" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ff951e6b8ac148968d1196a624817df3"><span data-key="4475f6cc06ea4b939981e5514c993263"><span data-offset-key="4475f6cc06ea4b939981e5514c993263:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="4475f6cc06ea4b939981e5514c993263:1">*class*</span><span data-offset-key="4475f6cc06ea4b939981e5514c993263:4">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="4475f6cc06ea4b939981e5514c993263:5">*iterable\*</span><span <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="46e347bcdb3445afafe4a884f78e9409"><span data-offset-key="46e347bcdb3445afafe4a884f78e9409:0">Rather than being a function, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="54c2d5d37a834930ac2a6618f6843d0b"><span data-offset-key="54c2d5d37a834930ac2a6618f6843d0b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5bc9fd1e2b8f418382197b3a801afcc1"><span data-offset-key="5bc9fd1e2b8f418382197b3a801afcc1:0"> is actually a mutable sequence type, as documented in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq-list" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="feb014e0e9974ac6882c20cb19f01f1c"><span data-offset-key="feb014e0e9974ac6882c20cb19f01f1c:0">Lists</span></span></a><span data-key="b54bbfd8f3dd4057abac667675f01b1b"><span data-offset-key="b54bbfd8f3dd4057abac667675f01b1b:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="21863a3c3dbf4edf85e7b70cf2976d3a"><span data-offset-key="21863a3c3dbf4edf85e7b70cf2976d3a:0">Sequence Types — list, tuple, range</span></span></a><span data-key="a1c7b73e2df94e3da609f737fae7d17c"><span data-offset-key="a1c7b73e2df94e3da609f737fae7d17c:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="a1c7b73e2df94e3da609f737fae7d17c:1">`locals`</span><span data-offset-key="a1c7b73e2df94e3da609f737fae7d17c:2">()</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ea6e0fc615db4b1290f8e259ebc00ed2"><span data-offset-key="ea6e0fc615db4b1290f8e259ebc00ed2:0">Update and return a dictionary representing the current local symbol table. Free variables are returned by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#locals" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b81cb71564c04657a9b85ae06ef325e6"><span data-offset-key="b81cb71564c04657a9b85ae06ef325e6:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">locals()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="24505d8cfded419ebb7fddf045cd86b1"><span data-offset-key="24505d8cfded419ebb7fddf045cd86b1:0"> when it is called in function blocks, but not in class blocks. Note that at the module level, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#locals" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="024a617608d34b91829ca5151715f229"><span data-offset-key="024a617608d34b91829ca5151715f229:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">locals()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d30109b055ce48dea91095b946c50c5b"><span data-offset-key="d30109b055ce48dea91095b946c50c5b:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#globals" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b133e05428fa4975a072813704ddfe26"><span data-offset-key="b133e05428fa4975a072813704ddfe26:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">globals()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="79a5df351d804e50a3a00b321c1d8408"><span data-offset-key="79a5df351d804e50a3a00b321c1d8408:0"> are the same dictionary.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6f7ee7672a9247848ba05cd98ca1f802"><span data-offset-key="6f7ee7672a9247848ba05cd98ca1f802:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ef163e6ff0724557b0217ceb0e01fd1d"><span data-offset-key="ef163e6ff0724557b0217ceb0e01fd1d:0">The contents of this dictionary should not be modified; changes may not affect the values of local and free variables used by the interpreter.</span><span data-offset-key="ef163e6ff0724557b0217ceb0e01fd1d:1">`map`</span><span data-offset-key="ef163e6ff0724557b0217ceb0e01fd1d:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="ef163e6ff0724557b0217ceb0e01fd1d:3">_function_</span><span data-offset-key="ef163e6ff0724557b0217ceb0e01fd1d:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="ef163e6ff0724557b0217ceb0e01fd1d:5">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="ef163e6ff0724557b0217ceb0e01fd1d:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="ef163e6ff0724557b0217ceb0e01fd1d:7">_..._</span><span data-offset-key="ef163e6ff0724557b0217ceb0e01fd1d:8">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="22ff30966a1b4368a20fbaef279f7573"><span data-offset-key="22ff30966a1b4368a20fbaef279f7573:0">Return an iterator that applies </span><span data-offset-key="22ff30966a1b4368a20fbaef279f7573:1">_function_</span><span data-offset-key="22ff30966a1b4368a20fbaef279f7573:2"> to every item of </span><span data-offset-key="22ff30966a1b4368a20fbaef279f7573:3">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="22ff30966a1b4368a20fbaef279f7573:4">, yielding the results. If additional </span><span data-offset-key="22ff30966a1b4368a20fbaef279f7573:5">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="22ff30966a1b4368a20fbaef279f7573:6"> arguments are passed, </span><span data-offset-key="22ff30966a1b4368a20fbaef279f7573:7">_function_</span><span data-offset-key="22ff30966a1b4368a20fbaef279f7573:8"> must take that many arguments and is applied to the items from all iterables in parallel. With multiple iterables, the iterator stops when the shortest iterable is exhausted. For cases where the function inputs are already arranged into argument tuples, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/itertools.html#itertools.starmap" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="23f808c6367342cd9e2dda2c85b7506b"><span data-offset-key="23f808c6367342cd9e2dda2c85b7506b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">itertools.starmap()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e"><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:1">`max`</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:3">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:5">\*\**</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:6">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:7">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:8">, </span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:9">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:10">\])</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:11">`max`</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:12">(</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:13">*arg1*</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:14">, </span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:15">*arg2*</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:16">, </span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:17">*\*args*</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:18">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:19">*key\*</span><span data-offset-key="2d9af55b63d2462fb388eaf3b4caf95e:20">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="57b18152bf804a7e89c14de1226a9dee"><span data-offset-key="57b18152bf804a7e89c14de1226a9dee:0">Return the largest item in an iterable or the largest of two or more arguments.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a557999bc6a14361989836a6a3456acd"><span data-offset-key="a557999bc6a14361989836a6a3456acd:0">If one positional argument is provided, it should be an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-iterable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="470b7fbb7cf04ed6ad1a4a220e06aa6f"><span data-offset-key="470b7fbb7cf04ed6ad1a4a220e06aa6f:0">iterable</span></span></a><span data-key="ab9c547ea433415f8e7971781b3582bc"><span data-offset-key="ab9c547ea433415f8e7971781b3582bc:0">. The largest item in the iterable is returned. If two or more positional arguments are provided, the largest of the positional arguments is returned.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7449938d5b364e1ab26271956a399e4b"><span data-offset-key="7449938d5b364e1ab26271956a399e4b:0">There are two optional keyword-only arguments. The </span><span data-offset-key="7449938d5b364e1ab26271956a399e4b:1">_key_</span><span data-offset-key="7449938d5b364e1ab26271956a399e4b:2"> argument specifies a one-argument ordering function like that used for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list.sort" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f16e7199673e4d768753057d4ed26e5b"><span data-offset-key="f16e7199673e4d768753057d4ed26e5b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list.sort()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="eecec72a5f6a4ae2a7f16c4a554b1f7c"><span data-offset-key="eecec72a5f6a4ae2a7f16c4a554b1f7c:0">. The </span><span data-offset-key="eecec72a5f6a4ae2a7f16c4a554b1f7c:1">_default_</span><span data-offset-key="eecec72a5f6a4ae2a7f16c4a554b1f7c:2"> argument specifies an object to return if the provided iterable is empty. If the iterable is empty and </span><span data-offset-key="eecec72a5f6a4ae2a7f16c4a554b1f7c:3">_default_</span><span data-offset-key="eecec72a5f6a4ae2a7f16c4a554b1f7c:4"> is not provided, a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ValueError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="20a9877f7e0b4efb90468e6490b890e8"><span data-offset-key="20a9877f7e0b4efb90468e6490b890e8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ValueError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4d345c635de44b659be268987a651f23"><span data-offset-key="4d345c635de44b659be268987a651f23:0"> is raised.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="efe36ffb985647128118c87a2a12e0ed"><span data-offset-key="efe36ffb985647128118c87a2a12e0ed:0">If multiple items are maximal, the function returns the first one encountered. This is consistent with other sort-stability preserving tools such as </span><span data-offset-key="efe36ffb985647128118c87a2a12e0ed:1">`sorted(iterable, key=keyfunc, reverse=True)[0]`</span><span data-offset-key="efe36ffb985647128118c87a2a12e0ed:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="efe36ffb985647128118c87a2a12e0ed:3">`heapq.nlargest(1, iterable, key=keyfunc)`</span><span data-offset-key="efe36ffb985647128118c87a2a12e0ed:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e9251814e4bb41dfb64601e16b3d31bc"><span data-offset-key="e9251814e4bb41dfb64601e16b3d31bc:0">New in version 3.4: The </span><span data-offset-key="e9251814e4bb41dfb64601e16b3d31bc:1">_default_</span><span data-offset-key="e9251814e4bb41dfb64601e16b3d31bc:2"> keyword-only argument.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ae48cc3bcb734e47a7374c855969b2db"><span data-offset-key="ae48cc3bcb734e47a7374c855969b2db:0">Changed in version 3.8: The </span><span data-offset-key="ae48cc3bcb734e47a7374c855969b2db:1">_key_</span><span data-offset-key="ae48cc3bcb734e47a7374c855969b2db:2"> can be </span><span data-offset-key="ae48cc3bcb734e47a7374c855969b2db:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="ae48cc3bcb734e47a7374c855969b2db:4">.</span><span data-offset-key="ae48cc3bcb734e47a7374c855969b2db:5">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="ae48cc3bcb734e47a7374c855969b2db:6"> </span><span data-offset-key="ae48cc3bcb734e47a7374c855969b2db:7">`memoryview`</span><span data-offset-key="ae48cc3bcb734e47a7374c855969b2db:8">(</span><span data-offset-key="ae48cc3bcb734e47a7374c855969b2db:9">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="ae48cc3bcb734e47a7374c855969b2db:10">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="be8f19c49c6d413385b2b6fc0581c936"><span data-offset-key="be8f19c49c6d413385b2b6fc0581c936:0">Return a “memory view” object created from the given argument. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typememoryview" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="da1d4a9845ac458c8ba79d1639561eac"><span data-offset-key="da1d4a9845ac458c8ba79d1639561eac:0">Memory Views</span></span></a><span data-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7"><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:0"> for more information.</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:1">`min`</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:3">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:5">\*\**</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:6">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:7">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:8">, </span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:9">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:10">\])</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:11">`min`</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:12">(</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:13">*arg1*</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:14">, </span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:15">*arg2*</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:16">, </span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:17">*\*args*</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:18">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:19">*key\*</span><span data-offset-key="7a1c87332ac34c42bc499a803170bde7:20">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="982a1bd1edae4e008d62b8afe071f8c6"><span data-offset-key="982a1bd1edae4e008d62b8afe071f8c6:0">Return the smallest item in an iterable or the smallest of two or more arguments.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f60c4711cbac44f1b5470530917d5b5c"><span data-offset-key="f60c4711cbac44f1b5470530917d5b5c:0">If one positional argument is provided, it should be an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-iterable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="15c3a0adcd1747e5ba53dcd08db770d3"><span data-offset-key="15c3a0adcd1747e5ba53dcd08db770d3:0">iterable</span></span></a><span data-key="618900b14a2a4770ac76349c1188d321"><span data-offset-key="618900b14a2a4770ac76349c1188d321:0">. The smallest item in the iterable is returned. If two or more positional arguments are provided, the smallest of the positional arguments is returned.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7a9ef9b2cb0942d2a10bfccd5e6a0a55"><span data-offset-key="7a9ef9b2cb0942d2a10bfccd5e6a0a55:0">There are two optional keyword-only arguments. The </span><span data-offset-key="7a9ef9b2cb0942d2a10bfccd5e6a0a55:1">_key_</span><span data-offset-key="7a9ef9b2cb0942d2a10bfccd5e6a0a55:2"> argument specifies a one-argument ordering function like that used for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list.sort" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ae65498ed5ed4eb78770b6d6ad88295c"><span data-offset-key="ae65498ed5ed4eb78770b6d6ad88295c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list.sort()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a8b4475a6ebf43789d930d6958bc0b2f"><span data-offset-key="a8b4475a6ebf43789d930d6958bc0b2f:0">. The </span><span data-offset-key="a8b4475a6ebf43789d930d6958bc0b2f:1">_default_</span><span data-offset-key="a8b4475a6ebf43789d930d6958bc0b2f:2"> argument specifies an object to return if the provided iterable is empty. If the iterable is empty and </span><span data-offset-key="a8b4475a6ebf43789d930d6958bc0b2f:3">_default_</span><span data-offset-key="a8b4475a6ebf43789d930d6958bc0b2f:4"> is not provided, a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ValueError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2e5fba194d664dc4ababec84bc35edf6"><span data-offset-key="2e5fba194d664dc4ababec84bc35edf6:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ValueError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="fe68a58d35d4450eb107ffd5db1ac611"><span data-offset-key="fe68a58d35d4450eb107ffd5db1ac611:0"> is raised.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d0796355de144fd687aecdda70a98bcf"><span data-offset-key="d0796355de144fd687aecdda70a98bcf:0">If multiple items are minimal, the function returns the first one encountered. This is consistent with other sort-stability preserving tools such as </span><span data-offset-key="d0796355de144fd687aecdda70a98bcf:1">`sorted(iterable, key=keyfunc)[0]`</span><span data-offset-key="d0796355de144fd687aecdda70a98bcf:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="d0796355de144fd687aecdda70a98bcf:3">`heapq.nsmallest(1, iterable, key=keyfunc)`</span><span data-offset-key="d0796355de144fd687aecdda70a98bcf:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e68d360b0e5a45f38a2600533f4d7da1"><span data-offset-key="e68d360b0e5a45f38a2600533f4d7da1:0">New in version 3.4: The </span><span data-offset-key="e68d360b0e5a45f38a2600533f4d7da1:1">_default_</span><span data-offset-key="e68d360b0e5a45f38a2600533f4d7da1:2"> keyword-only argument.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b74449449bc14613bb2371340be572b7"><span data-offset-key="b74449449bc14613bb2371340be572b7:0">Changed in version 3.8: The </span><span data-offset-key="b74449449bc14613bb2371340be572b7:1">_key_</span><span data-offset-key="b74449449bc14613bb2371340be572b7:2"> can be </span><span data-offset-key="b74449449bc14613bb2371340be572b7:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="b74449449bc14613bb2371340be572b7:4">.</span><span data-offset-key="b74449449bc14613bb2371340be572b7:5">`next`</span><span data-offset-key="b74449449bc14613bb2371340be572b7:6">(</span><span data-offset-key="b74449449bc14613bb2371340be572b7:7">_iterator_</span><span data-offset-key="b74449449bc14613bb2371340be572b7:8">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="b74449449bc14613bb2371340be572b7:9">_default_</span><span data-offset-key="b74449449bc14613bb2371340be572b7:10">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7368fc2e77524194abccebc1dbf074da"><span data-offset-key="7368fc2e77524194abccebc1dbf074da:0">Retrieve the next item from the </span><span data-offset-key="7368fc2e77524194abccebc1dbf074da:1">_iterator_</span><span data-offset-key="7368fc2e77524194abccebc1dbf074da:2"> by calling its </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#iterator.__next__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cc48bc79b6e046f7a1af6fb929105310"><span data-offset-key="cc48bc79b6e046f7a1af6fb929105310:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**next**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="725761f9769f47d09954d22c52450b4a"><span data-offset-key="725761f9769f47d09954d22c52450b4a:0"> method. <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cd94d10d0e61493f849a1bb4ebe4b306"><span data-offset-key="cd94d10d0e61493f849a1bb4ebe4b306:0">Return a new featureless object. </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9ef2c3327e784cfbb8b2bcdddea197fa"><span data-offset-key="9ef2c3327e784cfbb8b2bcdddea197fa:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">object</code></span></span></a><span data-key="66a53bff570c4bfdb5a5b7206bc58c34"><span data-offset-key="66a53bff570c4bfdb5a5b7206bc58c34:0"> is a base for all classes. It has the methods that are common to all instances of Python classes. This function does not accept any arguments.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="98b5e1853ed044618f204c58469c80b8"><span data-offset-key="98b5e1853ed044618f204c58469c80b8:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8552f819700c455ab49015fb3ccd787b"><span data-offset-key="8552f819700c455ab49015fb3ccd787b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="19da8e854bd14fa2ac88763176f4af59"><span data-offset-key="19da8e854bd14fa2ac88763176f4af59:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">object</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5dadc24d1329494ca911138120c7f0f0"><span data-offset-key="5dadc24d1329494ca911138120c7f0f0:0"> does </span><span data-offset-key="5dadc24d1329494ca911138120c7f0f0:1">_not_</span><span data-offset-key="5dadc24d1329494ca911138120c7f0f0:2"> have a </span></span><a data-key="da9899dd8c1a42dc96e5e9be72fec1c3"><span data-offset-key="da9899dd8c1a42dc96e5e9be72fec1c3:0">, so you can’t assign arbitrary attributes to an instance of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9452027ebf5e45d08e1817982f4656b3"><span data-key="fa7ccee6c8b84a018a78439b2f1e56b9"><span data-offset-key="fa7ccee6c8b84a018a78439b2f1e56b9:0"> class.</span><span data-offset-key="fa7ccee6c8b84a018a78439b2f1e56b9:1">`oct`</span><span <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e35802dceb6a48559701626608e0bf28"><span data-offset-key="e35802dceb6a48559701626608e0bf28:0">Convert an integer number to an octal string prefixed with “0o”. The result is a valid Python expression. If </span><span data-offset-key="e35802dceb6a48559701626608e0bf28:1">_x_</span><span data-offset-key="e35802dceb6a48559701626608e0bf28:2"> is not a Python </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b557910c899c4d4c97c1826df2b1be3f"><span data-offset-key="b557910c899c4d4c97c1826df2b1be3f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="dbefcc624c664e23ade55f85d6057c7d"><span data-offset-key="dbefcc624c664e23ade55f85d6057c7d:0"> object, it has to define an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4f622fad42fc4c2fae2491efe6e8dfaf"><span data-offset-key="4f622fad42fc4c2fae2491efe6e8dfaf:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**index**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d5093590fa7e4f3bb13da57c9895f1a7"><span data-offset-key="d5093590fa7e4f3bb13da57c9895f1a7:0"> method that returns an integer. For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> oct(8)'0o10'>>> oct(-56)'-0o70'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4e9f15576efe46bc85ffeec72c8a6f97"><span data-offset-key="4e9f15576efe46bc85ffeec72c8a6f97:0">If you want to convert an integer number to octal string either with prefix “0o” or not, you can use either of the following ways.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> '%#o' % 10, '%o' % 10('0o12', '12')>>> format(10, '#o'), format(10, 'o')('0o12', '12')>>> f'{10:#o}', f'{10:o}'('0o12', '12')

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="930a634a8e3d462eabb0f0762120bce9"><span data-offset-key="930a634a8e3d462eabb0f0762120bce9:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#format" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2f454521582545e3b5bd371add4c46ff"><span data-offset-key="2f454521582545e3b5bd371add4c46ff:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">format()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="99e9d15f5faf429181877251afaf2ee9"><span data-offset-key="99e9d15f5faf429181877251afaf2ee9:0"> for more information.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e91544d1bd0246c98df47fe30e7bdf81"><span data-offset-key="e91544d1bd0246c98df47fe30e7bdf81:0">&gt;</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe"><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:0">`open`</span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:2">_file_</span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:4">_mode='r'_</span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:5">, </span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:6">_buffering=-1_</span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:7">, </span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:8">_encoding=None_</span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:9">, </span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:10">_errors=None_</span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:11">, </span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:12">_newline=None_</span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:13">, </span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:14">_closefd=True_</span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:15">, </span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:16">_opener=None_</span><span data-offset-key="08706653234449eb81f38eaeded22ffe:17">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6b19b08cb7a04094b8d1b10ed8b6f1c0"><span data-offset-key="6b19b08cb7a04094b8d1b10ed8b6f1c0:0">Open </span><span data-offset-key="6b19b08cb7a04094b8d1b10ed8b6f1c0:1">_file_</span><span data-offset-key="6b19b08cb7a04094b8d1b10ed8b6f1c0:2"> and return a corresponding </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-file-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="252f997f5e744ac6b9156c3e0d3809b2"><span data-offset-key="252f997f5e744ac6b9156c3e0d3809b2:0">file object</span></span></a><span data-key="2ee62063cded43b197d4e156cd114fce"><span data-offset-key="2ee62063cded43b197d4e156cd114fce:0">. If the file cannot be opened, an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#OSError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="578e4e8d3ffc4a86af7d198b34770814"><span data-offset-key="578e4e8d3ffc4a86af7d198b34770814:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">OSError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9a248fb514984b67b47b83fed1bd3a99"><span data-offset-key="9a248fb514984b67b47b83fed1bd3a99:0"> is raised. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/tutorial/inputoutput.html#tut-files" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fbcef029f6634a4086de0a1671cfb2ff"><span data-offset-key="fbcef029f6634a4086de0a1671cfb2ff:0">Reading and Writing Files</span></span></a><span data-key="a0c3c08b590d4fccbb80408b4ac87ba0"><span data-offset-key="a0c3c08b590d4fccbb80408b4ac87ba0:0"> for more examples of how to use this function.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="639106a0bea94b91805379f47cb50394"><span data-offset-key="639106a0bea94b91805379f47cb50394:0">_file_</span><span data-offset-key="639106a0bea94b91805379f47cb50394:1"> is a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d1d2d591131c494d89b93b4844205c65"><span data-offset-key="d1d2d591131c494d89b93b4844205c65:0">path-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="452fc6c9984a42eba0214228cbac693c"><span data-offset-key="452fc6c9984a42eba0214228cbac693c:0"> giving the pathname (absolute or relative to the current working directory) of the file to be opened or an integer file descriptor of the file to be wrapped. (If a file descriptor is given, it is closed when the returned I/O object is closed, unless </span><span data-offset-key="452fc6c9984a42eba0214228cbac693c:1">_closefd_</span><span data-offset-key="452fc6c9984a42eba0214228cbac693c:2"> is set to </span><span data-offset-key="452fc6c9984a42eba0214228cbac693c:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="452fc6c9984a42eba0214228cbac693c:4">.)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545"><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:0">_mode_</span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:1"> is an optional string that specifies the mode in which the file is opened. It defaults to </span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:2">`'r'`</span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:3"> which means open for reading in text mode. Other common values are </span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:4">`'w'`</span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:5"> for writing (truncating the file if it already exists), </span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:6">`'x'`</span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:7"> for exclusive creation and </span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:8">`'a'`</span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:9"> for appending (which on </span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:10">_some_</span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:11"> Unix systems, means that </span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:12">_all_</span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:13"> writes append to the end of the file regardless of the current seek position). In text mode, if </span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:14">_encoding_</span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:15"> is not specified the encoding used is platform dependent: </span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:16">`locale.getpreferredencoding(False)`</span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:17"> is called to get the current locale encoding. (For reading and writing raw bytes use binary mode and leave </span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:18">_encoding_</span><span data-offset-key="99ad2652a4964b8ca2b934d94cb97545:19"> unspecified.) The available modes are:</span></span></span>

<table><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><tbody><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span for exclusive creation, failing if the file already exists</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span appending to the end of the file if it exists</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="even"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span mode</span></span></span></p></td></tr><tr class="odd"><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-slate-leaf="true">'t'</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span
