class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">'+'</code></span></span></span></p></td><td style="text-align: left;"><p><span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0aaaff7853554b449fb52a9ae71c6f2d"><span data-offset-key="0aaaff7853554b449fb52a9ae71c6f2d:0">open for updating (reading and writing)</span></span></span></p></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78"><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:0">The default mode is </span><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:1">`'r'`</span><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:2"> (open for reading text, synonym of </span><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:3">`'rt'`</span><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:4">). Modes </span><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:5">`'w+'`</span><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:6"> and </span><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:7">`'w+b'`</span><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:8"> open and truncate the file. Modes </span><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:9">`'r+'`</span><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:10"> and </span><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:11">`'r+b'`</span><span data-offset-key="4b33d22676bf4598a260fcf2934eea78:12"> open the file with no truncation.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a35d693ec1284f72b0374110497a9928"><span data-offset-key="a35d693ec1284f72b0374110497a9928:0">As mentioned in the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io-overview" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9a433e9b392340a2a3dac087b38d4fda"><span data-offset-key="9a433e9b392340a2a3dac087b38d4fda:0">Overview</span></span></a><span data-key="1a5791600f834a44abb9de1d8ff4d2fc"><span data-offset-key="1a5791600f834a44abb9de1d8ff4d2fc:0">, Python distinguishes between binary and text I/O. Files opened in binary mode (including </span><span data-offset-key="1a5791600f834a44abb9de1d8ff4d2fc:1">`'b'`</span><span data-offset-key="1a5791600f834a44abb9de1d8ff4d2fc:2"> in the </span><span data-offset-key="1a5791600f834a44abb9de1d8ff4d2fc:3">_mode_</span><span data-offset-key="1a5791600f834a44abb9de1d8ff4d2fc:4"> argument) return contents as </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="899e6307f5da4bf995c19d40bede86b0"><span data-offset-key="899e6307f5da4bf995c19d40bede86b0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3e93ce50f0fe4e11a6dff9fce0726d10"><span data-offset-key="3e93ce50f0fe4e11a6dff9fce0726d10:0"> objects without any decoding. In text mode (the default, or when </span><span data-offset-key="3e93ce50f0fe4e11a6dff9fce0726d10:1">`'t'`</span><span data-offset-key="3e93ce50f0fe4e11a6dff9fce0726d10:2"> is included in the </span><span data-offset-key="3e93ce50f0fe4e11a6dff9fce0726d10:3">_mode_</span><span data-offset-key="3e93ce50f0fe4e11a6dff9fce0726d10:4"> argument), the contents of the file are returned as </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="00ff5a0fb89c44ac993c475e0f7bdb43"><span data-offset-key="00ff5a0fb89c44ac993c475e0f7bdb43:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c7254370bc0944a8a33dec450c8ac20a"><span data-offset-key="c7254370bc0944a8a33dec450c8ac20a:0">, the bytes having been first decoded using a platform-dependent encoding or using the specified </span><span data-offset-key="c7254370bc0944a8a33dec450c8ac20a:1">_encoding_</span><span data-offset-key="c7254370bc0944a8a33dec450c8ac20a:2"> if given.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="56e3287affef484fa00cc68d45ad9613"><span data-offset-key="56e3287affef484fa00cc68d45ad9613:0">There is an additional mode character permitted, </span><span data-offset-key="56e3287affef484fa00cc68d45ad9613:1">`'U'`</span><span data-offset-key="56e3287affef484fa00cc68d45ad9613:2">, which no longer has any effect, and is considered deprecated. It previously enabled </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-universal-newlines" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="114bdb4a4bbb48d993aec62ae609caca"><span data-offset-key="114bdb4a4bbb48d993aec62ae609caca:0">universal newlines</span></span></a><span data-key="2fc192a4746c41b292abd3cebcea4e83"><span data-offset-key="2fc192a4746c41b292abd3cebcea4e83:0"> in text mode, which became the default behaviour in Python 3.0. Refer to the documentation of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#open-newline-parameter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="50a9ebec0c4e4b37af2297b7717fbbcc"><span data-offset-key="50a9ebec0c4e4b37af2297b7717fbbcc:0">newline</span></span></a><span data-key="ba5d4e489f1e47389b7d6c5ebfe0f3dc"><span data-offset-key="ba5d4e489f1e47389b7d6c5ebfe0f3dc:0"> parameter for further details.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b3b45e79dd6b45bc89e235974075f804"><span data-offset-key="b3b45e79dd6b45bc89e235974075f804:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e67749443e30466ab8cbaf3a2a2968a8"><span data-offset-key="e67749443e30466ab8cbaf3a2a2968a8:0">Python doesn’t depend on the underlying operating system’s notion of text files; all the processing is done by Python itself, and is therefore platform-independent.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1a6e49ddfc3a4bd59cd49db0801c4e13"><span data-offset-key="1a6e49ddfc3a4bd59cd49db0801c4e13:0">_buffering_</span><span data-offset-key="1a6e49ddfc3a4bd59cd49db0801c4e13:1"> is an optional integer used to set the buffering policy. Pass 0 to switch buffering off (only allowed in binary mode), 1 to select line buffering (only usable in text mode), and an integer &gt; 1 to indicate the size in bytes of a fixed-size chunk buffer. When no </span><span data-offset-key="1a6e49ddfc3a4bd59cd49db0801c4e13:2">_buffering_</span><span data-offset-key="1a6e49ddfc3a4bd59cd49db0801c4e13:3"> argument is given, the default buffering policy works as follows:</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="43cc6c49fd7a443288bdcf66554e8934"><span data-offset-key="43cc6c49fd7a443288bdcf66554e8934:0">Binary files are buffered in fixed-size chunks; the size of the buffer is chosen using a heuristic trying to determine the underlying device’s “block size” and falling back on </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.DEFAULT_BUFFER_SIZE" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7507b114a7a64c1fa989a4ae16afa3fa"><span data-offset-key="7507b114a7a64c1fa989a4ae16afa3fa:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.DEFAULT_BUFFER_SIZE</code></span></span></a><span data-key="cb0196cd49934684b3e08deb39c17942"><span data-offset-key="cb0196cd49934684b3e08deb39c17942:0">. On many systems, the buffer will typically be 4096 or 8192 bytes long.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a5d058cdb71b4f62a9e1efce268641e4"><span data-offset-key="a5d058cdb71b4f62a9e1efce268641e4:0">“Interactive” text files (files for which </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.IOBase.isatty" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="87505bab8e7d410e9a9e91719cc39bba"><span data-offset-key="87505bab8e7d410e9a9e91719cc39bba:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">isatty()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f70824095cbf4003bdaef4c531c44ef5"><span data-offset-key="f70824095cbf4003bdaef4c531c44ef5:0"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="f70824095cbf4003bdaef4c531c44ef5:1">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="f70824095cbf4003bdaef4c531c44ef5:2">) use line buffering. Other text files use the policy described above for binary files.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="33ff1e9b48da4502b4535dfc72591974"><span data-offset-key="33ff1e9b48da4502b4535dfc72591974:0">_encoding_</span><span data-offset-key="33ff1e9b48da4502b4535dfc72591974:1"> is the name of the encoding used to decode or encode the file. This should only be used in text mode. The default encoding is platform dependent (whatever </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/locale.html#locale.getpreferredencoding" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="daa0c846d9e94d2b8779f8becc7fed08"><span data-offset-key="daa0c846d9e94d2b8779f8becc7fed08:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">locale.getpreferredencoding()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d1bc7adb6d8c443d9a576356647bb87b"><span data-offset-key="d1bc7adb6d8c443d9a576356647bb87b:0"> returns), but any </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-text-encoding" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1b639d4cdb64447b8243976ddc72236e"><span data-offset-key="1b639d4cdb64447b8243976ddc72236e:0">text encoding</span></span></a><span data-key="c971013b8a374bea8badb10bdf062b9b"><span data-offset-key="c971013b8a374bea8badb10bdf062b9b:0"> supported by Python can be used. See the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/codecs.html#module-codecs" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="33850ae0d533430eb611ab2da34aa997"><span data-offset-key="33850ae0d533430eb611ab2da34aa997:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">codecs</code></span></span></a><span data-key="07a575230cf748c7a7eb55176a600de9"><span data-offset-key="07a575230cf748c7a7eb55176a600de9:0"> module for the list of supported encodings.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="63c4c958ef034231bf463e335f4d4cd6"><span data-offset-key="63c4c958ef034231bf463e335f4d4cd6:0">_errors_</span><span data-offset-key="63c4c958ef034231bf463e335f4d4cd6:1"> is an optional string that specifies how encoding and decoding errors are to be handled—this cannot be used in binary mode. A variety of standard error handlers are available (listed under </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/codecs.html#error-handlers" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2bccc608c83343a9ad7f427f998d8044"><span data-offset-key="2bccc608c83343a9ad7f427f998d8044:0">Error Handlers</span></span></a><span data-key="8dcf9118f0f94aecb3a91ff415a7764d"><span data-offset-key="8dcf9118f0f94aecb3a91ff415a7764d:0">), though any error handling name that has been registered with </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/codecs.html#codecs.register_error" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0d369d3b305744e78277363a3c65d306"><span data-offset-key="0d369d3b305744e78277363a3c65d306:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">codecs.register_error()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6c2224158a0248728f2a9a95bf2388a5"><span data-offset-key="6c2224158a0248728f2a9a95bf2388a5:0"> is also valid. The standard names include:</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="71206d6eed914a058fd6ab4123da145c"><span data-offset-key="71206d6eed914a058fd6ab4123da145c:0">`'strict'`</span><span data-offset-key="71206d6eed914a058fd6ab4123da145c:1"> to raise a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ValueError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d1158b52c54e4ed5a4659b32594e384e"><span data-offset-key="d1158b52c54e4ed5a4659b32594e384e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ValueError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1cd9f14a47074d379160c1c61257fc80"><span data-offset-key="1cd9f14a47074d379160c1c61257fc80:0"> exception if there is an encoding error. The default value of </span><span data-offset-key="1cd9f14a47074d379160c1c61257fc80:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="1cd9f14a47074d379160c1c61257fc80:2"> has the same effect.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1fc7b70388d64dc3825ef728fcf24619"><span data-offset-key="1fc7b70388d64dc3825ef728fcf24619:0">`'ignore'`</span><span data-offset-key="1fc7b70388d64dc3825ef728fcf24619:1"> ignores errors. Note that ignoring encoding errors can lead to data loss.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e0766242ecc94445b0b8d43acc95e034"><span data-offset-key="e0766242ecc94445b0b8d43acc95e034:0">`'replace'`</span><span data-offset-key="e0766242ecc94445b0b8d43acc95e034:1"> causes a replacement marker (such as </span><span data-offset-key="e0766242ecc94445b0b8d43acc95e034:2">`'?'`</span><span data-offset-key="e0766242ecc94445b0b8d43acc95e034:3">) to be inserted where there is malformed data.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6c6b92bea6a849059f9e31d4d507f5dc"><span data-offset-key="6c6b92bea6a849059f9e31d4d507f5dc:0">`'surrogateescape'`</span><span data-offset-key="6c6b92bea6a849059f9e31d4d507f5dc:1"> will represent any incorrect bytes as low surrogate code units ranging from U+DC80 to U+DCFF. These surrogate code units will then be turned back into the same bytes when the </span><span data-offset-key="6c6b92bea6a849059f9e31d4d507f5dc:2">`surrogateescape`</span><span data-offset-key="6c6b92bea6a849059f9e31d4d507f5dc:3"> error handler is used when writing data. This is useful for processing files in an unknown encoding.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="390b6a5dcb4c4e23a9a2210359b3e59f"><span data-offset-key="390b6a5dcb4c4e23a9a2210359b3e59f:0">`'xmlcharrefreplace'`</span><span data-offset-key="390b6a5dcb4c4e23a9a2210359b3e59f:1"> is only supported when writing to a file. Characters not supported by the encoding are replaced with the appropriate XML character reference </span><span data-offset-key="390b6a5dcb4c4e23a9a2210359b3e59f:2">`&#nnn;`</span><span data-offset-key="390b6a5dcb4c4e23a9a2210359b3e59f:3">.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="91ebc4ae1dcf4fce9111b6ece9dfa1f2"><span data-offset-key="91ebc4ae1dcf4fce9111b6ece9dfa1f2:0">`'backslashreplace'`</span><span data-offset-key="91ebc4ae1dcf4fce9111b6ece9dfa1f2:1"> replaces malformed data by Python’s backslashed escape sequences.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="594e105c776e442586f646b4923e7740"><span data-offset-key="594e105c776e442586f646b4923e7740:0">`'namereplace'`</span><span data-offset-key="594e105c776e442586f646b4923e7740:1"> (also only supported when writing) replaces unsupported characters with </span><span data-offset-key="594e105c776e442586f646b4923e7740:2">`\N{...}`</span><span data-offset-key="594e105c776e442586f646b4923e7740:3"> escape sequences.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="48b67ea17a5d4f5687734e2e0a2f687d"><span data-offset-key="48b67ea17a5d4f5687734e2e0a2f687d:0">_newline_</span><span data-offset-key="48b67ea17a5d4f5687734e2e0a2f687d:1"> controls how </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-universal-newlines" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="343990951ddb4278be474978a5aeae4e"><span data-offset-key="343990951ddb4278be474978a5aeae4e:0">universal newlines</span></span></a><span data-key="91030ce57acc4ff3a96e3b2dd27df06e"><span data-offset-key="91030ce57acc4ff3a96e3b2dd27df06e:0"> mode works (it only applies to text mode). It can be </span><span data-offset-key="91030ce57acc4ff3a96e3b2dd27df06e:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="91030ce57acc4ff3a96e3b2dd27df06e:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="91030ce57acc4ff3a96e3b2dd27df06e:3">`''`</span><span data-offset-key="91030ce57acc4ff3a96e3b2dd27df06e:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="91030ce57acc4ff3a96e3b2dd27df06e:5">`'\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="91030ce57acc4ff3a96e3b2dd27df06e:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="91030ce57acc4ff3a96e3b2dd27df06e:7">`'\r'`</span><span data-offset-key="91030ce57acc4ff3a96e3b2dd27df06e:8">, and </span><span data-offset-key="91030ce57acc4ff3a96e3b2dd27df06e:9">`'\r\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="91030ce57acc4ff3a96e3b2dd27df06e:10">. It works as follows:</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1"><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:0">When reading input from the stream, if </span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:1">_newline_</span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:2"> is </span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:4">, universal newlines mode is enabled. Lines in the input can end in </span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:5">`'\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:7">`'\r'`</span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:8">, or </span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:9">`'\r\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:10">, and these are translated into </span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:11">`'\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:12"> before being returned to the caller. If it is </span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:13">`''`</span><span data-offset-key="e76c85a2e0c94a5b885063dd076347d1:14">, universal newlines mode is enabled, but line endings are returned to the caller untranslated. If it has any of the other legal values, input lines are only terminated by the given string, and the line ending is returned to the caller untranslated.</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="68d04857006b4e3580e06ea638d001d1"><span data-offset-key="68d04857006b4e3580e06ea638d001d1:0">When writing output to the stream, if </span><span data-offset-key="68d04857006b4e3580e06ea638d001d1:1">_newline_</span><span data-offset-key="68d04857006b4e3580e06ea638d001d1:2"> is </span><span data-offset-key="68d04857006b4e3580e06ea638d001d1:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="68d04857006b4e3580e06ea638d001d1:4">, any </span><span data-offset-key="68d04857006b4e3580e06ea638d001d1:5">`'\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="68d04857006b4e3580e06ea638d001d1:6"> characters written are translated to the system default line separator, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.linesep" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8697d7a7f5304115bf0288ccb7487e16"><span data-offset-key="8697d7a7f5304115bf0288ccb7487e16:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">os.linesep</code></span></span></a><span data-key="901aa4d3ecae4d7dba76c1959b5b3bb1"><span data-offset-key="901aa4d3ecae4d7dba76c1959b5b3bb1:0">. If </span><span data-offset-key="901aa4d3ecae4d7dba76c1959b5b3bb1:1">_newline_</span><span data-offset-key="901aa4d3ecae4d7dba76c1959b5b3bb1:2"> is </span><span data-offset-key="901aa4d3ecae4d7dba76c1959b5b3bb1:3">`''`</span><span data-offset-key="901aa4d3ecae4d7dba76c1959b5b3bb1:4"> or </span><span data-offset-key="901aa4d3ecae4d7dba76c1959b5b3bb1:5">`'\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="901aa4d3ecae4d7dba76c1959b5b3bb1:6">, no translation takes place. If </span><span data-offset-key="901aa4d3ecae4d7dba76c1959b5b3bb1:7">_newline_</span><span data-offset-key="901aa4d3ecae4d7dba76c1959b5b3bb1:8"> is any of the other legal values, any </span><span data-offset-key="901aa4d3ecae4d7dba76c1959b5b3bb1:9">`'\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="901aa4d3ecae4d7dba76c1959b5b3bb1:10"> characters written are translated to the given string.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4ab06770002a4f8a82182169d567e2fb"><span data-offset-key="4ab06770002a4f8a82182169d567e2fb:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="4ab06770002a4f8a82182169d567e2fb:1">_closefd_</span><span data-offset-key="4ab06770002a4f8a82182169d567e2fb:2"> is </span><span data-offset-key="4ab06770002a4f8a82182169d567e2fb:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="4ab06770002a4f8a82182169d567e2fb:4"> and a file descriptor rather than a filename was given, the underlying file descriptor will be kept open when the file is closed. If a filename is given </span><span data-offset-key="4ab06770002a4f8a82182169d567e2fb:5">_closefd_</span><span data-offset-key="4ab06770002a4f8a82182169d567e2fb:6"> must be </span><span data-offset-key="4ab06770002a4f8a82182169d567e2fb:7">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="4ab06770002a4f8a82182169d567e2fb:8"> (the default) otherwise an error will be raised.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8387f8403903482a8855ac9cef03286a"><span data-offset-key="8387f8403903482a8855ac9cef03286a:0">A custom opener can be used by passing a callable as </span><span data-offset-key="8387f8403903482a8855ac9cef03286a:1">_opener_</span><span data-offset-key="8387f8403903482a8855ac9cef03286a:2">. The underlying file descriptor for the file object is then obtained by calling </span><span data-offset-key="8387f8403903482a8855ac9cef03286a:3">_opener_</span><span data-offset-key="8387f8403903482a8855ac9cef03286a:4"> with (</span><span data-offset-key="8387f8403903482a8855ac9cef03286a:5">_file_</span><span data-offset-key="8387f8403903482a8855ac9cef03286a:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="8387f8403903482a8855ac9cef03286a:7">_flags_</span><span data-offset-key="8387f8403903482a8855ac9cef03286a:8">). </span><span data-offset-key="8387f8403903482a8855ac9cef03286a:9">_opener_</span><span data-offset-key="8387f8403903482a8855ac9cef03286a:10"> must return an open file descriptor (passing </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.open" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="733448612d1e4b5282ed869dc3a041a3"><span data-offset-key="733448612d1e4b5282ed869dc3a041a3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">os.open</code></span></span></a><span data-key="982f56270a4d45ecb676195198579ea1"><span data-offset-key="982f56270a4d45ecb676195198579ea1:0"> as </span><span data-offset-key="982f56270a4d45ecb676195198579ea1:1">_opener_</span><span data-offset-key="982f56270a4d45ecb676195198579ea1:2"> results in functionality similar to passing </span><span data-offset-key="982f56270a4d45ecb676195198579ea1:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="982f56270a4d45ecb676195198579ea1:4">).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="370c374d26314a2686a6baaf9c858c69"><span data-offset-key="370c374d26314a2686a6baaf9c858c69:0">The newly created file is </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#fd-inheritance" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5c2130cbf9944bce9791036ce54292f9"><span data-offset-key="5c2130cbf9944bce9791036ce54292f9:0">non-inheritable</span></span></a><span data-key="7dac4bc237284f45b8dd01cd9f0a35b1"><span data-offset-key="7dac4bc237284f45b8dd01cd9f0a35b1:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="78a417401f5240ebbde0d86a6ecc2657"><span data-offset-key="78a417401f5240ebbde0d86a6ecc2657:0">The following example uses the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#dir-fd" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5112eca5135147969119243752517478"><span data-offset-key="5112eca5135147969119243752517478:0">dir_fd</span></span></a><span data-key="4749890a39934145a0e63e8502d6f34b"><span data-offset-key="4749890a39934145a0e63e8502d6f34b:0"> parameter of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.open" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e5f91f3841a346418e0b5a1bbb949255"><span data-offset-key="e5f91f3841a346418e0b5a1bbb949255:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">os.open()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f6f3cd083554405a96fca76ca116e97a"><span data-offset-key="f6f3cd083554405a96fca76ca116e97a:0"> function to open a file relative to a given directory:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> import os>>> dir_fd = os.open('somedir', os.O_RDONLY)>>> def opener(path, flags):...     return os.open(path, flags, dir_fd=dir_fd)...>>> with open('spamspam.txt', 'w', opener=opener) as f:...     print('This will be written to somedir/spamspam.txt', file=f)...>>> os.close(dir_fd)  # don't leak a file descriptor

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="77228f7febd84f6fa4e5691605eb8a9e"><span data-offset-key="77228f7febd84f6fa4e5691605eb8a9e:0">The type of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-file-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="19c3079721cd480da3b20bc1b79d9528"><span data-offset-key="19c3079721cd480da3b20bc1b79d9528:0">file object</span></span></a><span data-key="e7f502181978477a8d52e47b24503dae"><span data-offset-key="e7f502181978477a8d52e47b24503dae:0"> returned by the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#open" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7cb9d54027be422d931a862e4066aa15"><span data-offset-key="7cb9d54027be422d931a862e4066aa15:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">open()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d94a4f0100b0410991f18f4ecc624ff7"><span data-offset-key="d94a4f0100b0410991f18f4ecc624ff7:0"> function depends on the mode. When </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#open" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="86cda3f60bc145bd8161d4505aadd140"><span data-offset-key="86cda3f60bc145bd8161d4505aadd140:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">open()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e23c4139f4a44da9945e196bfab0eb8d"><span data-offset-key="e23c4139f4a44da9945e196bfab0eb8d:0"> is used to open a file in a text mode (</span><span data-offset-key="e23c4139f4a44da9945e196bfab0eb8d:1">`'w'`</span><span data-offset-key="e23c4139f4a44da9945e196bfab0eb8d:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="e23c4139f4a44da9945e196bfab0eb8d:3">`'r'`</span><span data-offset-key="e23c4139f4a44da9945e196bfab0eb8d:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="e23c4139f4a44da9945e196bfab0eb8d:5">`'wt'`</span><span data-offset-key="e23c4139f4a44da9945e196bfab0eb8d:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="e23c4139f4a44da9945e196bfab0eb8d:7">`'rt'`</span><span data-offset-key="e23c4139f4a44da9945e196bfab0eb8d:8">, etc.), it returns a subclass of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.TextIOBase" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7ff3f1b9353d41a79e6f24b9890ff91f"><span data-offset-key="7ff3f1b9353d41a79e6f24b9890ff91f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.TextIOBase</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0884b295377b4b148636bc7b8b696764"><span data-offset-key="0884b295377b4b148636bc7b8b696764:0"> (specifically </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.TextIOWrapper" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c9bab83928b94f1a91c65e02f99ac3b9"><span data-offset-key="c9bab83928b94f1a91c65e02f99ac3b9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.TextIOWrapper</code></span></span></a><span data-key="07bad128625c48a2a061d1183029666e"><span data-offset-key="07bad128625c48a2a061d1183029666e:0">). When used to open a file in a binary mode with buffering, the returned class is a subclass of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.BufferedIOBase" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="38c8974b02794ca28889ea6c7a781778"><span data-offset-key="38c8974b02794ca28889ea6c7a781778:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.BufferedIOBase</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0670f47512d84078a7fb97e3e8793e77"><span data-offset-key="0670f47512d84078a7fb97e3e8793e77:0">. The exact class varies: in read binary mode, it returns an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.BufferedReader" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f79ea2a1950d4142bde0c3e2d26c841d"><span data-offset-key="f79ea2a1950d4142bde0c3e2d26c841d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.BufferedReader</code></span></span></a><span data-key="45e734cb4a074088a9da78e0172db88a"><span data-offset-key="45e734cb4a074088a9da78e0172db88a:0">; in write binary and append binary modes, it returns an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.BufferedWriter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f540aac1e6604480a831ce4133f44b29"><span data-offset-key="f540aac1e6604480a831ce4133f44b29:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.BufferedWriter</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c02ba9ad77fd4d638c47e9b6e47a5104"><span data-offset-key="c02ba9ad77fd4d638c47e9b6e47a5104:0">, and in read/write mode, it returns an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.BufferedRandom" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4d9997ab542643b8af2b6bc8fce0ec74"><span data-offset-key="4d9997ab542643b8af2b6bc8fce0ec74:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.BufferedRandom</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0f0a9486c27443c39a71f883907a11b1"><span data-offset-key="0f0a9486c27443c39a71f883907a11b1:0">. When buffering is disabled, the raw stream, a subclass of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.RawIOBase" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8d753ad666674b60b218a369ebbfe4f8"><span data-offset-key="8d753ad666674b60b218a369ebbfe4f8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.RawIOBase</code></span></span></a><span data-key="149699c2c0c34c459e247915c376ab83"><span data-offset-key="149699c2c0c34c459e247915c376ab83:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.FileIO" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3855a979bb554931ba4269fd034f42ab"><span data-offset-key="3855a979bb554931ba4269fd034f42ab:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.FileIO</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9204117031e949899f52a4273b04276d"><span data-offset-key="9204117031e949899f52a4273b04276d:0">, is returned.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="91acb07eef8e4c579272cc7a1c3197ca"><span data-offset-key="91acb07eef8e4c579272cc7a1c3197ca:0">See also the > <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c9b635bb82f8433698dffdacf1b997da"><span data-offset-key="c9b635bb82f8433698dffdacf1b997da:0">Changed in version 3.6:</span></span></span>

> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dd3d3459b2eb415d911ff437dad5fc93"><span data-offset-key="dd3d3459b2eb415d911ff437dad5fc93:0">Support added to accept objects implementing </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.PathLike" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d6ce41f5a6844d09998865327034ed2b"><span data-offset-key="d6ce41f5a6844d09998865327034ed2b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">os.PathLike</code></span></span></a><span data-key="fd0c9529117c435dbfadcd376be06412"><span data-offset-key="fd0c9529117c435dbfadcd376be06412:0">.</span></span></span>

> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="66ceb137f82145a9b1b1421570b4d28c"><span data-offset-key="66ceb137f82145a9b1b1421570b4d28c:0">On Windows, opening a console buffer may return a subclass of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.RawIOBase" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f08e03021f7445989bf9f82528fbd3b5"><span data-offset-key="f08e03021f7445989bf9f82528fbd3b5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.RawIOBase</code></span></span></a><span data-key="41e5279d36b148ce8c5623cfd324a40d"><span data-offset-key="41e5279d36b148ce8c5623cfd324a40d:0"> other than </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.FileIO" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a060920dd04b4d81abc719e5c76585b5"><span data-offset-key="a060920dd04b4d81abc719e5c76585b5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.FileIO</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a29496a232bc44b19bd61b88876d209d"><span data-offset-key="a29496a232bc44b19bd61b88876d209d:0">.</span></span></span>
>
> <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f570951641eb421ead8e7edde79a8ae3"><span data-offset-key="f570951641eb421ead8e7edde79a8ae3:0">`ord`</span><span data-offset-key="f570951641eb421ead8e7edde79a8ae3:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="f570951641eb421ead8e7edde79a8ae3:2">_c_</span><span data-offset-key="f570951641eb421ead8e7edde79a8ae3:3">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6f7b810a7a2741a29a5c298fb72b30a1"><span data-offset-key="6f7b810a7a2741a29a5c298fb72b30a1:0">Given a string representing one Unicode character, return an integer representing the Unicode code point of that character. For example, </span><span data-offset-key="6f7b810a7a2741a29a5c298fb72b30a1:1">`ord('a')`</span><span data-offset-key="6f7b810a7a2741a29a5c298fb72b30a1:2"> returns the integer </span><span data-offset-key="6f7b810a7a2741a29a5c298fb72b30a1:3">`97`</span><span data-offset-key="6f7b810a7a2741a29a5c298fb72b30a1:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="6f7b810a7a2741a29a5c298fb72b30a1:5">`ord('€')`</span><span data-offset-key="6f7b810a7a2741a29a5c298fb72b30a1:6"> (Euro sign) returns </span><span data-offset-key="6f7b810a7a2741a29a5c298fb72b30a1:7">`8364`</span><span data-offset-key="6f7b810a7a2741a29a5c298fb72b30a1:8">. This is the inverse of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#chr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bd33a94c88b24a0da2af350062fb91f1"><span data-offset-key="bd33a94c88b24a0da2af350062fb91f1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">chr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a0a501f5d4ad40c39f7ab4e56ec6e30f"><span data-offset-key="a0a501f5d4ad40c39f7ab4e56ec6e30f:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="a0a501f5d4ad40c39f7ab4e56ec6e30f:1">`pow`</span><span data-offset-key="a0a501f5d4ad40c39f7ab4e56ec6e30f:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="a0a501f5d4ad40c39f7ab4e56ec6e30f:3">_base_</span><span data-offset-key="a0a501f5d4ad40c39f7ab4e56ec6e30f:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="a0a501f5d4ad40c39f7ab4e56ec6e30f:5">_exp_</span><span data-offset-key="a0a501f5d4ad40c39f7ab4e56ec6e30f:6">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="a0a501f5d4ad40c39f7ab4e56ec6e30f:7">_mod_</span><span data-offset-key="a0a501f5d4ad40c39f7ab4e56ec6e30f:8">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758"><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:1">_base_</span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:2"> to the power </span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:3">_exp_</span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:4">; if </span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:5">_mod_</span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:6"> is present, return </span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:7">_base_</span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:8"> to the power </span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:9">_exp_</span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:10">, modulo </span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:11">_mod_</span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:12"> (computed more efficiently than </span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:13">`pow(base, exp) % mod`</span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:14">). The two-argument form </span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:15">`pow(base, exp)`</span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:16"> is equivalent to using the power operator: </span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:17">`base**exp`</span><span data-offset-key="fe75ed1e09994af0bf1a1d67bc1b9758:18">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d2d2aa01f5984ebba2a074f755658706"><span data-offset-key="d2d2aa01f5984ebba2a074f755658706:0">The arguments must have numeric types. With mixed operand types, the coercion rules for binary arithmetic operators apply. For </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c2783d5de1cf4e9bbb6e2e2707e0274d"><span data-offset-key="c2783d5de1cf4e9bbb6e2e2707e0274d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b245b156546746f69f2ed4ab8c5b7e04"><span data-offset-key="b245b156546746f69f2ed4ab8c5b7e04:0"> operands, the result has the same type as the operands (after coercion) unless the second argument is negative; in that case, all arguments are converted to float and a float result is delivered. For example, </span><span data-offset-key="b245b156546746f69f2ed4ab8c5b7e04:1">`10**2`</span><span data-offset-key="b245b156546746f69f2ed4ab8c5b7e04:2"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="b245b156546746f69f2ed4ab8c5b7e04:3">`100`</span><span data-offset-key="b245b156546746f69f2ed4ab8c5b7e04:4">, but </span><span data-offset-key="b245b156546746f69f2ed4ab8c5b7e04:5">`10**-2`</span><span data-offset-key="b245b156546746f69f2ed4ab8c5b7e04:6"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="b245b156546746f69f2ed4ab8c5b7e04:7">`0.01`</span><span data-offset-key="b245b156546746f69f2ed4ab8c5b7e04:8">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a55bb1ff6cf64049ab8b6b3002ac3cf3"><span data-offset-key="a55bb1ff6cf64049ab8b6b3002ac3cf3:0">For </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="22f39cafe6404ac99b2b2c823573b668"><span data-offset-key="22f39cafe6404ac99b2b2c823573b668:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b"><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:0"> operands </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:1">_base_</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:3">_exp_</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:4">, if </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:5">_mod_</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:6"> is present, </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:7">_mod_</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:8"> must also be of integer type and </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:9">_mod_</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:10"> must be nonzero. If </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:11">_mod_</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:12"> is present and </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:13">_exp_</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:14"> is negative, </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:15">_base_</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:16"> must be relatively prime to </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:17">_mod_</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:18">. In that case, </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:19">`pow(inv_base, -exp, mod)`</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:20"> is returned, where </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:21">_inv_base_</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:22"> is an inverse to </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:23">_base_</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:24"> modulo </span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:25">_mod_</span><span data-offset-key="659b8d8851d9476aa99617123ce6331b:26">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7cba71075d144134b7272025e97c5a56"><span data-offset-key="7cba71075d144134b7272025e97c5a56:0">Here’s an example of computing an inverse for </span><span data-offset-key="7cba71075d144134b7272025e97c5a56:1">`38`</span><span data-offset-key="7cba71075d144134b7272025e97c5a56:2"> modulo </span><span data-offset-key="7cba71075d144134b7272025e97c5a56:3">`97`</span><span data-offset-key="7cba71075d144134b7272025e97c5a56:4">:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> pow(38, -1, mod=97)23>>> 23 * 38 % 97 == 1True

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8d6c50d714f64826ada724d95e1f4c8c"><span data-offset-key="8d6c50d714f64826ada724d95e1f4c8c:0">Changed in version 3.8: For </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ae349eb85c714cb9aabca537b9cb5765"><span data-offset-key="ae349eb85c714cb9aabca537b9cb5765:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="635353134d184e3bbb4435affddb68ae"><span data-offset-key="635353134d184e3bbb4435affddb68ae:0"> operands, the three-argument form of </span><span data-offset-key="635353134d184e3bbb4435affddb68ae:1">`pow`</span><span data-offset-key="635353134d184e3bbb4435affddb68ae:2"> now allows the second argument to be negative, permitting computation of modular inverses.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80"><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:0">Changed in version 3.8: Allow keyword arguments. Formerly, only positional arguments were supported.</span><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:1">`print`</span><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:3">_\*objects_</span><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:5">_sep=' '_</span><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:7">_end='\\n'_</span><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:8">, </span><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:9">_file=sys.stdout_</span><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:10">, </span><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:11">_flush=False_</span><span data-offset-key="3b25066ae4be4029b101d90bd08aae80:12">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720"><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:0">Print </span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:1">_objects_</span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:2"> to the text stream </span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:3">_file_</span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:4">, separated by </span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:5">_sep_</span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:6"> and followed by </span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:7">_end_</span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:8">. </span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:9">_sep_</span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:10">, </span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:11">_end_</span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:12">, </span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:13">_file_</span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:14"> and </span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:15">_flush_</span><span data-offset-key="8fc1d289a76f43a091312d9187cbc720:16">, if present, must be given as keyword arguments.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1c2a97ee5b5244fe801582af97d6fef8"><span data-offset-key="1c2a97ee5b5244fe801582af97d6fef8:0">All non-keyword arguments are converted to strings like </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ec3c1dc52c04449ea789d24dc7652298"><span data-offset-key="ec3c1dc52c04449ea789d24dc7652298:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f"><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:0"> does and written to the stream, separated by </span><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:1">_sep_</span><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:2"> and followed by </span><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:3">_end_</span><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:4">. Both </span><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:5">_sep_</span><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:6"> and </span><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:7">_end_</span><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:8"> must be strings; they can also be </span><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:9">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:10">, which means to use the default values. If no </span><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:11">_objects_</span><span data-offset-key="6962aef3d11942b4b6447feb57425b1f:12"> are given, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#print" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c6c923d52ffc431e938f4968003c284c"><span data-offset-key="c6c923d52ffc431e938f4968003c284c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">print()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="484a2e6bf63c4b85b50ce1b11dbe08f1"><span data-offset-key="484a2e6bf63c4b85b50ce1b11dbe08f1:0"> will just write </span><span data-offset-key="484a2e6bf63c4b85b50ce1b11dbe08f1:1">_end_</span><span data-offset-key="484a2e6bf63c4b85b50ce1b11dbe08f1:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1bd85fed76474801906737419b3e8201"><span data-offset-key="1bd85fed76474801906737419b3e8201:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="1bd85fed76474801906737419b3e8201:1">_file_</span><span data-offset-key="1bd85fed76474801906737419b3e8201:2"> argument must be an object with a </span><span data-offset-key="1bd85fed76474801906737419b3e8201:3">`write(string)`</span><span data-offset-key="1bd85fed76474801906737419b3e8201:4"> method; if it is not present or </span><span data-offset-key="1bd85fed76474801906737419b3e8201:5">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="1bd85fed76474801906737419b3e8201:6">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.stdout" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0013d3696e714daab011278f8d2de5f3"><span data-offset-key="0013d3696e714daab011278f8d2de5f3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.stdout</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d5ca1f6a85bc46bc8f4a09867af1ff52"><span data-offset-key="d5ca1f6a85bc46bc8f4a09867af1ff52:0"> will be used. Since printed arguments are converted to text strings, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#print" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f43d001edf634453ad74cbb08082ba45"><span data-offset-key="f43d001edf634453ad74cbb08082ba45:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">print()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b5cfef2194fe4035bb15a7d6c8dc72d3"><span data-offset-key="b5cfef2194fe4035bb15a7d6c8dc72d3:0"> cannot be used with binary mode file objects. For these, use </span><span data-offset-key="b5cfef2194fe4035bb15a7d6c8dc72d3:1">`file.write(...)`</span><span data-offset-key="b5cfef2194fe4035bb15a7d6c8dc72d3:2"> instead.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a53b70d05891404cb7adb01965972b72"><span data-offset-key="a53b70d05891404cb7adb01965972b72:0">Whether output is buffered is usually determined by </span><span data-offset-key="a53b70d05891404cb7adb01965972b72:1">_file_</span><span data-offset-key="a53b70d05891404cb7adb01965972b72:2">, but if the </span><span data-offset-key="a53b70d05891404cb7adb01965972b72:3">_flush_</span><span data-offset-key="a53b70d05891404cb7adb01965972b72:4"> keyword argument is true, the stream is forcibly flushed.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e"><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:0">Changed in version 3.3: Added the </span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:1">_flush_</span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:2"> keyword argument.</span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:3">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:4"> </span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:5">`property`</span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:6">(</span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:7">_fget=None_</span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:8">, </span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:9">_fset=None_</span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:10">, </span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:11">_fdel=None_</span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:12">, </span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:13">_doc=None_</span><span data-offset-key="b6bd605fc8564fd7afe70630773cec8e:14">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dec6d21adf594b6f921acc8ad6297342"><span data-offset-key="dec6d21adf594b6f921acc8ad6297342:0">Return a property attribute.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="15b24697eaaa4c3d812dd9621e291198"><span data-offset-key="15b24697eaaa4c3d812dd9621e291198:0">_fget_</span><span data-offset-key="15b24697eaaa4c3d812dd9621e291198:1"> is a function for getting an attribute value. </span><span data-offset-key="15b24697eaaa4c3d812dd9621e291198:2">_fset_</span><span data-offset-key="15b24697eaaa4c3d812dd9621e291198:3"> is a function for setting an attribute value. </span><span data-offset-key="15b24697eaaa4c3d812dd9621e291198:4">_fdel_</span><span data-offset-key="15b24697eaaa4c3d812dd9621e291198:5"> is a function for deleting an attribute value. And </span><span data-offset-key="15b24697eaaa4c3d812dd9621e291198:6">_doc_</span><span data-offset-key="15b24697eaaa4c3d812dd9621e291198:7"> creates a docstring for the attribute.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6af973f37108414795833663025940bc"><span data-offset-key="6af973f37108414795833663025940bc:0">A typical use is to define a managed attribute </span><span data-offset-key="6af973f37108414795833663025940bc:1">`x`</span><span data-offset-key="6af973f37108414795833663025940bc:2">:</span></span></span>

    class C:    def __init__(self):        self._x = None​    def getx(self):        return self._x​    def setx(self, value):        self._x = value​    def delx(self):        del self._x​    x = property(getx, setx, delx, "I'm the 'x' property.")

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4276139fbbe94df581279301f5c7e044"><span data-offset-key="4276139fbbe94df581279301f5c7e044:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="4276139fbbe94df581279301f5c7e044:1">_c_</span><span data-offset-key="4276139fbbe94df581279301f5c7e044:2"> is an instance of </span><span data-offset-key="4276139fbbe94df581279301f5c7e044:3">_C_</span><span data-offset-key="4276139fbbe94df581279301f5c7e044:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="4276139fbbe94df581279301f5c7e044:5">`c.x`</span><span data-offset-key="4276139fbbe94df581279301f5c7e044:6"> will invoke the getter, </span><span data-offset-key="4276139fbbe94df581279301f5c7e044:7">`c.x = value`</span><span data-offset-key="4276139fbbe94df581279301f5c7e044:8"> will invoke the setter and </span><span data-offset-key="4276139fbbe94df581279301f5c7e044:9">`del c.x`</span><span data-offset-key="4276139fbbe94df581279301f5c7e044:10"> the deleter.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ca0b57e055ed464da9a9c6b6099ad68f"><span data-offset-key="ca0b57e055ed464da9a9c6b6099ad68f:0">If given, </span><span data-offset-key="ca0b57e055ed464da9a9c6b6099ad68f:1">_doc_</span><span data-offset-key="ca0b57e055ed464da9a9c6b6099ad68f:2"> will be the docstring of the property attribute. Otherwise, the property will copy </span><span data-offset-key="ca0b57e055ed464da9a9c6b6099ad68f:3">_fget_</span><span data-offset-key="ca0b57e055ed464da9a9c6b6099ad68f:4">’s docstring (if it exists). This makes it possible to create read-only properties easily using </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#property" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6be838d33a924d19b97d66f87f88c7c9"><span data-offset-key="6be838d33a924d19b97d66f87f88c7c9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">property()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="cff9443c07b74221aeb98ef95686ac45"><span data-offset-key="cff9443c07b74221aeb98ef95686ac45:0"> as a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-decorator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ddf3fafd15a349ac85fad68f910034fb"><span data-offset-key="ddf3fafd15a349ac85fad68f910034fb:0">decorator</span></span></a><span data-key="692b8fabd33c4193a42d6ac7d265f1e8"><span data-offset-key="692b8fabd33c4193a42d6ac7d265f1e8:0">:</span></span></span>

    class Parrot:    def __init__(self):        self._voltage = 100000​    @property    def voltage(self):        """Get the current voltage."""        return self._voltage

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f1f8497744894ed891e0df492fea5f14"><span data-offset-key="f1f8497744894ed891e0df492fea5f14:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="f1f8497744894ed891e0df492fea5f14:1">`@property`</span><span data-offset-key="f1f8497744894ed891e0df492fea5f14:2"> decorator turns the </span><span data-offset-key="f1f8497744894ed891e0df492fea5f14:3">`voltage()`</span><span data-offset-key="f1f8497744894ed891e0df492fea5f14:4"> method into a “getter” for a read-only attribute with the same name, and it sets the docstring for </span><span data-offset-key="f1f8497744894ed891e0df492fea5f14:5">_voltage_</span><span data-offset-key="f1f8497744894ed891e0df492fea5f14:6"> to “Get the current voltage.”</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2784608a70a9421c8dfc1c45360169a4"><span data-offset-key="2784608a70a9421c8dfc1c45360169a4:0">A property object has </span><span data-offset-key="2784608a70a9421c8dfc1c45360169a4:1">`getter`</span><span data-offset-key="2784608a70a9421c8dfc1c45360169a4:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="2784608a70a9421c8dfc1c45360169a4:3">`setter`</span><span data-offset-key="2784608a70a9421c8dfc1c45360169a4:4">, and </span><span data-offset-key="2784608a70a9421c8dfc1c45360169a4:5">`deleter`</span><span data-offset-key="2784608a70a9421c8dfc1c45360169a4:6"> methods usable as decorators that create a copy of the property with the corresponding accessor function set to the decorated function. This is best explained with an example:</span></span></span>

    class C:    def __init__(self):        self._x = None​    @property    def x(self):        """I'm the 'x' property."""        return self._x​    @x.setter    def x(self, value):        self._x = value​    @x.deleter    def x(self):        del self._x

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0bce31b648ac4c3e8e60faa4afc7b0f0"><span data-offset-key="0bce31b648ac4c3e8e60faa4afc7b0f0:0">This code is exactly equivalent to the first example. Be sure to give the additional functions the same name as the original property (</span><span data-offset-key="0bce31b648ac4c3e8e60faa4afc7b0f0:1">`x`</span><span data-offset-key="0bce31b648ac4c3e8e60faa4afc7b0f0:2"> in this case.)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="11b7a6b2541c4c0689a24a4cf42ac710"><span data-offset-key="11b7a6b2541c4c0689a24a4cf42ac710:0">The returned property object also has the attributes </span><span data-offset-key="11b7a6b2541c4c0689a24a4cf42ac710:1">`fget`</span><span data-offset-key="11b7a6b2541c4c0689a24a4cf42ac710:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="11b7a6b2541c4c0689a24a4cf42ac710:3">`fset`</span><span data-offset-key="11b7a6b2541c4c0689a24a4cf42ac710:4">, and </span><span data-offset-key="11b7a6b2541c4c0689a24a4cf42ac710:5">`fdel`</span><span data-offset-key="11b7a6b2541c4c0689a24a4cf42ac710:6"> corresponding to the constructor arguments.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0"><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:0">Changed in version 3.5: The docstrings of property objects are now writeable.</span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:1">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:2"> </span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:3">`range`</span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:5">_stop_</span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:6">)</span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:7">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:8"> </span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:9">`range`</span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:10">(</span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:11">_start_</span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:12">, </span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:13">_stop_</span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:14">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:15">_step_</span><span data-offset-key="eb2e9ca1e3134981b5b27caaafdbe9f0:16">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1c200fcf8db340ec8019965900a03259"><span data-offset-key="1c200fcf8db340ec8019965900a03259:0">Rather than being a function, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#range" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a43a2bd105bc47729a9be54b645dd997"><span data-offset-key="a43a2bd105bc47729a9be54b645dd997:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">range</code></span></span></a><span data-key="fa5b0e9fdb02488a900becc544b44359"><span data-offset-key="fa5b0e9fdb02488a900becc544b44359:0"> is actually an immutable sequence type, as documented in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq-range" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4aece80e7629479194e13c4f0ff4ca1f"><span data-offset-key="4aece80e7629479194e13c4f0ff4ca1f:0">Ranges</span></span></a><span data-key="c5a6b51af39b45d2b0093a6ad3cf92e7"><span data-offset-key="c5a6b51af39b45d2b0093a6ad3cf92e7:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="291027fd9e8f4a00907b95e34d95b988"><span data-offset-key="291027fd9e8f4a00907b95e34d95b988:0">Sequence Types — list, tuple, range</span></span></a><span data-key="f572c30f6af34290a4b78cf2939a37b9"><span data-offset-key="f572c30f6af34290a4b78cf2939a37b9:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="f572c30f6af34290a4b78cf2939a37b9:1">`repr`</span><span data-offset-key="f572c30f6af34290a4b78cf2939a37b9:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="f572c30f6af34290a4b78cf2939a37b9:3">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="f572c30f6af34290a4b78cf2939a37b9:4">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="53e23cdf2f904f2a99ebafc2829e44f8"><span data-offset-key="53e23cdf2f904f2a99ebafc2829e44f8:0">Return a string containing a printable representation of an object. For many types, this function makes an attempt to return a string that would yield an object with the same value when passed to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#eval" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="81626800d9ad4c959470a4c64f08d97a"><span data-offset-key="81626800d9ad4c959470a4c64f08d97a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">eval()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d0e698f03e634743a4572cf0a4c14b17"><span data-offset-key="d0e698f03e634743a4572cf0a4c14b17:0">, otherwise the representation is a string enclosed in angle brackets that contains the name of the type of the object together with additional information often including the name and address of the object. A class can control what this function returns for its instances by defining a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__repr__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3de468884a474de590e26d3080a4d401"><span data-offset-key="3de468884a474de590e26d3080a4d401:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**repr**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6ff850b5a6ab42a5aa23a10b4599996f"><span data-offset-key="6ff850b5a6ab42a5aa23a10b4599996f:0"> method.</span><span data-offset-key="6ff850b5a6ab42a5aa23a10b4599996f:1">`reversed`</span><span data-offset-key="6ff850b5a6ab42a5aa23a10b4599996f:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="6ff850b5a6ab42a5aa23a10b4599996f:3">_seq_</span><span data-offset-key="6ff850b5a6ab42a5aa23a10b4599996f:4">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8ad6e10fa8e24dee80c1f719af7f1518"><span data-offset-key="8ad6e10fa8e24dee80c1f719af7f1518:0">Return a reverse </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-iterator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="14b5ff32e4bf469591c05e46a49630e2"><span data-offset-key="14b5ff32e4bf469591c05e46a49630e2:0">iterator</span></span></a><span data-key="14ac9d9b724347368959f5c9d2e77357"><span data-offset-key="14ac9d9b724347368959f5c9d2e77357:0">. </span><span data-offset-key="14ac9d9b724347368959f5c9d2e77357:1">_seq_</span><span data-offset-key="14ac9d9b724347368959f5c9d2e77357:2"> must be an object which has a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__reversed__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ef17fd0271044a909b8237615d6782f5"><span data-offset-key="ef17fd0271044a909b8237615d6782f5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**reversed**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c1fdd5b0a818455cba960f3ca960dd3c"><span data-offset-key="c1fdd5b0a818455cba960f3ca960dd3c:0"> method or supports the sequence protocol (the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__len__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7112e2a7484844fbabdf1c561bdc3280"><span data-offset-key="7112e2a7484844fbabdf1c561bdc3280:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**len**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a1a2aff1f4ae4eb4b9b83e9266aa5539"><span data-offset-key="a1a2aff1f4ae4eb4b9b83e9266aa5539:0"> method and the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e11fcd5e0ebb416597472e9ff2320b92"><span data-offset-key="e11fcd5e0ebb416597472e9ff2320b92:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**getitem**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1611f8eb852048968ec757adb5adaae7"><span data-offset-key="1611f8eb852048968ec757adb5adaae7:0"> method with integer arguments starting at </span><span data-offset-key="1611f8eb852048968ec757adb5adaae7:1">`0`</span><span data-offset-key="1611f8eb852048968ec757adb5adaae7:2">).</span><span data-offset-key="1611f8eb852048968ec757adb5adaae7:3">`round`</span><span data-offset-key="1611f8eb852048968ec757adb5adaae7:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="1611f8eb852048968ec757adb5adaae7:5">_number_</span><span data-offset-key="1611f8eb852048968ec757adb5adaae7:6">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="1611f8eb852048968ec757adb5adaae7:7">_ndigits_</span><span data-offset-key="1611f8eb852048968ec757adb5adaae7:8">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c3b598da3667476a8935617c8b11ebcd"><span data-offset-key="c3b598da3667476a8935617c8b11ebcd:0">Return </span><span data-offset-key="c3b598da3667476a8935617c8b11ebcd:1">_number_</span><span data-offset-key="c3b598da3667476a8935617c8b11ebcd:2"> rounded to </span><span data-offset-key="c3b598da3667476a8935617c8b11ebcd:3">_ndigits_</span><span data-offset-key="c3b598da3667476a8935617c8b11ebcd:4"> precision after the decimal point. If </span><span data-offset-key="c3b598da3667476a8935617c8b11ebcd:5">_ndigits_</span><span data-offset-key="c3b598da3667476a8935617c8b11ebcd:6"> is omitted or is </span><span data-offset-key="c3b598da3667476a8935617c8b11ebcd:7">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="c3b598da3667476a8935617c8b11ebcd:8">, it returns the nearest integer to its input.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="91e953d4cbff4471842a5c160c7c174f"><span data-offset-key="91e953d4cbff4471842a5c160c7c174f:0">For the built-in types supporting </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#round" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4fb8bcc17795475d920d5f227bb86171"><span data-offset-key="4fb8bcc17795475d920d5f227bb86171:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">round()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328"><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:0">, values are rounded to the closest multiple of 10 to the power minus </span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:1">_ndigits_</span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:2">; if two multiples are equally close, rounding is done toward the even choice (so, for example, both </span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:3">`round(0.5)`</span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:5">`round(-0.5)`</span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:6"> are </span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:7">`0`</span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:8">, and </span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:9">`round(1.5)`</span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:10"> is </span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:11">`2`</span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:12">). Any integer value is valid for </span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:13">_ndigits_</span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:14"> (positive, zero, or negative). The return value is an integer if </span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:15">_ndigits_</span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:16"> is omitted or </span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:17">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:18">. Otherwise the return value has the same type as </span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:19">_number_</span><span data-offset-key="3c760b22984d45c380c887c10f7d9328:20">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f067d582cc11436ea20720725d1ce0df"><span data-offset-key="f067d582cc11436ea20720725d1ce0df:0">For a general Python object </span><span data-offset-key="f067d582cc11436ea20720725d1ce0df:1">`number`</span><span data-offset-key="f067d582cc11436ea20720725d1ce0df:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="f067d582cc11436ea20720725d1ce0df:3">`round`</span><span data-offset-key="f067d582cc11436ea20720725d1ce0df:4"> delegates to </span><span data-offset-key="f067d582cc11436ea20720725d1ce0df:5">`number.__round__`</span><span data-offset-key="f067d582cc11436ea20720725d1ce0df:6">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="426efdc7257b4a158c4435647e116b45"><span data-offset-key="426efdc7257b4a158c4435647e116b45:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="331114955e74423ab6f9e6eaf3c2502a"><span data-offset-key="331114955e74423ab6f9e6eaf3c2502a:0">The behavior of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#round" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8710d4bc457f42068ed8626eee432af1"><span data-offset-key="8710d4bc457f42068ed8626eee432af1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">round()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7d8dca12602b49eeb1f0351ea8c72fe9"><span data-offset-key="7d8dca12602b49eeb1f0351ea8c72fe9:0"> for floats can be surprising: for example, </span><span data-offset-key="7d8dca12602b49eeb1f0351ea8c72fe9:1">`round(2.675, 2)`</span><span data-offset-key="7d8dca12602b49eeb1f0351ea8c72fe9:2"> gives </span><span data-offset-key="7d8dca12602b49eeb1f0351ea8c72fe9:3">`2.67`</span><span data-offset-key="7d8dca12602b49eeb1f0351ea8c72fe9:4"> instead of the expected </span><span data-offset-key="7d8dca12602b49eeb1f0351ea8c72fe9:5">`2.68`</span><span data-offset-key="7d8dca12602b49eeb1f0351ea8c72fe9:6">. This is not a bug: it’s a result of the fact that most decimal fractions can’t be represented exactly as a float. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/tutorial/floatingpoint.html#tut-fp-issues" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e003007ba3af4740b30f38ac0394e2f0"><span data-offset-key="e003007ba3af4740b30f38ac0394e2f0:0">Floating Point Arithmetic: Issues and Limitations</span></span></a><span data-key="b1da16bed96b4ef88edb80cc238a5df0"><span data-offset-key="b1da16bed96b4ef88edb80cc238a5df0:0"> for more information.</span><span data-offset-key="b1da16bed96b4ef88edb80cc238a5df0:1">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="b1da16bed96b4ef88edb80cc238a5df0:2"> </span><span data-offset-key="b1da16bed96b4ef88edb80cc238a5df0:3">`set`</span><span data-offset-key="b1da16bed96b4ef88edb80cc238a5df0:4">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="b1da16bed96b4ef88edb80cc238a5df0:5">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="b1da16bed96b4ef88edb80cc238a5df0:6">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="80cff3ab71484d918b19ad6963ec71b8"><span data-offset-key="80cff3ab71484d918b19ad6963ec71b8:0">Return a new </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#set" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e8c6407d6f094cf59a1b3fc2c72637b5"><span data-offset-key="e8c6407d6f094cf59a1b3fc2c72637b5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">set</code></span></span></a><span data-key="94c594211f3d4cbaa78b264b78ce377d"><span data-offset-key="94c594211f3d4cbaa78b264b78ce377d:0"> object, optionally with elements taken from </span><span data-offset-key="94c594211f3d4cbaa78b264b78ce377d:1">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="94c594211f3d4cbaa78b264b78ce377d:2">. </span><span data-offset-key="94c594211f3d4cbaa78b264b78ce377d:3">`set`</span><span data-offset-key="94c594211f3d4cbaa78b264b78ce377d:4"> is a built-in class. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#set" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="de168bf90034400fb7a6d67c25240eae"><span data-offset-key="de168bf90034400fb7a6d67c25240eae:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">set</code></span></span></a><span data-key="584cec0991f346e5820ff8c8d6a2a356"><span data-offset-key="584cec0991f346e5820ff8c8d6a2a356:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#types-set" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e2ed5a9c023e417f8e808446748fd3be"><span data-offset-key="e2ed5a9c023e417f8e808446748fd3be:0">Set Types — set, frozenset</span></span></a><span data-key="4a7a15083de74d05820e03a9be9f0c3a"><span data-offset-key="4a7a15083de74d05820e03a9be9f0c3a:0"> for documentation about this class.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="289ee6c4567c4a48af5827a5be2c1686"><span data-offset-key="289ee6c4567c4a48af5827a5be2c1686:0">For other containers see the built-in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ffa335abb7ed481d8f7f16aa33fe7512"><span data-offset-key="ffa335abb7ed481d8f7f16aa33fe7512:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">frozenset</code></span></span></a><span data-key="fbd08ec3df294698baf14b916c5480c8"><span data-offset-key="fbd08ec3df294698baf14b916c5480c8:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7a8471f3c82e4221ac0f6c64c8d1ed3f"><span data-offset-key="7a8471f3c82e4221ac0f6c64c8d1ed3f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3159a11c75004c2fbdc503968c839690"><span data-offset-key="3159a11c75004c2fbdc503968c839690:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3abdc3d6225a4564b6a9ef778a480d5f"><span data-offset-key="3abdc3d6225a4564b6a9ef778a480d5f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">tuple</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e233d04c93544e1facbc20d69fe4d6d9"><span data-offset-key="e233d04c93544e1facbc20d69fe4d6d9:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f308e93c19504209a3130b208be72a2d"><span data-offset-key="f308e93c19504209a3130b208be72a2d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9967456d98cf45f3aeba57b5f85b03ac"><span data-offset-key="9967456d98cf45f3aeba57b5f85b03ac:0"> classes, as well as the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.html#module-collections" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e01c14caa0434c8c86c9f3017766c304"><span data-offset-key="e01c14caa0434c8c86c9f3017766c304:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">collections</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8f308d266dab416488e3d2496c317536"><span data-offset-key="8f308d266dab416488e3d2496c317536:0"> module.</span><span data-offset-key="8f308d266dab416488e3d2496c317536:1">`setattr`</span><span
