data-offset-key="8f308d266dab416488e3d2496c317536:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="8f308d266dab416488e3d2496c317536:3">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="8f308d266dab416488e3d2496c317536:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="8f308d266dab416488e3d2496c317536:5">_name_</span><span data-offset-key="8f308d266dab416488e3d2496c317536:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="8f308d266dab416488e3d2496c317536:7">_value_</span><span data-offset-key="8f308d266dab416488e3d2496c317536:8">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="506e8520194640798070b889b75709d5"><span data-offset-key="506e8520194640798070b889b75709d5:0">This is the counterpart of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#getattr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="572bc5156911434394f8b2fbb4111ed4"><span data-offset-key="572bc5156911434394f8b2fbb4111ed4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">getattr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4652f1d2bf4a47ad993ae38669e7be67"><span data-offset-key="4652f1d2bf4a47ad993ae38669e7be67:0">. The arguments are an object, a string and an arbitrary value. The string may name an existing attribute or a new attribute. The function assigns the value to the attribute, provided the object allows it. For example, </span><span data-offset-key="4652f1d2bf4a47ad993ae38669e7be67:1">`setattr(x, 'foobar', 123)`</span><span data-offset-key="4652f1d2bf4a47ad993ae38669e7be67:2"> is equivalent to </span><span data-offset-key="4652f1d2bf4a47ad993ae38669e7be67:3">`x.foobar = 123`</span><span data-offset-key="4652f1d2bf4a47ad993ae38669e7be67:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e1167423240f4711b32120d8c8f478f0"><span data-offset-key="e1167423240f4711b32120d8c8f478f0:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d6f7204f8b484cbdab63015c5d3cfb25"><span data-offset-key="d6f7204f8b484cbdab63015c5d3cfb25:0">Since </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/expressions.html#private-name-mangling" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4606b3abdfb2431aa5afd52951353e8a"><span data-offset-key="4606b3abdfb2431aa5afd52951353e8a:0">private name mangling</span></span></a><span data-key="da0f499667ed447fb2664a2d49f8daec"><span data-offset-key="da0f499667ed447fb2664a2d49f8daec:0"> happens at compilation time, one must manually mangle a private attribute’s (attributes with two leading underscores) name in order to set it with </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#setattr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="699562e2da4c44bdba9d9918cfeaa93e"><span data-offset-key="699562e2da4c44bdba9d9918cfeaa93e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">setattr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4"><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:1">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:2"> </span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:3">`slice`</span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:5">_stop_</span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:6">)</span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:7">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:8"> </span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:9">`slice`</span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:10">(</span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:11">_start_</span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:12">, </span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:13">_stop_</span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:14">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:15">_step_</span><span data-offset-key="7a3a176647d6452e8ad54a26ed98d1d4:16">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="11636e659e964161b875ea1195d021c2"><span data-offset-key="11636e659e964161b875ea1195d021c2:0">Return a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-slice" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="54b5813a7125427a8afee514ee0ccad8"><span data-offset-key="54b5813a7125427a8afee514ee0ccad8:0">slice</span></span></a><span data-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b"><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:0"> object representing the set of indices specified by </span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:1">`range(start, stop, step)`</span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:2">. The </span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:3">_start_</span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:5">_step_</span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:6"> arguments default to </span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:7">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:8">. Slice objects have read-only data attributes </span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:9">`start`</span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:10">, </span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:11">`stop`</span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:12"> and </span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:13">`step`</span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:14"> which merely return the argument values (or their default). They have no other explicit functionality; however they are used by Numerical Python and other third party extensions. Slice objects are also generated when extended indexing syntax is used. For example: </span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:15">`a[start:stop:step]`</span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:16"> or </span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:17">`a[start:stop, i]`</span><span data-offset-key="8361490632d44934b445dd463617cd9b:18">. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/itertools.html#itertools.islice" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6624ba7c4cb34ecfb543cf298e14aca3"><span data-offset-key="6624ba7c4cb34ecfb543cf298e14aca3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">itertools.islice()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="10fa1849be934d449aaf72c6263619fd"><span data-offset-key="10fa1849be934d449aaf72c6263619fd:0"> for an alternate version that returns an iterator.</span><span data-offset-key="10fa1849be934d449aaf72c6263619fd:1">`sorted`</span><span data-offset-key="10fa1849be934d449aaf72c6263619fd:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="10fa1849be934d449aaf72c6263619fd:3">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="10fa1849be934d449aaf72c6263619fd:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="10fa1849be934d449aaf72c6263619fd:5">\*\**</span><span data-offset-key="10fa1849be934d449aaf72c6263619fd:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="10fa1849be934d449aaf72c6263619fd:7">*key=None*</span><span data-offset-key="10fa1849be934d449aaf72c6263619fd:8">, </span><span data-offset-key="10fa1849be934d449aaf72c6263619fd:9">*reverse=False\*</span><span data-offset-key="10fa1849be934d449aaf72c6263619fd:10">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="60897e4ca54748229b63c5b0046b07ab"><span data-offset-key="60897e4ca54748229b63c5b0046b07ab:0">Return a new sorted list from the items in </span><span data-offset-key="60897e4ca54748229b63c5b0046b07ab:1">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="60897e4ca54748229b63c5b0046b07ab:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0c3df685492345e183c6af7b4f9831f3"><span data-offset-key="0c3df685492345e183c6af7b4f9831f3:0">Has two optional arguments which must be specified as keyword arguments.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fe6fab41b1f9427b8a3d618df5c960af"><span data-offset-key="fe6fab41b1f9427b8a3d618df5c960af:0">_key_</span><span data-offset-key="fe6fab41b1f9427b8a3d618df5c960af:1"> specifies a function of one argument that is used to extract a comparison key from each element in </span><span data-offset-key="fe6fab41b1f9427b8a3d618df5c960af:2">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="fe6fab41b1f9427b8a3d618df5c960af:3"> (for example, </span><span data-offset-key="fe6fab41b1f9427b8a3d618df5c960af:4">`key=str.lower`</span><span data-offset-key="fe6fab41b1f9427b8a3d618df5c960af:5">). The default value is </span><span data-offset-key="fe6fab41b1f9427b8a3d618df5c960af:6">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="fe6fab41b1f9427b8a3d618df5c960af:7"> (compare the elements directly).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c84fd3d424a24408ab303912ec74fde1"><span data-offset-key="c84fd3d424a24408ab303912ec74fde1:0">_reverse_</span><span data-offset-key="c84fd3d424a24408ab303912ec74fde1:1"> is a boolean value. If set to </span><span data-offset-key="c84fd3d424a24408ab303912ec74fde1:2">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="c84fd3d424a24408ab303912ec74fde1:3">, then the list elements are sorted as if each comparison were reversed.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="248dfb2cba5646e0bb6f76880272590e"><span data-offset-key="248dfb2cba5646e0bb6f76880272590e:0">Use </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functools.html#functools.cmp_to_key" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5248e6dfafe44e00a77ebe2086a2d628"><span data-offset-key="5248e6dfafe44e00a77ebe2086a2d628:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">functools.cmp_to_key()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="55b60ce442d54447b262de735ece59c2"><span data-offset-key="55b60ce442d54447b262de735ece59c2:0"> to convert an old-style </span><span data-offset-key="55b60ce442d54447b262de735ece59c2:1">_cmp_</span><span data-offset-key="55b60ce442d54447b262de735ece59c2:2"> function to a </span><span data-offset-key="55b60ce442d54447b262de735ece59c2:3">_key_</span><span data-offset-key="55b60ce442d54447b262de735ece59c2:4"> function.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="25d59bb43051494396dd553d419d8b52"><span data-offset-key="25d59bb43051494396dd553d419d8b52:0">The built-in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#sorted" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5fe8f9d8bfb5428baee651e0381b7918"><span data-offset-key="5fe8f9d8bfb5428baee651e0381b7918:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sorted()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="45c436adcdf44d18bb3910d68205c4c1"><span data-offset-key="45c436adcdf44d18bb3910d68205c4c1:0"> function is guaranteed to be stable. A sort is stable if it guarantees not to change the relative order of elements that compare equal — this is helpful for sorting in multiple passes (for example, sort by department, then by salary grade).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1094e922f3da44bbb1055e0c6a606dda"><span data-offset-key="1094e922f3da44bbb1055e0c6a606dda:0">For sorting examples and a brief sorting tutorial, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/howto/sorting.html#sortinghowto" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ed24f70db1a246a1a450837d21464f83"><span data-offset-key="ed24f70db1a246a1a450837d21464f83:0">Sorting HOW TO</span></span></a><span data-key="e2945e40220f463f9bca02f5f7558c6d"><span data-offset-key="e2945e40220f463f9bca02f5f7558c6d:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="e2945e40220f463f9bca02f5f7558c6d:1">`@staticmethod`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2893f6d42caf4fdebff61debafc6d4ca"><span data-offset-key="2893f6d42caf4fdebff61debafc6d4ca:0">Transform a method into a static method.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0c39896a473945948e472afad8ae74b0"><span data-offset-key="0c39896a473945948e472afad8ae74b0:0">A static method does not receive an implicit first argument. To declare a static method, use this idiom:</span></span></span>

    class C:    @staticmethod    def f(arg1, arg2, ...): ...

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ed6e8366d2264e649e279d33c981ce14"><span data-offset-key="ed6e8366d2264e649e279d33c981ce14:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="ed6e8366d2264e649e279d33c981ce14:1">`@staticmethod`</span><span data-offset-key="ed6e8366d2264e649e279d33c981ce14:2"> form is a function </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-decorator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5f86f8230b05471797541c9c7301e42d"><span data-offset-key="5f86f8230b05471797541c9c7301e42d:0">decorator</span></span></a><span data-key="64956113711143f8bdd78682a032c48d"><span data-offset-key="64956113711143f8bdd78682a032c48d:0"> – see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#function" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3a931b0fd40d4b9ebde6f25042b22b5a"><span data-offset-key="3a931b0fd40d4b9ebde6f25042b22b5a:0">Function definitions</span></span></a><span data-key="12da6bac4a9741afbff9a13e4e0bf133"><span data-offset-key="12da6bac4a9741afbff9a13e4e0bf133:0"> for details.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6bfcf2e7880547a8aa1da7f3b3b32c87"><span data-offset-key="6bfcf2e7880547a8aa1da7f3b3b32c87:0">A static method can be called either on the class (such as </span><span data-offset-key="6bfcf2e7880547a8aa1da7f3b3b32c87:1">`C.f()`</span><span data-offset-key="6bfcf2e7880547a8aa1da7f3b3b32c87:2">) or on an instance (such as </span><span data-offset-key="6bfcf2e7880547a8aa1da7f3b3b32c87:3">`C().f()`</span><span data-offset-key="6bfcf2e7880547a8aa1da7f3b3b32c87:4">).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="757c13dcff6d4fbd8152b8c778c0ca29"><span data-offset-key="757c13dcff6d4fbd8152b8c778c0ca29:0">Static methods in Python are similar to those found in Java or C++. Also see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#classmethod" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e72208778d9b4e87a82f3aec8401bb93"><span data-offset-key="e72208778d9b4e87a82f3aec8401bb93:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">classmethod()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5f51ae0215f84026848e8b910f54b246"><span data-offset-key="5f51ae0215f84026848e8b910f54b246:0"> for a variant that is useful for creating alternate class constructors.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="45b7fda6bb5d4c8a8bb28cc1ab093f47"><span data-offset-key="45b7fda6bb5d4c8a8bb28cc1ab093f47:0">Like all decorators, it is also possible to call </span><span data-offset-key="45b7fda6bb5d4c8a8bb28cc1ab093f47:1">`staticmethod`</span><span data-offset-key="45b7fda6bb5d4c8a8bb28cc1ab093f47:2"> as a regular function and do something with its result. This is needed in some cases where you need a reference to a function from a class body and you want to avoid the automatic transformation to instance method. For these cases, use this idiom:</span></span></span>

    class C:    builtin_open = staticmethod(open)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cc791db9924342939fac446cffd0dd3d"><span data-offset-key="cc791db9924342939fac446cffd0dd3d:0">For more information on static methods, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#types" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b05c0f271a2144c8bd2d3cbf38de6d80"><span data-offset-key="b05c0f271a2144c8bd2d3cbf38de6d80:0">The standard type hierarchy</span></span></a><span data-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598"><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:1">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:2"> </span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:3">`str`</span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:5">_object=''_</span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:6">)</span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:7">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:8"> </span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:9">`str`</span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:10">(</span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:11">_object=b''_</span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:12">, </span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:13">_encoding='utf-8'_</span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:14">, </span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:15">_errors='strict'_</span><span data-offset-key="6b97a473c3af4c9ab117cb5ba8ae2598:16">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="182666c27133483ea3d24ad52c800d80"><span data-offset-key="182666c27133483ea3d24ad52c800d80:0">Return a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f35f3df7b2244a009a33efad81dec955"><span data-offset-key="f35f3df7b2244a009a33efad81dec955:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="be91395e877f439a86dc2edd7961a556"><span data-offset-key="be91395e877f439a86dc2edd7961a556:0"> version of </span><span data-offset-key="be91395e877f439a86dc2edd7961a556:1">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="be91395e877f439a86dc2edd7961a556:2">. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="79ea551ce46c4c0cb6467b8e09590f08"><span data-offset-key="79ea551ce46c4c0cb6467b8e09590f08:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b79d6409ee7f460fabc822f78257ddb8"><span data-offset-key="b79d6409ee7f460fabc822f78257ddb8:0"> for details.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="76c67dcba2eb4aab918c9060cf348099"><span data-offset-key="76c67dcba2eb4aab918c9060cf348099:0">`str`</span><span data-offset-key="76c67dcba2eb4aab918c9060cf348099:1"> is the built-in string </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-class" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="deeadec982144ddbb1347fee7f70e71e"><span data-offset-key="deeadec982144ddbb1347fee7f70e71e:0">class</span></span></a><span data-key="6f82304c25ce4365b0bbba128b0f83f0"><span data-offset-key="6f82304c25ce4365b0bbba128b0f83f0:0">. For general information about strings, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#textseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7dca4020170f415496e61a477818cf63"><span data-offset-key="7dca4020170f415496e61a477818cf63:0">Text Sequence Type — str</span></span></a><span data-key="cc3437e98ac3439a8772965326b419c0"><span data-offset-key="cc3437e98ac3439a8772965326b419c0:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="cc3437e98ac3439a8772965326b419c0:1">`sum`</span><span data-offset-key="cc3437e98ac3439a8772965326b419c0:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="cc3437e98ac3439a8772965326b419c0:3">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="cc3437e98ac3439a8772965326b419c0:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="cc3437e98ac3439a8772965326b419c0:5">_/_</span><span data-offset-key="cc3437e98ac3439a8772965326b419c0:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="cc3437e98ac3439a8772965326b419c0:7">_start=0_</span><span data-offset-key="cc3437e98ac3439a8772965326b419c0:8">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a46f05ed5bc24af98cc11167af138711"><span data-offset-key="a46f05ed5bc24af98cc11167af138711:0">Sums </span><span data-offset-key="a46f05ed5bc24af98cc11167af138711:1">_start_</span><span data-offset-key="a46f05ed5bc24af98cc11167af138711:2"> and the items of an </span><span data-offset-key="a46f05ed5bc24af98cc11167af138711:3">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="a46f05ed5bc24af98cc11167af138711:4"> from left to right and returns the total. The </span><span data-offset-key="a46f05ed5bc24af98cc11167af138711:5">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="a46f05ed5bc24af98cc11167af138711:6">’s items are normally numbers, and the start value is not allowed to be a string.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="86035934090f4e6ea30d48307099cd20"><span data-offset-key="86035934090f4e6ea30d48307099cd20:0">For some use cases, there are good alternatives to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#sum" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="587ed718218342059dd20ddf90622d23"><span data-offset-key="587ed718218342059dd20ddf90622d23:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sum()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="bccca04a99d14796a303fa70ec1c0d74"><span data-offset-key="bccca04a99d14796a303fa70ec1c0d74:0">. The preferred, fast way to concatenate a sequence of strings is by calling </span><span data-offset-key="bccca04a99d14796a303fa70ec1c0d74:1">`''.join(sequence)`</span><span data-offset-key="bccca04a99d14796a303fa70ec1c0d74:2">. To add floating point values with extended precision, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/math.html#math.fsum" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8635bdb444cc4152b016d580d22a1eea"><span data-offset-key="8635bdb444cc4152b016d580d22a1eea:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">math.fsum()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="575852cecba247baaed8edf3d96e0bf4"><span data-offset-key="575852cecba247baaed8edf3d96e0bf4:0">. To concatenate a series of iterables, consider using </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/itertools.html#itertools.chain" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fa4484a38e6d47ebaf35dcf834edd21e"><span data-offset-key="fa4484a38e6d47ebaf35dcf834edd21e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">itertools.chain()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e3487edf4aff4d39aeb3f83162e912ab"><span data-offset-key="e3487edf4aff4d39aeb3f83162e912ab:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8216d3b84d9a40bc972207a5fa63ad67"><span data-offset-key="8216d3b84d9a40bc972207a5fa63ad67:0">Changed in version 3.8: The </span><span data-offset-key="8216d3b84d9a40bc972207a5fa63ad67:1">_start_</span><span data-offset-key="8216d3b84d9a40bc972207a5fa63ad67:2"> parameter can be specified as a keyword argument.</span><span data-offset-key="8216d3b84d9a40bc972207a5fa63ad67:3">`super`</span><span data-offset-key="8216d3b84d9a40bc972207a5fa63ad67:4">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="8216d3b84d9a40bc972207a5fa63ad67:5">_type_</span><span data-offset-key="8216d3b84d9a40bc972207a5fa63ad67:6">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="8216d3b84d9a40bc972207a5fa63ad67:7">_object-or-type_</span><span data-offset-key="8216d3b84d9a40bc972207a5fa63ad67:8">\]\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0c45336d131b4a1fb8e619104ad39c0c"><span data-offset-key="0c45336d131b4a1fb8e619104ad39c0c:0">Return a proxy object that delegates method calls to a parent or sibling class of </span><span data-offset-key="0c45336d131b4a1fb8e619104ad39c0c:1">_type_</span><span data-offset-key="0c45336d131b4a1fb8e619104ad39c0c:2">. This is useful for accessing inherited methods that have been overridden in a class.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d0b0496887a242988c32d60ace378c79"><span data-offset-key="d0b0496887a242988c32d60ace378c79:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="d0b0496887a242988c32d60ace378c79:1">_object-or-type_</span><span data-offset-key="d0b0496887a242988c32d60ace378c79:2"> determines the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-method-resolution-order" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a4dcfb5a89b14f4cb6e89c1124d5102b"><span data-offset-key="a4dcfb5a89b14f4cb6e89c1124d5102b:0">method resolution order</span></span></a><span data-key="eacbbd01acca4bc8853befb335c3aaac"><span data-offset-key="eacbbd01acca4bc8853befb335c3aaac:0"> to be searched. The search starts from the class right after the </span><span data-offset-key="eacbbd01acca4bc8853befb335c3aaac:1">_type_</span><span data-offset-key="eacbbd01acca4bc8853befb335c3aaac:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7e4dce9445b3488ea01d1b9ecf16945e"><span data-offset-key="7e4dce9445b3488ea01d1b9ecf16945e:0">For example, if </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#class.__mro__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="934a387f9329437bb89f223829ad5a1a"><span data-offset-key="934a387f9329437bb89f223829ad5a1a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**mro**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="06f6fad37eb14faf9043a4d6f8c59b99"><span data-offset-key="06f6fad37eb14faf9043a4d6f8c59b99:0"> of </span><span data-offset-key="06f6fad37eb14faf9043a4d6f8c59b99:1">_object-or-type_</span><span data-offset-key="06f6fad37eb14faf9043a4d6f8c59b99:2"> is </span><span data-offset-key="06f6fad37eb14faf9043a4d6f8c59b99:3">`D -> B -> C -> A -> object`</span><span data-offset-key="06f6fad37eb14faf9043a4d6f8c59b99:4"> and the value of </span><span data-offset-key="06f6fad37eb14faf9043a4d6f8c59b99:5">_type_</span><span data-offset-key="06f6fad37eb14faf9043a4d6f8c59b99:6"> is </span><span data-offset-key="06f6fad37eb14faf9043a4d6f8c59b99:7">`B`</span><span data-offset-key="06f6fad37eb14faf9043a4d6f8c59b99:8">, then </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#super" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f7534573ec4947baa39f86204956e4bd"><span data-offset-key="f7534573ec4947baa39f86204956e4bd:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">super()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="17b1b78b10f949ed85125ba002229783"><span data-offset-key="17b1b78b10f949ed85125ba002229783:0"> searches </span><span data-offset-key="17b1b78b10f949ed85125ba002229783:1">`C -> A -> object`</span><span data-offset-key="17b1b78b10f949ed85125ba002229783:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d108df4307484f82817a04b73c84f00f"><span data-offset-key="d108df4307484f82817a04b73c84f00f:0">The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#class.__mro__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6171ae84b01e4a189a1ff52843da183d"><span data-offset-key="6171ae84b01e4a189a1ff52843da183d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**mro**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a6fb182d5fb9404bb50869f0c284e8a1"><span data-offset-key="a6fb182d5fb9404bb50869f0c284e8a1:0"> attribute of the </span><span data-offset-key="a6fb182d5fb9404bb50869f0c284e8a1:1">_object-or-type_</span><span data-offset-key="a6fb182d5fb9404bb50869f0c284e8a1:2"> lists the method resolution search order used by both </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#getattr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5f3f2bf8c22d4c188979c691ae277b8e"><span data-offset-key="5f3f2bf8c22d4c188979c691ae277b8e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">getattr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="fb200c8b0e424a9282053910f3f77235"><span data-offset-key="fb200c8b0e424a9282053910f3f77235:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#super" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="278dce9b10fe481c8400225a8e1857a4"><span data-offset-key="278dce9b10fe481c8400225a8e1857a4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">super()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a5d8d2de84524343ab24a1f2457dd30b"><span data-offset-key="a5d8d2de84524343ab24a1f2457dd30b:0">. The attribute is dynamic and can change whenever the inheritance hierarchy is updated.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="45ef44e1da014e9e939bd1b0d6f5a3eb"><span data-offset-key="45ef44e1da014e9e939bd1b0d6f5a3eb:0">If the second argument is omitted, the super object returned is unbound. If the second argument is an object, </span><span data-offset-key="45ef44e1da014e9e939bd1b0d6f5a3eb:1">`isinstance(obj, type)`</span><span data-offset-key="45ef44e1da014e9e939bd1b0d6f5a3eb:2"> must be true. If the second argument is a type, </span><span data-offset-key="45ef44e1da014e9e939bd1b0d6f5a3eb:3">`issubclass(type2, type)`</span><span data-offset-key="45ef44e1da014e9e939bd1b0d6f5a3eb:4"> must be true (this is useful for classmethods).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4d6b819dd5444f4f81beec65c9adc7e3"><span data-offset-key="4d6b819dd5444f4f81beec65c9adc7e3:0">There are two typical use cases for </span><span data-offset-key="4d6b819dd5444f4f81beec65c9adc7e3:1">_super_</span><span data-offset-key="4d6b819dd5444f4f81beec65c9adc7e3:2">. In a class hierarchy with single inheritance, </span><span data-offset-key="4d6b819dd5444f4f81beec65c9adc7e3:3">_super_</span><span data-offset-key="4d6b819dd5444f4f81beec65c9adc7e3:4"> can be used to refer to parent classes without naming them explicitly, thus making the code more maintainable. This use closely parallels the use of </span><span data-offset-key="4d6b819dd5444f4f81beec65c9adc7e3:5">_super_</span><span data-offset-key="4d6b819dd5444f4f81beec65c9adc7e3:6"> in other programming languages.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9b4acabecce54e368083178630aa7457"><span data-offset-key="9b4acabecce54e368083178630aa7457:0">The second use case is to support cooperative multiple inheritance in a dynamic execution environment. This use case is unique to Python and is not found in statically compiled languages or languages that only support single inheritance. This makes it possible to implement “diamond diagrams” where multiple base classes implement the same method. Good design dictates that such implementations have the same calling signature in every case (because the order of calls is determined at runtime, because that order adapts to changes in the class hierarchy, and because that order can include sibling classes that are unknown prior to runtime).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="53fac07339d24a0889458c9c69dd2951"><span data-offset-key="53fac07339d24a0889458c9c69dd2951:0">For both use cases, a typical superclass call looks like this:</span></span></span>

    class C(B):    def method(self, arg):        super().method(arg)    # This does the same thing as:                               # super(C, self).method(arg)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="80fea875b80545d3bd4764d4e459aca1"><span data-offset-key="80fea875b80545d3bd4764d4e459aca1:0">In addition to method lookups, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#super" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1af981d1848e4517b22e2491fd72dc2d"><span data-offset-key="1af981d1848e4517b22e2491fd72dc2d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">super()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c2d4c42502c24844b1ecfba2415cce07"><span data-offset-key="c2d4c42502c24844b1ecfba2415cce07:0"> also works for attribute lookups. One possible use case for this is calling </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-descriptor" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ed5df4713b10476092dfaea7c179be2e"><span data-offset-key="ed5df4713b10476092dfaea7c179be2e:0">descriptors</span></span></a><span data-key="5e3ab49e03b149edb3e528ef10957255"><span data-offset-key="5e3ab49e03b149edb3e528ef10957255:0"> in a parent or sibling class.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c4035b11b0624665b44969b6bd079a58"><span data-offset-key="c4035b11b0624665b44969b6bd079a58:0">Note that </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#super" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4cf5441ea34048f48e4262600aacace9"><span data-offset-key="4cf5441ea34048f48e4262600aacace9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">super()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9a4d93dc000a4bd89d21efa6217b07bb"><span data-offset-key="9a4d93dc000a4bd89d21efa6217b07bb:0"> is implemented as part of the binding process for explicit dotted attribute lookups such as </span><span data-offset-key="9a4d93dc000a4bd89d21efa6217b07bb:1">`super().__getitem__(name)`</span><span data-offset-key="9a4d93dc000a4bd89d21efa6217b07bb:2">. It does so by implementing its own </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getattribute__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d09aa51583564c30958118ff43b09ee0"><span data-offset-key="d09aa51583564c30958118ff43b09ee0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**getattribute**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="edca0e08d9ae4bab84ae93847458a723"><span data-offset-key="edca0e08d9ae4bab84ae93847458a723:0"> method for searching classes in a predictable order that supports cooperative multiple inheritance. Accordingly, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#super" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="36c70f0785284398b8bdfc6658efc748"><span data-offset-key="36c70f0785284398b8bdfc6658efc748:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">super()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0e880dae28604306975e936277a7bedd"><span data-offset-key="0e880dae28604306975e936277a7bedd:0"> is undefined for implicit lookups using statements or operators such as </span><span data-offset-key="0e880dae28604306975e936277a7bedd:1">`super()[name]`</span><span data-offset-key="0e880dae28604306975e936277a7bedd:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c0fa0602da7f44e1b46adca60741690a"><span data-offset-key="c0fa0602da7f44e1b46adca60741690a:0">Also note that, aside from the zero argument form, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#super" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bab3cfdf43d04504b3c7086c57020bc8"><span data-offset-key="bab3cfdf43d04504b3c7086c57020bc8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">super()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="74fb7e21d8024dcc928f70b2f0061d82"><span data-offset-key="74fb7e21d8024dcc928f70b2f0061d82:0"> is not limited to use inside methods. The two argument form specifies the arguments exactly and makes the appropriate references. The zero argument form only works inside a class definition, as the compiler fills in the necessary details to correctly retrieve the class being defined, as well as accessing the current instance for ordinary methods.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="12a793b759c54ed59dd7ac8e88d3fe5a"><span data-offset-key="12a793b759c54ed59dd7ac8e88d3fe5a:0">For practical suggestions on how to design cooperative classes using </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#super" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f26585def0114d02b7a09635169408bc"><span data-offset-key="f26585def0114d02b7a09635169408bc:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">super()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="36c930cc4da14cd9980619b2aae302dd"><span data-offset-key="36c930cc4da14cd9980619b2aae302dd:0">, see </span></span><a href="https://rhettinger.wordpress.com/2011/05/26/super-considered-super/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9beb8df6e9964992a63659655832884e"><span data-offset-key="9beb8df6e9964992a63659655832884e:0">guide to using super()</span></span></a><span data-key="3428d979c3da43cb8adb5dde6da51916"><span data-offset-key="3428d979c3da43cb8adb5dde6da51916:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="3428d979c3da43cb8adb5dde6da51916:1">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="3428d979c3da43cb8adb5dde6da51916:2"> </span><span data-offset-key="3428d979c3da43cb8adb5dde6da51916:3">`tuple`</span><span data-offset-key="3428d979c3da43cb8adb5dde6da51916:4">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="3428d979c3da43cb8adb5dde6da51916:5">_iterable_</span><span data-offset-key="3428d979c3da43cb8adb5dde6da51916:6">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2d048580797f4b31a0d877f1480d5535"><span data-offset-key="2d048580797f4b31a0d877f1480d5535:0">Rather than being a function, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e136dbd1636044fb8a106d6ccc16f516"><span data-offset-key="e136dbd1636044fb8a106d6ccc16f516:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">tuple</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0911b97c8005421ab3ce469b15a75fe7"><span data-offset-key="0911b97c8005421ab3ce469b15a75fe7:0"> is actually an immutable sequence type, as documented in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq-tuple" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0b947003cd1a4c1fb60d7dcc0d24d3be"><span data-offset-key="0b947003cd1a4c1fb60d7dcc0d24d3be:0">Tuples</span></span></a><span data-key="a2891d900af24e73a0a1aec9f6ca1dc2"><span data-offset-key="a2891d900af24e73a0a1aec9f6ca1dc2:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="27f1dfd14f134ae2b932a666ddf80141"><span data-offset-key="27f1dfd14f134ae2b932a666ddf80141:0">Sequence Types — list, tuple, range</span></span></a><span data-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161"><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:0">.</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:1">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:2"> </span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:3">`type`</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:4">(</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:5">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:6">)</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:7">_class_</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:8"> </span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:9">`type`</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:10">(</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:11">_name_</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:12">, </span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:13">_bases_</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:14">, </span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:15">_dict_</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:16">, </span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:17">_\*\*kwds_</span><span data-offset-key="df320507a034492fbe0f984f16c2c161:18">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5a0ad24a46e84b93ac3bdabc2db9804b"><span data-offset-key="5a0ad24a46e84b93ac3bdabc2db9804b:0">With one argument, return the type of an </span><span data-offset-key="5a0ad24a46e84b93ac3bdabc2db9804b:1">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="5a0ad24a46e84b93ac3bdabc2db9804b:2">. The return value is a type object and generally the same object as returned by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#instance.__class__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5e14937a3414455a91ce73654acd1800"><span data-offset-key="5e14937a3414455a91ce73654acd1800:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">object.**class**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ea9dea5241ef413282926bed22877d91"><span data-offset-key="ea9dea5241ef413282926bed22877d91:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d36d05325ff04f00b2e2341d6f19ac5e"><span data-offset-key="d36d05325ff04f00b2e2341d6f19ac5e:0">The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#isinstance" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f858a3c8b9d5412d92256d1b5466dc56"><span data-offset-key="f858a3c8b9d5412d92256d1b5466dc56:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">isinstance()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6e4d69e069364c21afb80f70c5431f8f"><span data-offset-key="6e4d69e069364c21afb80f70c5431f8f:0"> built-in function is recommended for testing the type of an object, because it takes subclasses into account.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="acffa58ece75444b838afdb9a8dfaadf"><span data-offset-key="acffa58ece75444b838afdb9a8dfaadf:0">With three arguments, return a new type object. This is essentially a dynamic form of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#class" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9b85d81d9f724a428eaa5e6cd0cbf26b"><span data-offset-key="9b85d81d9f724a428eaa5e6cd0cbf26b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">class</code></span></span></a><span data-key="eb1acabb085047c2afb8e41520f3b389"><span data-offset-key="eb1acabb085047c2afb8e41520f3b389:0"> statement. The </span><span data-offset-key="eb1acabb085047c2afb8e41520f3b389:1">_name_</span><span data-offset-key="eb1acabb085047c2afb8e41520f3b389:2"> string is the class name and becomes the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#definition.__name__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cb8972978727437a88f2c6c9bbe3caaf"><span data-offset-key="cb8972978727437a88f2c6c9bbe3caaf:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**name**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8e0a90eb04df4943b75b2328d5f6e4a8"><span data-offset-key="8e0a90eb04df4943b75b2328d5f6e4a8:0"> attribute. The </span><span data-offset-key="8e0a90eb04df4943b75b2328d5f6e4a8:1">_bases_</span><span data-offset-key="8e0a90eb04df4943b75b2328d5f6e4a8:2"> tuple contains the base classes and becomes the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#class.__bases__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="15a26ed951d84370b47014c27b6748fd"><span data-offset-key="15a26ed951d84370b47014c27b6748fd:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**bases**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="306f3fb2feec4c5983b999dd3828f676"><span data-offset-key="306f3fb2feec4c5983b999dd3828f676:0"> attribute; if empty, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="17cd12f8e124474d9f742fc44a0b88a2"><span data-offset-key="17cd12f8e124474d9f742fc44a0b88a2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">object</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d07d153c4b8841ca8caf6cd38a33397b"><span data-offset-key="d07d153c4b8841ca8caf6cd38a33397b:0">, the ultimate base of all classes, is added. The </span><span data-offset-key="d07d153c4b8841ca8caf6cd38a33397b:1">_dict_</span><span data-offset-key="d07d153c4b8841ca8caf6cd38a33397b:2"> dictionary contains attribute and method definitions for the class body; it may be copied or wrapped before becoming the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#object.__dict__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6786caecdd7249cd9b6192c150ae5469"><span data-offset-key="6786caecdd7249cd9b6192c150ae5469:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**dict**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="756e7dd533854576aa222e55c0d8ebee"><span data-offset-key="756e7dd533854576aa222e55c0d8ebee:0"> attribute. The following two statements create identical </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#type" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b3bfdc887b6a497cb97b3f1882ce9dc6"><span data-offset-key="b3bfdc887b6a497cb97b3f1882ce9dc6:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">type</code></span></span></a><span data-key="88e69a5fae38469d896cdc0b7e4214c8"><span data-offset-key="88e69a5fae38469d896cdc0b7e4214c8:0"> objects:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> class X:...     a = 1...>>> X = type('X', (), dict(a=1))

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="195ac10d8469476a85aceeba3ce495af"><span data-offset-key="195ac10d8469476a85aceeba3ce495af:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bltin-type-objects" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2ac1514ba7fb44c49817d28c5e2e77e6"><span data-offset-key="2ac1514ba7fb44c49817d28c5e2e77e6:0">Type Objects</span></span></a><span data-key="78318704df94496689718021507a74ec"><span data-offset-key="78318704df94496689718021507a74ec:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4a9464ef43004fea90121cf4f3289250"><span data-offset-key="4a9464ef43004fea90121cf4f3289250:0">Keyword arguments provided to the three argument form are passed to the appropriate metaclass machinery (usually </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__init_subclass__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bcaccd23e1c14d479390f9178c8d6002"><span data-offset-key="bcaccd23e1c14d479390f9178c8d6002:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**init_subclass**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d02c479ece5d4305a7c46c03559a2354"><span data-offset-key="d02c479ece5d4305a7c46c03559a2354:0">) in the same way that keywords in a class definition (besides </span><span data-offset-key="d02c479ece5d4305a7c46c03559a2354:1">_metaclass_</span><span data-offset-key="d02c479ece5d4305a7c46c03559a2354:2">) would.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8596c8b2a1034063aa6e2906b62b850d"><span data-offset-key="8596c8b2a1034063aa6e2906b62b850d:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#class-customization" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9b72970a3f974c91bacfd3ed62e5032f"><span data-offset-key="9b72970a3f974c91bacfd3ed62e5032f:0">Customizing class creation</span></span></a><span data-key="92addffbb5b24eeebbf422a2fca66fd5"><span data-offset-key="92addffbb5b24eeebbf422a2fca66fd5:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="89a8b10f33db4a6b82473f0e75ad7535"><span data-offset-key="89a8b10f33db4a6b82473f0e75ad7535:0">Changed in version 3.6: Subclasses of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#type" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="249f2df970b94e91901356cb42a83dab"><span data-offset-key="249f2df970b94e91901356cb42a83dab:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">type</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b133326c238649f785f5665841604ce4"><span data-offset-key="b133326c238649f785f5665841604ce4:0"> which don’t override </span><span data-offset-key="b133326c238649f785f5665841604ce4:1">`type.__new__`</span><span data-offset-key="b133326c238649f785f5665841604ce4:2"> may no longer use the one-argument form to get the type of an object.</span><span data-offset-key="b133326c238649f785f5665841604ce4:3">`vars`</span><span data-offset-key="b133326c238649f785f5665841604ce4:4">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="b133326c238649f785f5665841604ce4:5">_object_</span><span data-offset-key="b133326c238649f785f5665841604ce4:6">\])</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f5d926541f034f4d9cf19ec1237235aa"><span data-offset-key="f5d926541f034f4d9cf19ec1237235aa:0">Return the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#object.__dict__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0b7519b199a94888a61df91e5cc1363e"><span data-offset-key="0b7519b199a94888a61df91e5cc1363e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**dict**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f31f923f618f4a48b743374d788341c6"><span data-offset-key="f31f923f618f4a48b743374d788341c6:0"> attribute for a module, class, instance, or any other object with a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#object.__dict__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="65343c38467749c89edaefc658bcac70"><span data-offset-key="65343c38467749c89edaefc658bcac70:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**dict**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f199914ffc814dc59c8e17e58eba8c74"><span data-offset-key="f199914ffc814dc59c8e17e58eba8c74:0"> attribute.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6e08a604393242988dd48b9ad87c5a33"><span data-offset-key="6e08a604393242988dd48b9ad87c5a33:0">Objects such as modules and instances have an updateable </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#object.__dict__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9163ce43eca34204ab97ea76805853ab"><span data-offset-key="9163ce43eca34204ab97ea76805853ab:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**dict**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1240b6a9da8f45f282bb9bd710b241cd"><span data-offset-key="1240b6a9da8f45f282bb9bd710b241cd:0"> attribute; however, other objects may have write restrictions on their </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#object.__dict__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dccdc4154e444b65a7887e32a104bc70"><span data-offset-key="dccdc4154e444b65a7887e32a104bc70:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**dict**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="666a37315a77470dbed916d3b81ff041"><span data-offset-key="666a37315a77470dbed916d3b81ff041:0"> attributes (for example, classes use a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/types.html#types.MappingProxyType" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8829688f396a4df694c3816348ca5831"><span data-offset-key="8829688f396a4df694c3816348ca5831:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">types.MappingProxyType</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e9c4381363c447b48ce8c2c2120f2048"><span data-offset-key="e9c4381363c447b48ce8c2c2120f2048:0"> to prevent direct dictionary updates).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3f3491639ca14b54b81790cc44a8815f"><span data-offset-key="3f3491639ca14b54b81790cc44a8815f:0">Without an argument, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#vars" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c51152bf43324158b8fe9a0571767ba4"><span data-offset-key="c51152bf43324158b8fe9a0571767ba4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">vars()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5587e63a6c854bedb7c6f54db4099a43"><span data-offset-key="5587e63a6c854bedb7c6f54db4099a43:0"> acts like </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#locals" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="75a54c5efec34d4e9b82662a165728a0"><span data-offset-key="75a54c5efec34d4e9b82662a165728a0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">locals()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="714fe30b3ee34418b8f5d934b9fe5692"><span data-offset-key="714fe30b3ee34418b8f5d934b9fe5692:0">. Note, the locals dictionary is only useful for reads since updates to the locals dictionary are ignored.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="950c4bc4cbfa400d8a04123f15420bb0"><span data-offset-key="950c4bc4cbfa400d8a04123f15420bb0:0">A </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2e7ab0c3fafc481f913f0bf08a1c4556"><span data-offset-key="2e7ab0c3fafc481f913f0bf08a1c4556:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">TypeError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="041855e7b8db41fe8b336db4502a8af2"><span data-offset-key="041855e7b8db41fe8b336db4502a8af2:0"> exception is raised if an object is specified but it doesn’t have a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#object.__dict__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="13622dcad39d459eafcf938326bb76fa"><span data-offset-key="13622dcad39d459eafcf938326bb76fa:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**dict**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4f723a681db345b592107476e2029182"><span data-offset-key="4f723a681db345b592107476e2029182:0"> attribute (for example, if its class defines the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__slots__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="842c984ccfde4df7a6131a7bf01d0da5"><span data-offset-key="842c984ccfde4df7a6131a7bf01d0da5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**slots**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d3231901e06147719310c5fb8722654e"><span data-offset-key="d3231901e06147719310c5fb8722654e:0"> attribute).</span><span data-offset-key="d3231901e06147719310c5fb8722654e:1">`zip`</span><span data-offset-key="d3231901e06147719310c5fb8722654e:2">(</span><span data-offset-key="d3231901e06147719310c5fb8722654e:3">_\*iterables_</span><span data-offset-key="d3231901e06147719310c5fb8722654e:4">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="de836476de65446ab9ae6b5aaa1b77a9"><span data-offset-key="de836476de65446ab9ae6b5aaa1b77a9:0">Make an iterator that aggregates elements from each of the iterables.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4f35ced48617400296b047e738f58a1f"><span data-offset-key="4f35ced48617400296b047e738f58a1f:0">Returns an iterator of tuples, where the </span><span data-offset-key="4f35ced48617400296b047e738f58a1f:1">_i_</span><span data-offset-key="4f35ced48617400296b047e738f58a1f:2">-th tuple contains the </span><span data-offset-key="4f35ced48617400296b047e738f58a1f:3">_i_</span><span data-offset-key="4f35ced48617400296b047e738f58a1f:4">-th element from each of the argument sequences or iterables. The iterator stops when the shortest input iterable is exhausted. With a single iterable argument, it returns an iterator of 1-tuples. With no arguments, it returns an empty iterator. Equivalent to:</span></span></span>

    def zip(*iterables):    # zip('ABCD', 'xy') --> Ax By    sentinel = object()    iterators = [iter(it) for it in iterables]    while iterators:        result = []        for it in iterators:            elem = next(it, sentinel)            if elem is sentinel:                return            result.append(elem)        yield tuple(result)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="75fa2e43dcc148fcb6ba5e088f55bd06"><span data-offset-key="75fa2e43dcc148fcb6ba5e088f55bd06:0">The left-to-right evaluation order of the iterables is guaranteed. This makes possible an idiom for clustering a data series into n-length groups using </span><span data-offset-key="75fa2e43dcc148fcb6ba5e088f55bd06:1">`zip(*[iter(s)]*n)`</span><span data-offset-key="75fa2e43dcc148fcb6ba5e088f55bd06:2">. This repeats the </span><span data-offset-key="75fa2e43dcc148fcb6ba5e088f55bd06:3">_same_</span><span data-offset-key="75fa2e43dcc148fcb6ba5e088f55bd06:4"> iterator </span><span data-offset-key="75fa2e43dcc148fcb6ba5e088f55bd06:5">`n`</span><span data-offset-key="75fa2e43dcc148fcb6ba5e088f55bd06:6"> times so that each output tuple has the result of </span><span data-offset-key="75fa2e43dcc148fcb6ba5e088f55bd06:7">`n`</span><span data-offset-key="75fa2e43dcc148fcb6ba5e088f55bd06:8"> calls to the iterator. This has the effect of dividing the input into n-length chunks.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2e95e240195044eaa7df7ba50d29872b"><span data-offset-key="2e95e240195044eaa7df7ba50d29872b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#zip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4a65d220768541d99152427f2c953a49"><span data-offset-key="4a65d220768541d99152427f2c953a49:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">zip()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="20f151d7d7e24d0a855e3d550b4f6e12"><span data-offset-key="20f151d7d7e24d0a855e3d550b4f6e12:0"> should only be used with unequal length inputs when you don’t care about trailing, unmatched values from the longer iterables. If those values are important, use </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/itertools.html#itertools.zip_longest" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3324bd1138ce4bafb218f83791c14520"><span data-offset-key="3324bd1138ce4bafb218f83791c14520:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">itertools.zip_longest()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7ec7a6bb56074d79bd9c75ef10e2e280"><span data-offset-key="7ec7a6bb56074d79bd9c75ef10e2e280:0"> instead.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9bf8bb7f549e4f8d80e065970570b51a"><span data-offset-key="9bf8bb7f549e4f8d80e065970570b51a:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#zip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1312a796dbc840dc8ded805ba991449e"><span data-offset-key="1312a796dbc840dc8ded805ba991449e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">zip()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="222f663bcfe649f7834b7d71ffd60fdb"><span data-offset-key="222f663bcfe649f7834b7d71ffd60fdb:0"> in conjunction with the </span><span data-offset-key="222f663bcfe649f7834b7d71ffd60fdb:1">`*`</span><span data-offset-key="222f663bcfe649f7834b7d71ffd60fdb:2"> operator can be used to unzip a list:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> x = [1, 2, 3]>>> y = [4, 5, 6]>>> zipped = zip(x, y)>>> list(zipped)[(1, 4), (2, 5), (3, 6)]>>> x2, y2 = zip(*zip(x, y))>>> x == list(x2) and y == list(y2)True

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc"><span data-offset-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc:0">`__import__`</span><span data-offset-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc:2">_name_</span><span data-offset-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc:4">_globals=None_</span><span data-offset-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc:5">, </span><span data-offset-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc:6">_locals=None_</span><span data-offset-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc:7">, </span><span data-offset-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc:8">_fromlist=()_</span><span data-offset-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc:9">, </span><span data-offset-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc:10">_level=0_</span><span data-offset-key="5060260964334479a2969705cc309bcc:11">)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="552325eb64cb4999aa5ec6fbbbfaa383"><span data-offset-key="552325eb64cb4999aa5ec6fbbbfaa383:0">Note</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="39192042b28a4a718fd414e33a1ccd92"><span data-offset-key="39192042b28a4a718fd414e33a1ccd92:0">This is an advanced function that is not needed in everyday Python programming, unlike </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.import_module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bd6a40cabd61438fb2323b6d2963cb07"><span data-offset-key="bd6a40cabd61438fb2323b6d2963cb07:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">importlib.import_module()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a3d05e6bf2294c77a2364c408e429352"><span data-offset-key="a3d05e6bf2294c77a2364c408e429352:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a5e89adb970544b9b62e4f08985dabb1"><span data-offset-key="a5e89adb970544b9b62e4f08985dabb1:0">This function is invoked by the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#import" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="af7335050b8241918f455eb36df46dd5"><span data-offset-key="af7335050b8241918f455eb36df46dd5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">import</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6c330892aa9349ac8b72eb5dc4475a03"><span data-offset-key="6c330892aa9349ac8b72eb5dc4475a03:0"> statement. It can be replaced (by importing the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/builtins.html#module-builtins" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d6538c73923e407ea5dc2b3963e04183"><span data-offset-key="d6538c73923e407ea5dc2b3963e04183:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">builtins</code></span></span></a><span data-key="89d8a4cbc8f0408fbe96552103605728"><span data-offset-key="89d8a4cbc8f0408fbe96552103605728:0"> module and assigning to </span><span data-offset-key="89d8a4cbc8f0408fbe96552103605728:1">`builtins.__import__`</span><span data-offset-key="89d8a4cbc8f0408fbe96552103605728:2">) in order to change semantics of the </span><span data-offset-key="89d8a4cbc8f0408fbe96552103605728:3">`import`</span><span data-offset-key="89d8a4cbc8f0408fbe96552103605728:4"> statement, but doing so is </span><span data-offset-key="89d8a4cbc8f0408fbe96552103605728:5">**strongly**</span><span data-offset-key="89d8a4cbc8f0408fbe96552103605728:6"> discouraged as it is usually simpler to use import hooks (see </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0302" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9d33d50948f8494387403ef686844db0"><span data-offset-key="9d33d50948f8494387403ef686844db0:0"><strong>PEP 302</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="acf7c709a0e74826bba26de9b1c8141e"><span data-offset-key="acf7c709a0e74826bba26de9b1c8141e:0">) to attain the same goals and does not cause issues with code which assumes the default import implementation is in use. Direct use of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#__import__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9875d69be8bc4bf186a0873b8569c9f5"><span data-offset-key="9875d69be8bc4bf186a0873b8569c9f5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**import**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="dcec2ed465a84d9d9f6fcdb4d9f8cfed"><span data-offset-key="dcec2ed465a84d9d9f6fcdb4d9f8cfed:0"> is also discouraged in favor of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.import_module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4b9cbe5790ef4e49afe047d398662fdd"><span data-offset-key="4b9cbe5790ef4e49afe047d398662fdd:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">importlib.import_module()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c689081c663e42a69f205b6e9801dae7"><span data-offset-key="c689081c663e42a69f205b6e9801dae7:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900"><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:0">The function imports the module </span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:1">_name_</span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:2">, potentially using the given </span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:3">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:5">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:6"> to determine how to interpret the name in a package context. The </span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:7">_fromlist_</span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:8"> gives the names of objects or submodules that should be imported from the module given by </span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:9">_name_</span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:10">. The standard implementation does not use its </span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:11">_locals_</span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:12"> argument at all, and uses its </span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:13">_globals_</span><span data-offset-key="a47152aa2334476491dddd016c507900:14"> only to determine the package context of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#import" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4675487082f34bc8be05c3aa0d21e8b9"><span data-offset-key="4675487082f34bc8be05c3aa0d21e8b9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">import</code></span></span></a><span data-key="059ed43466354ae4ba77d7a69c969de9"><span data-offset-key="059ed43466354ae4ba77d7a69c969de9:0"> statement.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e6aeebc168f54f22afb7f98fff308540"><span data-offset-key="e6aeebc168f54f22afb7f98fff308540:0">_level_</span><span data-offset-key="e6aeebc168f54f22afb7f98fff308540:1"> specifies whether to use absolute or relative imports. </span><span data-offset-key="e6aeebc168f54f22afb7f98fff308540:2">`0`</span><span data-offset-key="e6aeebc168f54f22afb7f98fff308540:3"> (the default) means only perform absolute imports. Positive values for </span><span data-offset-key="e6aeebc168f54f22afb7f98fff308540:4">_level_</span><span data-offset-key="e6aeebc168f54f22afb7f98fff308540:5"> indicate the number of parent directories to search relative to the directory of the module calling </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#__import__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3db09a9614af4894a47e429fa96b21ea"><span data-offset-key="3db09a9614af4894a47e429fa96b21ea:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**import**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="eb4dd71e65d74c5aa83bd6c3110b34f6"><span data-offset-key="eb4dd71e65d74c5aa83bd6c3110b34f6:0"> (see </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0328" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="83a5c2dc9f9f455d8e362a221e800ebf"><span data-offset-key="83a5c2dc9f9f455d8e362a221e800ebf:0"><strong>PEP 328</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="aaa45c0de9004cecb2204ff2587c480c"><span data-offset-key="aaa45c0de9004cecb2204ff2587c480c:0"> for the details).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa"><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:0">When the </span><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:1">_name_</span><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:2"> variable is of the form </span><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:3">`package.module`</span><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:4">, normally, the top-level package (the name up till the first dot) is returned, </span><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:5">_not_</span><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:6"> the module named by </span><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:7">_name_</span><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:8">. However, when a non-empty </span><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:9">_fromlist_</span><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:10"> argument is given, the module named by </span><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:11">_name_</span><span data-offset-key="e48a631d38c448b09edac9eb65ed9ffa:12"> is returned.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d5ddf9f951104cf5a17a9843e662525e"><span data-offset-key="d5ddf9f951104cf5a17a9843e662525e:0">For example, the statement </span><span data-offset-key="d5ddf9f951104cf5a17a9843e662525e:1">`import spam`</span><span data-offset-key="d5ddf9f951104cf5a17a9843e662525e:2"> results in bytecode resembling the following code:</span></span></span>

    spam = __import__('spam', globals(), locals(), [], 0)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d0431cba33714c52ae54742f38c32968"><span data-offset-key="d0431cba33714c52ae54742f38c32968:0">The statement </span><span data-offset-key="d0431cba33714c52ae54742f38c32968:1">`import spam.ham`</span><span data-offset-key="d0431cba33714c52ae54742f38c32968:2"> results in this call:</span></span></span>

    spam = __import__('spam.ham', globals(), locals(), [], 0)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5eac12efe19742e5be2efaae92b2c01d"><span data-offset-key="5eac12efe19742e5be2efaae92b2c01d:0">Note how </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#__import__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2428a925b71d4ff18b696d3fa2e6062f"><span data-offset-key="2428a925b71d4ff18b696d3fa2e6062f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**import**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="86041796ffa44b7ebed616188815872b"><span data-offset-key="86041796ffa44b7ebed616188815872b:0"> returns the toplevel module here because this is the object that is bound to a name by the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#import" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8afe76cccd594b7e8a88020697aeb42d"><span data-offset-key="8afe76cccd594b7e8a88020697aeb42d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">import</code></span></span></a><span data-key="07b095ed377a47978dd8a6063de94ba5"><span data-offset-key="07b095ed377a47978dd8a6063de94ba5:0"> statement.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="251511156e564a7a8c5f0dafa0b93e5c"><span data-offset-key="251511156e564a7a8c5f0dafa0b93e5c:0">On the other hand, the statement </span><span data-offset-key="251511156e564a7a8c5f0dafa0b93e5c:1">`from spam.ham import eggs, sausage as saus`</span><span data-offset-key="251511156e564a7a8c5f0dafa0b93e5c:2"> results in</span></span></span>

    _temp = __import__('spam.ham', globals(), locals(), ['eggs', 'sausage'], 0)eggs = _temp.eggssaus = _temp.sausage
